# Wiki Log

Append-only record of all wiki operations.

---

## 2026-06-08 — Ingest: Elfen + Velrathi reverse-culture runs (to bedrock) + Dao's Pendulum principle

Ingested three new `LLMWikiRaw` files dated 2026-06-08: `elfen_consolidated.txt`, `velrathi_consolidated.txt`, and `eadras_principle_dao_pendulum.txt` — the complete Grainbound reverse-culture runs for the first two progenitor races plus a setting-level principle. (The 2026-06-06/06-07 `*_reverse_culture_session_*` files and `files.zip` are the superseded working inputs the two `_consolidated.txt` files overwrite; not separately ingested.) Four load-bearing decisions taken by user direction before writing: **(1)** the buried truths go to **`_sealed/`**; **(2)** the public part of the Demon-War-root retcon (lawful resurrection tried first and refused) is added publicly, mercy-causation sealed; **(3)** the Velrathi greying retcon is adopted (and downstream "cadaverous" mentions chased); **(4)** one continuous pass, no check-ins.

**Five new sealed pages** (`wiki/_sealed/`, one-way linking; README contents list updated). **[[elfen-hidden-hands]]** — [[qoxli|Qoxli]] + [[sylph|Sylph]] each secretly wove a piece of herself into the Elfen at creation (sourcing hunt-reverence and the joyful-novelty/ennui-cure); no one (not even Mark) knows; the reveal *blooms*. **[[velrathi-hidden-hands]]** — [[lirra|Lirra]] (method) + [[nox|Nox]] (permission) as the two hands; the acquired greying is Nox-in-the-bloodline; the reveal lands darker. **[[engineered-authored-want]]** — the engineered races' contentment is an authored disposition (the Orug unanimity as keystone image); the Velrathi cannot perceive it; **Tome-only**. **[[velena-shani-mercy]]** — the true Demon-War root: [[velena|Velena]] was willing to return, **[[shani|Shani]] refused as mercy** (sparing her from reliving her murder), [[xarvion|Xarvion]] misread it and seized the Spear; indicts the gods; held by exiles + the Tome + both Bureaucratic Archives. **[[founders-return-grief]]** — [[dao|Dao]] knows the post-departure catastrophe and deliberately keeps it from the Three as mercy (the most fragile I.A.7 instance, gated by free choice); *the day the Three come home* = a latent apocalypse-of-grief. The three eldest-race secrets share one architecture (Tome-held, invisible to makers and made; differ only in valence/custody): love-that-blooms / knowledge-worn-on-the-body / authored-want-that-indicts-the-makers.

**Elfen public** (`elfen.md` substantially rewritten). Reframed from "wardens of the wildlands" to a **love letter** Mark made in the image of who he became and **walked among for millennia**; **equilibrium-keepers** (nature *and* civilization both necessary — not anti-civilization); making physics (non-consumptive song, lopsided tech ceiling, steel-equivalent vitrified wood, the **three-hand artifact**, time-and-body cost, conservation→no irreversible ratchet); **reproduction via [[womb-trees]]** (NEW page — born adult, daily knowledge-transfer, wisdom-doesn't-transfer); **lifespan** (bell curve ~5,000 yr, 20,000 tail, singular-apex funnel, ennui-as-the-real-enemy, the scheduled decapitation of the summit); **governance** (capability-assignment, Council of the Eldest, hollow-outward "monarchy," apex kept out of rule); **diet** (metabolic vegetarianism, the one funerary ethic); **water-vulnerability** (the true existential threat: dammed rivers; materials-for-watershed treaty); **psionics/intimacy** (mind-link, mechanical consent, the kept-thing retention rule, forced-merge apex-atrocity); four **values**; the vice **"Lost in Smoke"** (anti-ascension); **belief** (Mark/Qoxli/Ascended Elfen, with a public mystery breadcrumb); **cradle/timeline** (Elfen ~40,000 BP on the eastern continent's green heartland; Velrathi neighbors in the arid SW lobe; Tarran cradle = the moon Gaia; triad interdependence is **post-colonization**). `elfen-architecture.md` gained a materials/cost/three-hand section.

**Velrathi public** (`velrathi.md` substantially rewritten). Reframed from "cadaverous masters of magic" to **empiricists** (observe→understand→reproduce; willful ignorance the only sin); the **prestige-requires-publication** brake (no forbidden *and* no secret arts; radically transparent pre-Banishment; secrecy is the post-exile Nox-rising); the **greying retcon** (made with ordinary skin; grey+red acquired over millennia via negative-energy use in pregnancy, self-accelerating, with **throwbacks**; the phenotype = the prestige economy made flesh); **foodways** (optimized slurry-bars / "dosing not dining"; the hospitality-soup keystone; the justify-don't-admit "sugar-cane tell"); **psionics/Mind Blank** (open child, dual emergence at puberty, privacy-in-trust, prosthetic privacy democratized by modern manufacturing); **lifespan** (publication as the mortality-hedge); **belief** (reverence-grounded-in-reality → worship-as-study → Bureaucracy; universal origin-blind scope; the Nox worship-vs-acknowledge split as the arc's measure); the **cultivation mode** (Stone-Bound/apprentices/formulas); the **Amunorian succession** (Tarran-line humans claim Velrathi heirship via Velrathi-blooded subjects + the surviving homeland archives; the exiles' **shame**); the vice **"Lost in the Weeds."** `velrathi-architecture.md` refined (Stone-Bound = an *elevated* pre-existing genius loci; the three-step development arc; spell-plate-as-greeting). `amunorians.md` gained the genealogical-irony/archives/shame section and resolved its open question about whether exiles take the claim seriously.

**Cross-race + principle.** `the-three.md` — forked childhoods sourcing the three temperaments; made-in-their-own-image; the **seeker-nature departure** (stepped away to explore other Mythoi; left believing their peoples mature) with a public Dao's-Pendulum cross-ref. `dao.md` — new **Dao's Pendulum** section (serene long-view; darkness as *amplitude* not breakage; the structural engine under earned hope; sits atop I.C.16; his observer-seat per I.A.2). `principles-of-eadras.md` — **principle #37 (Dao's Pendulum)**, appended after #36 to preserve all existing cross-referenced numbering (I.A.7, I.C.16, I.D.18, etc.). `peoples-of-eadras.md` — the **genetic-degradation law + divine-stability mechanism** (the hidden-hand gods perfected the eldest races' genetics; engineering a child race disrupts it → child/grandchild lines degrade, founders don't; three-tier framing) + fixed the "cadaverous" Velrathi table row. `xarvion.md` / `velena.md` — the public **lawful-route-tried-first-and-refused** step (Velena's willingness, Shani's identity, and the mercy-causation held sealed); softened Velena's "does not wish to return" toward agnosticism so the public page neither contradicts nor betrays the sealed truth. `tarans.md` — light seeker-departure cross-ref (the full Tarran reverse-culture run remains to come).

**Curator notes.** (a) The dao-pendulum file's loose "Melania with the Tarran ~10,000–11,000 years" was **not** adopted where it conflicts with established canon — `the-three`/`tarans` keep the firm **20,000–19,000 BP withdrawal** (≈19–20k years of presence); the public framing uses "many millennia"/"the long cooperative age" rather than the looser figure. (b) Elfen ~40,000 BP / Velrathi ~39,000 BP sharpen but do not contradict the established "~39,000 BP progenitor emergence." (c) Three-Gaias and Tarran-cradle-on-Gaia were **already** canon (`peoples-of-eadras`, `tarans`, `great-banishment`) — the run's geography is additive, not a retcon. (d) The two vices are kept as sections on the race pages rather than standalone pages, to control page count.

`index.md` updated (new [[womb-trees]] line + refreshed Elfen/Velrathi/Tarran description lines). `ai-index.md` regenerated. Open-questions live wires added.

## 2026-06-04 — Canon: mantle-only Sourceshine transformation + the mana toll (user direction)

User direction (same session as the unicorn ingest below, resolving its curator flag): the Sourceshine→Eldritch→Mana mechanism is now precise. **Sourceshine passes down through everything like light through clear water and transforms at one place only — the mantle** (the deep bedrock layer it cannot pass), which **reflects it upward as Eldritch**. The reflected Eldritch flows up and through the standing world the same way, **except matter absorbs small amounts of it in passing — the absorbed residue is mana**. Three accumulation laws: (1) mana **builds over time scaled by the size and complexity** of the holding matter; (2) **biological material accumulates more than inert material**; (3) mana **accumulates up the food chain** — a creature inherits the mana of what it eats, making long-lived/complex/apex organisms the most mana-dense matter in the world (the in-cycle basis of the spell-ingredient and alchemical economy). This **supersedes** the older "Sourceshine interacts with bedrock, sea, soil, or living matter → Eldritch" framing (those materials *absorb*; only the mantle *transforms*) and replaces the transforms-a-fraction gloss from earlier today.

Edits: **[[eldritch-cycle]]** (Phase 1 renamed *Source to Mantle*; new *The mana toll* subsection under Distribution; diagram redrawn; stale "Source = expression of Lirra" parenthetical removed per 2026-05-06 canon), **[[eldritch]]** (summary; *How It Forms* rewritten; new *Mana — the toll matter takes* section; three-state mana bullet), **[[magic-in-eadras]]** (Source section ¶; three-state Sourceshine paragraph; *Why Eadras is unusually mana-rich* bullets), **[[collection-fields]]** (new *Distinct from the mana toll* subsection — toll is passive/all-matter/mass-scaled, field is living-only/power-scaled; the two compound). [[mana-metals]] checked — already consistent ("near mantle activity" = densest reflection zone); no change. Protocol back-propagation: `protocols/core-canon-and-thematic-principles.md` Eldritch-formation sentence updated in place (still v2; unicorn raw-side exception also added). Stale "Source = expression of Lirra" line in [[eldritch-cycle]] cleaned per 2026-05-06 canon while in the section.

## 2026-06-04 — Ingest: Unicorn Culture-Engine session (biology, quorum, fuse-and-split, Great Silence, herd politics, collection fields)

Ingested `unicorn-culture-engine-session-2026-06-03.txt` from `LLMWikiRaw` — the complete Grainbound Race-Culture-Builder run on unicorns (Steps 1–6 + Final Test), pre-tagged `[CONFIRMED]/[PROPOSED]/[DERIVED]/[ACTION]/[PHYSICS]/[OPEN]`. User ratified the [PROPOSED] items item-by-item (2026-06-04): **all ratified as established** except the un-awakened-foal *horror framing* (bare mechanism kept — it was [CONFIRMED] in Step 1) and the Black Hand engineered-mare-starvation story hook (**dropped** entirely, per user).

**New pages (2).** **[[unicorn-biology]]** — the bodily architecture: two separate fuel lines (forage→body; raw Sourceshine→horn/mind); the horn as sole manipulator + telepathy organ + Source-intake ("crippled" = handless + voiceless-to-kind + starving, at once); horn-length = stored autonomy (battery timer for sky-poor missions); shared-field cognition; quorum floor (~8 physical / 10 observed, sacred two-body margin); awakening by first Sourceshine bath (Source-sealed foal stays a horse); breeding (near-perpetual pregnancy; **mares are the chokepoint** — two independent failure thresholds, thinking floor vs breeding floor); Source-starvation / decapitated-herd state; dragon-crafted Sourceshine-storage crystals; consequence-perfect/fact-blind prey-brain memory. **[[collection-fields]]** — the [PHYSICS] finding given its own page **pre-reconciled against [[apotheosis]]** (user direction): every creature's unconscious magic-gathering field scales with power (slow power↔wisdom feedback); the ceiling is the *capacity side* of Ascension while **designation remains the deciding act** (Principle 17 intact); field-merge of a unicorn quorum is the candidate explanation for why ~8 bodies host a mind; unstudied by any mortal tradition. Reciprocal capacity-side paragraph added to [[apotheosis]].

**[[unicorns]] substantially expanded.** Shared-field cognition (no native "I"; bodies as sense-organs); stallion/alpha-mare reframed from individuals to **consolidated functions** the sovereign herd-mind resolves between (continuously shifting, running-average not office); **the extruded I** (splinter-herd first resort, solo-I last resort; the I is *issued*, not seized; individuality as the most expensive authorized act — the lone unicorn of myth is a cost, not a hero); **fuse-and-split** (mare-poor herds fuse, split evenly carrying each other's memories → the derived *mechanism* for Herd-Deep Memory: demographic safety valve and memory-distribution network are the same act); **the Great Silence** (quorum collapse — the we dying while bodies live on — worse than death; grounds quorum sacredness, fusion-as-salvation, Source-reverence, the mythic voice); **Traditionalist vs Individualist herds** (policy difference about what may come home; the half-power tax; the self-enforcing access rule — physics, not policy; the one real heresy: the returner who refuses the Circling but won't leave); **telekinesis-courtesy misread** (the species' only physical courtesy reads as assault → grounds [[herd-listeners]] and the shy-unicorn myth as scar tissue of botched first contacts); **daily liturgy** (sun-greeting to feed; sunset Runs); **three virtues** (Vigilance/Solidarity/Acceptance, each traced to bedrock; the "phlegmatic" calm is the outward sign of Acceptance); duplicated *Telepathy and Psionics* heading fixed.

**Eldritch-blind cascade (the session's [ACTION] items + two further conflicts found in-pass).** New load-bearing rule: **unicorns alone use raw Sourceshine and cannot sense or use Eldritch at all.** (1) **[[unicorns]] Silver Runs rewritten per user ruling** — the Runs are about *memory*, not ecology: each unicorn sings a single note (the note IS the memory), each run can carry a different memory, performed only at sunset in honor of the Source; "horns channel purified Eldritch" framing deleted. (2) **[[magic-in-eadras]]** — "unicorns remain attuned to reflected Eldritch / dawn catalyst" replaced: unicorns stand outside the reflected paradigm in the *opposite* direction from dragons; dawn is feeding. (3) **[[great-exchange]] + [[dragons]] + [[unicorns]]** — the dragons' second teaching ("new and aggressive applications of Eldritch magic" — impossible for an Eldritch-blind species) **replaced by the Sourceshine-storage crystal craft** (user decision), with the harder Dragon-Path reading added (dragons taught *survival of the absence of thinking-with*, not thinking-alone) and a timing note (craft is post-Darkhoof, via the standing Exchange relationship). (4) **[[eldritch]]** — unicorn raw-only exception added + Sourceshine propagation canon (passes through everything; **only bedrock blocks it**; ambient everywhere above ground; sky-sealed places Source-poor). *Curator note: the transforms-a-fraction gloss initially used to harmonize this with the older "bedrock, sea, soil, or living matter" transformation claim was **superseded the same day** by user direction — see the 2026-06-04 mantle-only/mana-toll entry above.*

**Crystalmancy no longer strictly Arathi-only.** Dragons hold a **recreated Sourceshine-storage crystal craft** (Eldritch-capable craft, Source-charged product, made for unicorns not themselves). Updated: [[crystalmancy]] (Modern survival + Dragon Truth sections), [[elfen-architecture]] (summary + "No crystalmancy" clarification → *structural* crystalmancy remains Arathi-only), [[magic-in-eadras]] and [[dragons]] (never-built-crystal claims scoped to "for themselves"), [[index]] description line.

**Sub-page grounding edits.** [[circling-of-the-returned]] — Traditionalist (dissolution) vs Individualist (screened, half-power persistence) outcomes + the refused-Circling heresy; functions-not-persons link fix. [[unicorn-wound-keeping]] — prey-brain biological bedrock (biology and discipline agreeing). [[herd-listeners]] — telekinesis-courtesy grounding ("the one human in a generation trained not to flinch").

**Open questions added** ([[open-questions]] § Races and Peoples → Unicorns): two memory systems (stored vs sung-resonance)?; exact quorum number; un-awakening reversibility; Source-starvation reversion; fusion-rite gap (whole-herd testing of inherited Wound-Kept layers); Darkhoof's post-Spear consequences in herd memory; collection-fields extensions (other collective beings, conduit-pool interaction, deliberate cultivation).

**Method note (OOC, not canon).** The Culture Engine is adopted as a QA/derivation pass for body-dense and under-developed races — smoke detector, not judge (true positive: Silver Runs Eldritch; false positive: crystal-craft contradiction, cleared by the dragon-maker relationship). Final Test passed: not humans in horse costumes.

`index.md` updated (2 new pages + 2 refreshed description lines); `ai-index.md` regenerated (344 links, 281 pages).

## 2026-06-03 — Ingest: Conduits/Towers/Order + Bold + Halaran trading cultures

Ingested three new source documents from `LLMWikiRaw` (dated 2026-06-03): `conduits-towers-order.txt`, `bold.txt`, and `trading-cultures-halaran.txt`. (Three further re-dropped files — `snake-folk.txt`, `the-three-amendment.txt`, `draconic-servitor-races.txt` — were byte-identical re-extractions of material already ingested 2026-06-02; no action taken. `snake-folk.txt` was confirmed identical to the already-ingested `snake-folk_1.txt`.) Five load-bearing canon conflicts were surfaced and resolved by user decision (two AskUserQuestion rounds); the remainder was additive.

**Conduit system** (`conduits-towers-order.txt`). Added the **fixed-width drain-pooling mechanism**: each conduit drains through a limited-width mouth that **only [[lirra|Lirra]] can set** (and set once), so Eldritch backs up into a rich standing **conduit-pool** at each end — by choosing the widths Lirra shaped the world's magical geography. Reconciled the source's "natural / no-tending" language with the established Evye–Fryr origin + continuous Lirra-governance. Edits to [[seven-conduits]], [[eldritch-cycle]], [[lirra]]. **The Order** ([[order-sharanel]]) gained its rationale: Lirra needs no priesthood because *all spellcasting is technically worship of Lirra*; the Order is her **face in the world**, a humanoid institution (not draconic — kobolds do not tend Towers), recent relative to deep time.

**Conduit-census retcon** (user direction). **[[ratharil|Ratharil]] is now one of the 14 ends — the single end that never carried a Tower** (a primordial dragon **shrine** marks it; dragons keep an older, direct relationship with the gods; no Order presence). New `## The conduit shrine` section on [[ratharil]]. **The [[verdant-scar|Verdant Scar]] is removed from the 14 modern ends** — its Arathi-era Arath-Veyr↔[[altea|Altea]] conduit history is *kept* (deep time), but it is no longer a modern terminus (now framed as a ley-vault regulator). **Not all six destroyed Towers fell in the Crusade — at least one (the Demon-Wastes-edge ruin) fell in the [[demon-war|Demon War]].** [[amunorians|Sarathis]]'s modern conduit Far-Kin is now open canon (the Scar pairing dropped; the two coordinates remain geographic antipodes). Distribution: 3 submarine + 2 NW ([[dragon-empire|Dragon Empire]]) + 1 SW ([[varkhul|Varkhul]], antipodal to Ratharil) + bulk on [[halaran|Halaran]] = ~12 of 14; ~2 ends left open. Cascade edits: [[seven-conduits]], [[order-sharanel]], [[verdant-scar]], [[eadras-world-map]], [[oldest-continuous-settlements]], [[index]].

**Bold** (`bold.txt`). Expanded [[bold]]: the **biggest city in the world**; **30,000 years of continuous humanoid habitation** (no draconic/Arathi layers); the richest **conduit-pool** as the structural reason it never died; a **palimpsest** of architectural strata; the Tower's **survival of the Anti-Magic Crusade** (it held more spellcasters than any other Tower); the **Ismander Scar** (~500 ya — a warlord dissolved the Republic, forged a one-generation continental empire, died of an unknown disease, the Republic restored); the **polyglot naming schema**; and the **Dragon District** (humanoid-built/dragon-scaled showroom-resort, [[kobolds|kobold]] brokers, **trash-as-treasure** payment in shed scales/teeth/claws, Bold as the world's **faucet for dragon-materials**). Layered cleanly onto the existing kingdom → post-Demon-War-republic history.

**Halaran trading cultures** (`trading-cultures-halaran.txt`). Replaced the three-way **trade triangle** with the **five-culture network** ([[bold|Bold]], [[azure-basin|Azure Basin]], [[amunorians|Amunorian successor states]], [[orden|Orden]], [[free-cities|Free Cities]]) plus the **north/south caravan passes** through the Collision Range. **[[orden|Orden]] moved from the cold *north* to the cold *south*** (~30–80°S; user direction — supersedes the 2026-05-31 placement), making it the cold-south counterpart to the cold-north [[orcs|orc]] steppe; the continent now runs cold-north → warm-equator → cold-south. New page **[[free-cities]]** (tropical Holy-Roman-Empire-without-an-emperor; freedom won twice, from Amunor and from Ismander). [[amunorians]] reconciled as **both** a relocated diaspora *and* squabbling successor states on the old heartland (Ismander took half the territory). [[azure-basin]] reframed to the five-culture network + suffered-worst-under-Ismander. Updated [[halaran]], [[azure-basin]], [[orden]], [[amunorians]], [[bold]], [[index]].

**Canon-conflict decisions (user, 2026-06-03).** (1) Orden → cold south. (2) Conduit census: 14 ends, Ratharil in (never a Tower), Verdant Scar out (modern-only sever — Arathi-era kept), one fall a Demon-War loss, distribution 2 NW / 1 SW / 3 sea / bulk eastern. (3) Sarathis antipode left open. (4) Trade world → five cultures; Amunor = diaspora **and** successor states. **Flagged for later:** the ~2 unplaced conduit ends; the pre-existing **Anti-Magic Crusade date inconsistency** (order-sharanel ~9,000–10,000 ya vs amunorians / new sources ~5,000 ya) — not resolved this pass. New entries added to [[open-questions]].

New page (1): `free-cities`. `index.md` updated; `open-questions.md` refreshed; `ai-index.md` regenerated.

## 2026-06-02 — Ingest: Draconic servitor races + snake folk + Tome reframe

Ingested four new source documents from `LLMWikiRaw` (dated this afternoon, after the morning 6-1/6-2 push): `tome-of-baldaran-context.txt` (= `Tome of Baldaran edits.txt`), `draconic-servitor-races.txt`, `the-three-amendment.txt`, and `snake-folk_1.txt` (a clean rewrite that explicitly supersedes the discarded earlier `snake-folk.txt`, whose "Thosh = misread Neverborn" framing is dropped). These were user-authored integration directives; three cross-checks against existing canon were surfaced and resolved by user decision (see below).

**Tome of Baldaran reframed** (`tome-of-baldaran.md`). The Tome's origin is recast from "Baldaran's personal preference gap" to **institutional recovery after the [[arathi-cataclysm|Arathi Cataclysm]]**: the Cataclysm devastated the world despite the gods' power to stop it; the Elder Gods withdrew radically (the origin of the [[doctrine-of-unheld-hand|Doctrine of the Unheld Hand]]); unstewarded, the [[divine-bureaucracy|Bureau of Records]] degraded; the Tome was built by Baldaran + Nox + Erendor + Handwright as the *active-curator recovery* of that function. Added the four-maker-choice-is-the-meaning framing and the eternal-existence paradox (formalized in the Third Age, but always-present because positioned outside time). The Bureau-vs-Tome relationship is now **divine triage, not rivalry**. Reconciled `divine-bureaucracy.md` to match (Bureau of Records degradation section; the "vs. the Tome" section rewritten; the stale 2026-05-09 open-question resolution updated).

**Draconic servitor races — new subsystem.** Renamed `dragonfolk.md → draconic-servitor-races.md` (`git mv`; *dragonfolk* / *Lizard People* kept as aliases) and rewrote it as the canonical creation-tradition page: dragons could not perform from-scratch creation, so they **reshaped their own flesh** and **bought genesis by bargain with the ascended dragon-gods** (~30,000 BP) — the sanctioned mirror of [[ixthal|Ixthal's]] concealed theft. Four castes — [[kobolds|kobold]] (mind/mouth), [[lizardfolk|lizardfolk]] (body), [[snake-folk|snake folk]] (magic/will), and [[dragonborn|dragonborn]] (champions) — bound by an unbreakable **divine Mandate** (pooled ~100 beings per living dragon → ~100M ceiling; egg-quickening gated; over-cap eggs wait; death-tether stalls but does not kill). Distinguished from the breakable **[[ratharil|Treaty of Ratharil]]** (the ~999,999 *dragon* population cap, signed ~5 mya): "they gave their creations the cage they themselves only ever agreed to wear."

**Dragonborn reconceived** (`dragonborn.md`, full rewrite + warning banner). Formerly "the largest Lizard People" population race; now **individually-forged, soul-linked champions** — forged from one working-caste egg + dragon eggshell, carrying a lent-not-spent sliver of the dragon's own soul, outside the Mandate. The captured-soul-fragment vulnerability flags a [[nox|Nox]]-domain plot vector.

**Snake folk — new civilization.** Renamed `snakefolk.md → snake-folk.md` (`git mv`; old name + *Yuan-ti* kept as aliases) and replaced the Yuan-ti placeholder with the full civilization: the engineered **magic caste**; a faction **schismed** at the [[anti-magic-crusade|Anti-Magic Crusade]] and inverted from magical assertion to a death-cult of devotional self-unmaking; their god **Thosh is a misremembered [[nox|Nox]]** (who freed them, refuses their worship, and walked away); erasure-prayers route through the degraded Bureaucracy (administrative noise read as divine will); the **Issa** throne-title avatar; the **loaded-gun** god-eraser ascension threat; and "the leash they cannot see" (their cap still tracks dragon numbers). Added the Thosh role to `nox.md`.

**the-three.md scoped.** The "all other races descended from the progenitors" doctrine is now scoped to the **humanoid progenitor lineage only**, with the draconic servitor races named as an explicit parallel exception (descended from no progenitor; not a second from-scratch creator-lineage).

**Canon-conflict decisions (user).** (1) **Schism date:** the doc's "~5,000 BP / ~25,000 years" was built on the *old* Crusade date; re-dated to **~9,500 ya / ~20,000 years** to match the canonical [[anti-magic-crusade|Anti-Magic Crusade]] horizon (user direction 2026-05-15, live on `amunorians.md`). (2) **Page structure:** `dragonfolk` folded into `draconic-servitor-races` (alias), one canonical page. (3) **Naming:** `snakefolk.md` renamed to `snake-folk.md` (alias kept). Link sweep updated `bathing-customs.md`, `open-questions.md`, `peoples-of-eadras.md`, `index.md`, `ai-index.md`. (Note: the just-deleted `dragonkin` is unrelated — Mendelian-bred Varkhul humanoids, not these dragon-flesh-reshaped races.)

## 2026-06-02 — Ingest: Varkhul society + native elves, elf culture, whales, Grok 6-2 canon, plane rename

Ingested five new source files from `LLMWikiRaw` (6-1 / 6-2) and pushed to git.

Done via `sweep_plane_rename.py` + `sweep_plane_rename_cleanup.py` (str.replace, dry-run first, per the no-sed rule): 53 files / 436 replacements plus 11 lowercase-residual fixes (heading-anchor slugs, relative sealed links, common-noun "shadowdark spirits"). `git mv` of `feywild.md → wyldglimmer.md` and `shadowdark.md → glimmerdark.md`; old names kept as `aliases` so historical `[[feywild]]`/`[[shadowdark]]` links still resolve. ## 2026-05-31 — Map-session Part 2 (metaphysics + Sarathis) and Draconic-language rebuild

Two further ingests from `D:\Worldbuilding\LLMWikiRaw`, both applied as established canon after user decisions.

### Map-session ingest Part 2 (`eadras_map_session_ingest_part2.txt`)

Supplement + corrections to the Part-1 map work. User decision: **apply the metaphysics correction fully**, reconciling the Dimming as Weave/assembly damage (not conduit damage).

- **Eldritch energy chain + conduit model** (foundational). [[magic-in-eadras]]: Sourceshine → bedrock-transduced → Eldritch → mana; **conduits are non-physical, core-anchored *drains*** — the low points Eldritch flows toward, hence magic-rich; the recycling path beyond the core (core → Source?) is open canon; the Weave locks Eldritch for **native-born access** and empties into the conduits.
- **Towers of Lirra are NOT regulators — they are assemblies of magic-users** who gather where magic pools deepest. A conduit is **indestructible** (can't be ruptured/leaked/drained from the surface); a fallen Tower = a scattered mage-community, not a ruptured engine. Reframed across [[seven-conduits]], [[conduit-cities]], [[order-sharanel]], [[magic-in-eadras]].
- **Dimming reconciliation.** [[anti-magic-crusade]] + [[thousand-year-dimming]]: the conduits did not "break"; the **Weave's anchoring failed at three junctions** when the Windspeakers died, and the **six Tower-assemblies** were destroyed. Poetic "three conduits screamed" language preserved as in-world memory under a clarifying note.
- **Core-anchor → true-antipode mechanism.** Conduit ends are *exact* antipodes through the core and stay exact as the crust drifts (explains the Arathi-vs-modern pairing shift). [[seven-conduits]], [[eadras-world-map]].
- **The Amunorian Empire placed.** [[amunorians]]: capital **Sarathis** at conduit **(1177, 640), ~22.5°S, southern [[halaran|Halaran]]** — the **true antipode of the [[verdant-scar|Verdant Scar]]**, and a *named* one of the six Crusade-destroyed Tower sites. Climate-straddle geography (fertile mountain-fed maritime core on the wet side; arid interior dominion / caravan hinterland over the range). The fall reframed to assembly-destruction (conduit intact). Bay-crossing diaspora to the [[azure-basin|Azure Basin]] resolves the Azure "was Sarathis nearby?" hook and the empire's fall-cause. Verdant Scar and world-map antipode notes updated to name Sarathis (correcting Part 1's "heartland/forest-river" placeholder).
- **Climate.** [[eadras-world-map]]: prevailing-wind/rain-shadow rule (tropical trade winds wet-east/dry-west; temperate westerlies wet-west/dry-east); added the temperate southern conduit city (1200,781); a phantom third southern city was retracted in the source (never entered the wiki).

### Draconic-language rebuild (`draconic-language-clean.md` + `eadras_draconic_language_addendum.txt`)

User decision: **replace the page with the clean version, then merge the addendum.**

- Overwrote `draconic-language.md` with the clean rebuild (tidy consonant table replacing the bloated half-finished in-progress edit; all canon preserved, same structure).
- Merged the addendum: **fire-phonation positional rules** (V word-initial ignition; F word-final authority-spark with end-migration; V/F independent); the full **12×3 vowel-slot matrix** (V₁ aspect / V₂ register / V₃ modality, two cells flagged provisional); the **hiatus/epenthesis rule** (default epenthetic Rh, euphony override, rule ordering with F-migration last); and the **Dragon Empire's Draconic name** *Dræhrafh* / ceremonial *Dræhrarahraf* (root D-H-F, "The Gathered Fire that Rules"), added to the Example-names table and a decoded walkthrough. New **Open canon** section (slot-absorption rule, provisional cells, mortal-reduction mapping, non-Rh epenthesis). Recorded the Draconic name on [[dragon-empire]].

## 2026-05-31 — Map-session ingest: modern world map, Halaran, oceanic Weave-magic

Ingested `EADRAS WORLDBUILDING — MAP SESSION.txt` (working session: climate, tectonics, continent layout, antipodes, oceanic Weave-magic). User decisions before writing: record as **established canon**; **adopt the oceanic-magic reframe fully**; **the 14 conduit ends already include the oceanic conduits**; **new dedicated world-map page**.

**Two new pages:**
- `eadras-world-map.md` — the equirectangular dragon-memory map (2048×1024, 1°=5.689px); coordinate system with the **Prime Meridian through the [[worldbreaker-scar|Worldbreaker Scar]]**; antipode rule; planetary climate model (Earth-analog latitude bands, ~70% ocean → milder/wetter; **NH gyres clockwise, SH counterclockwise**); geocentric astronomy that reproduces tilted-sphere climate identically; tectonic assembly to the modern arrangement; marked-coordinate/antipode table.
- `halaran.md` — the large **eastern continent** where the majority of peoples live; fused from two pole-crossing fragments; **volcanic Collision Range** across the middle; regions (Northern Mountains/Ratharil, Collision Range Shada'din-and-gnome industry, arid orc steppe, forested mid-west Demonfall/Kharathen, temperate heartland, Azure Basin bay); gyre-driven coastal temperatures.

**Placements added (consistent gap-fills):** Ratharil → northern Halaran (~58°N, coord ~1332,190), antipode on the Dark Continent; Dragon Empire → **northwestern continent**, tropical-south capital, "far east" reframed as an in-world directional, shares the landmass with the Verdant Scar, thriving-young-dragons vs faded-ancient-eras + generational fault line (young→Empire, elder→Ratharil); Verdant Scar → northwestern continent (coord ~151,385), antipode = ruined Crusade Tower on Halaran at (1175,639); Demonfall Marches + Kharathen → forested mid-west Halaran; Bold → **warm west coast of Halaran**, antipode is open ocean (corrects/drops the speculative Bold↔Scar pairing; Far-Kin still open).

**Azure Basin (`[CHANGE]`):** open geography **resolved** — the Basin is Halaran's warm, enclosed far-eastern bay (an arm of the Arathalassic, ringed by the Collision Range); Venethar and the Amunorian diaspora pinned to Halaran.

**Oceanic-magic reframe (`[CHANGE]`, adopted fully):** the five Modern Oceanic Races ([[merrow|Merrow]], [[sirens|Sirens]], [[shimmercloaks|Shimmercloaks]], [[ink-lords|Ink Lords]], [[tideclad|Tideclad]]) are now a **Weave-magical power** — oceanic [[netharim|Netharim]] (a branch of the same tradition, race-flavored: growth/ecology, resonance, memory/mind, story/archive, force/current), and **three of the fourteen conduit ends are submarine conduit-cities** with oceanic [[order-sharanel|Towers of Lirra]] (grown coral + [[crystalmancy#3. Aqualith — Sea Sapphires / Tide Opals|Aqualith]]). Conduit-count reconciliation per user ruling (**14 already includes the oceanic ends**): **14 = 1 Verdant Scar + 7 surviving Towers (3 submarine + 4 surface incl. Bold) + 6 Crusade-destroyed** — and the three submarine Towers **survived the Crusade intact** precisely because the surface persecution could not reach the seafloor, which is part of why a full seven endured. Edited: `order-sharanel` (new *Oceanic Towers and chapters* section + recomputed tally), `anti-magic-crusade`, `seven-conduits`, `conduit-cities` (Drowned-Tower type + named-cities), `netharim` (oceanic branch), and all five race pages.

**Reconciliations surfaced:**
- **Dark Continent = [[varkhul|Varkhul]].** The session's unnamed "southwestern Dark Continent behind the unbreachable ward" is the established prison-continent Varkhul inside the [[continental-ward|Continental Ward]]. **Confirmed by user 2026-05-31.**
- **Tectonic-naming reconciliation (FLAG ONLY, not merged):** session fragment names *Valdaran/Elyndar/Korvath/Thalindor* vs the established *Avalon/Damedes/Culethor/Eldravath* lineage. Logged in `open-questions.md`.

**Verified:** Aqualith is already canonical (`crystalmancy.md#3`) — no new page; the session's "Aqualith is the sea-crystal lineage" checks out.

Updated `index.md` (new pages under Continents; Varkhul note) and `open-questions.md` (tectonic-naming flag, Dark-Continent=Varkhul, submarine-conduit-cities, Bold Far-Kin update). All edited pages stamped 2026-05-31.

## 2026-05-29 — Arathi worldwalking + off-world diaspora; Crystalline-Age race correction

User direction (2026-05-29), arising while compiling an OOC doomed-intervention scenario brief (`derived/scenarios/the-first-exception.txt`, not canon). Two canon corrections promoted into the wiki.

**1. The Arathi were worldwalkers; an off-world diaspora survived the Cataclysm.** The Arathi were a cosmopolitan, multiversally-connected civilization ([[planewalkers]]) who crossed between Mythoi and kept a presence in [[nexus|Nexus]]. A scattered few who were off-world when the [[worldender|Worldbreaker]] fell survived as a **world-less diaspora** across the [[omniverse|Omniverse]], possibly persisting into the modern era. They are not a lineage and left no descendants on Eadras; the **on-world extinction remains absolute**. Edits:
- `arathi.md` — new section *Worldwalkers and the off-world diaspora*; scoped the "left no descendants / every last Arathi perished" claim to *on Eadras*.
- `arathi-cataclysm.md` — scoped the partial-extinction point and the Survivors section to *on Eadras*, with the off-world caveat.
- `post-cataclysm-fauna.md` — scoped the Drowned-Continuities rebuttal to *on Eadras*.
- `planewalkers.md` — added the Arathi as the great historical exception to Eadrasi planewalking rarity, plus the surviving diaspora.

**2. Crystalline-Age race correction.** Dragons and unicorns do **not** exist in the Crystalline Age — the first dragons wake ~8 mybp, roughly two million years *after* the Cataclysm. In that era the [[arathi|Arathi]] are the only sapient race, alongside their [[arathi-servitors|engineered servitor lineages]]. Fixed two lines in `eras.md` (the Crystalline-Age flavor bullet and the muddled cross-era-constants parenthetical), resolving a standing timeline contradiction.

Brief-side only (not canon): corrected the outer-realm currency mechanic in the scenario brief — **any** magic user can mint the coin (a very-high-power spell that exhausts mortals almost instantly; coins are condensed power, hence the energy boost a spirit gets from consuming one); the goddess of magic ([[lirra|Lirra]]) has effectively unlimited headroom but restrains herself to avoid wrecking the outer-realm economy.

**Protocol drift note:** `wiki/protocols/core-canon-and-thematic-principles.md` touches timeline and Arathi material; a drift check / regeneration may be warranted but was not done in this pass.

## 2026-05-16 (sixth) — CLAUDE.md ↔ system-governance.md reconciliation

User direction: *"reconcile."* The 2026-05-16 system-governance.md ingest (entry "fifth" below) created an in-wiki rule-set that overlapped with the long-standing `CLAUDE.md` project-instructions file; both claimed to be canonical for wiki rules. This entry resolves the dual-authority problem and migrates content.

### User decisions

- **Authority**: `wiki/system-governance.md` becomes the single source of truth for wiki rules. `CLAUDE.md` becomes a thin bootstrap pointing at it.
- **Enum values**: trimmed to match actual usage across the 274-page wiki. CLAUDE.md's aspirational extras (`open-canon` / `rework-pending` / `partial-rework-pending` / `sealed` on `canon_status`; `tome-secret` / `in-character` on `perspective`; `dragon-era` / `dragon-unicorn-era` on `historical_horizon`) struck — no page actually uses them. The trimmed sets (4 / 5 / 8 / 6 respectively) are now canonical.

### Conflicts identified before reconciliation

Verified via wiki-wide grep across 274 pages:

| Field | CLAUDE.md listed | system-governance listed | Actually in use |
|---|---|---|---|
| `canon_status` | 8 | 4 | **4** |
| `perspective` | 7 | 5 | **5** |
| `historical_horizon` | 10 | 8 | **8** |
| `knowledge_access` | 6 | 6 | matches |

### Content migrated from CLAUDE.md into system-governance.md

- **Section 1 Metadata Standards**:
  - `cssclasses` moved from required → optional; `axes_profile` added to optional table with full description; `aliases` description sharpened to call out the rename-safety-net role.
  - New subsection **Schema exceptions** — `log.md`, `index.md`, `_sealed/*`, `rpg/*`, `protocols/*`, reference pages.
  - New subsection **Axes-of-Creation block** — full Meta Bind `sliderAdvanced` markup; `axes-unset` cssclass lifecycle.
  - New subsection **OOC tonal-references block** — `<details class="ooc-block">` pattern with cultural-shorthand / intended-feel / visual-motifs sub-headings.
  - New subsection **Related pages block** — collapsible block convention; last-thing-on-page rule.
- **Section 2 Naming Rules → new subsection Renames and aliases** — `aliases:` requirement on renamed pages; Python sweep tooling (`sweep_wikilinks.py`, `sweep_padded_links.py`, `verify_no_stale_slugs.py`); **no-`sed` rule** with 2026-05-10 incident reference.
- **Section 5 AI Interaction Rules**:
  - Tone subsection augmented with the *"Light and darkness cannot exist without each other"* quote, the *Wheel of Time / Stormlight* tone reference, the **never-grimdark** absolute, and the *"nihilism is acceptable only as a villain's philosophy"* rule. Canonical-style reference-page list added.
  - Generation discipline item 4 expanded with inline citation format `(source: filename.ext)`, conflicting-sources rule, and unsourced-claims-need-verification rule.
  - New subsection **Source-to-wiki ingest workflow** — the 7-step process from CLAUDE.md (read → discuss → summary page → concept pages → wikilinks → index.md → log.md).
  - New subsection **Question answering** — 5-step process; cite-and-file-back-as-canon rule.
  - New subsection **Lint and audit** — checklist for contradictions, orphans, missing pages, outdated claims, body-structure compliance, frontmatter compliance.
- **New Section 6 Backups and Exports** — two-output-per-run (full + public) discipline; when-to-generate cadence; `split_export.py` recovery; cross-file edits and the no-`sed` rule (with the 2026-05-10 incident as the load-bearing reason). Existing Sections 6 (Protocol Layer) and 7 (Plugin Integration) renumbered to 7 and 8.

### Files changed

- **`wiki/system-governance.md`** — substantial expansion. Frontmatter cleanup (cssclasses table reorganization, axes_profile added); 6 new subsections; 1 new section; renumbering of 2 existing sections; intro-paragraph updated from "seven sections" → "eight sections"; Sources line extended; Last updated bumped to 2026-05-16.
- **`CLAUDE.md`** — rewritten as a thin bootstrap. Retains: purpose statement, folder structure, external source archives, hard rules (no-modify `raw/`, log convention, no-`sed`, ask-when-uncertain), sub-skill list, help/feedback. Points all rule-set content at `wiki/system-governance.md`. Net length reduced significantly.

### Authority precedence going forward

When `CLAUDE.md` and `wiki/system-governance.md` appear to conflict, **`wiki/system-governance.md` wins**; flag the drift and update `CLAUDE.md` to match. `CLAUDE.md` exists only because Claude Code auto-loads it on session start; the canonical rules live in the wiki where they can be referenced by Dataview, by the eadras-wiki skill, by external AI sessions through `wiki/protocols/`, and by the user during browsing.

### Pattern established

The reconciliation is the **first applied case** of the dual-authority resolution pattern: any file outside the wiki claiming to govern wiki behavior should defer to an in-wiki canonical document. Future Claude-Code skills, external-AI primers, and editor tooling should follow the same precedence rule.

## 2026-05-16 (fifth) — System governance, multi-calendar architecture, infrastructure foundation

Major infrastructure session. Codified the wiki's operational rule-set, established the canonical multi-calendar system (AP and six mortal systems), built the Obsidian plugin integration layer (Templater + Dataview + Chronos), and repaired a fleet-wide frontmatter bug that had been silently degrading Dataview indexing across 96% of the wiki.

### New pages

- **[[system-governance]]** — Canonical rule-set for the wiki. Seven sections: metadata standards, naming rules, calendar rules, canon hierarchy, AI interaction rules, the protocol layer, plugin integration. Replaces ad-hoc tribal-knowledge governance with a written reference page that every editor (human or AI) follows.
- **[[calendar|Calendar Systems of Eadras]]** — Documents the two-tier multi-system calendar architecture canonized this session. AP as cosmologically-true master (Tome and Gods only); six approximate mortal systems (BP, Firethorn regnal, First Rebrightening, Dragon Empire cycles, Velrathi Banishment-count, Katharim death-ledger, Bold conduit-cycles). Includes the master conversion table and era-aware gap-tracking query as live Dataview blocks, plus a Chronos Timeline visualization across the deep-time spine.

### New canonical decisions

- **AP (Absolute Physical time) is now the master chronology.** Anchored at AP 0 = the Primordial Sacrifice. Forward-counting. Cosmologically accessible only to the Tome of Baldaran and the Elder Gods. Mortals never originate AP dates; they receive them via Tome-curation or divine revelation.
- **No mortal calendar is precise relative to AP.** All six mortal systems are documented as approximations, with drift between them treated as canonical and not as error. A Velrathi date and a Katharim date for the same event will differ; the gap reflects accumulated mortal drift from AP-truth, not record-keeping failure.
- **Every event page must record `ap_date` in frontmatter.** Use `[unknown]` when the Tome's value has not been published. The wiki preserves the cosmological truth as hidden metadata; surface display uses the culturally-appropriate mortal calendar.
- **Era-appropriate mortal calendars apply by `historical_horizon`**:
  - High-Firethorn / Demon-War / early-Dimming events → `firethorn_regnal`
  - Dimming / modern-era events → `first_rebrightening`
  - Modern Dragon Empire affairs → `dragon_empire_cycle`
  - Post-Banishment Velrathi events → `velrathi_banishment`
  - Katharim-recorded events → `katharim_ledger`
  - Bold mercantile events → `bold_conduit_cycle`
- **Mortal civilizations use multiple, mutually-disagreeing calendars by design.** This is not a flaw to be corrected. Mortals lack the cosmological reference frame from which AP is measurable; every mortal calendar is a culturally-anchored approximation.

### New infrastructure

- **Six Templater templates under `wiki/templates/`** (`template--event.md`, `template--deity.md`, `template--race.md`, `template--place.md`, `template--organization.md`, `template--new-page.md`). Each prompts for canonical frontmatter via Templater's suggester API and seeds the standard body structure. The event template handles the full calendar-field set.
- **Live Dataview queries at [[calendar]]** — a master conversion table that pulls from all event-page frontmatter, and an era-aware gap-tracking query that flags missing fields per `historical_horizon` and recommends the appropriate mortal-calendar fields for each era.
- **Chronos Timeline visualization at [[calendar]]** showing the major-event spine across AP and mortal systems.
- **Plugin integration documented in [[system-governance]] Section 7** — Templater, Dataview, Chronos Timeline, Meta Bind, Admonitions, Excalidraw, Kanban, PDF++, Importer, BRAT.

### Updated infrastructure

- **`.claude/skills/eadras-wiki/SKILL.md`** — Updated to load both [[system-governance]] and [[calendar]] on session start, encode the AP-handling discipline (never invent AP values), reference Templater templates for new-page creation, document the wiki's complete folder semantics, and reflect the multi-calendar architecture.

### Critical fix: wiki-wide frontmatter cleanup

Discovered during Dataview verification that 263 of 273 wiki pages had a leading blank line before their YAML frontmatter. This is a hard YAML parsing violation: frontmatter must be the first thing in the file with no leading whitespace. Dataview was silently treating those 263 pages as having no frontmatter at all and indexing only 10 pages out of the entire wiki.

Repaired via PowerShell script that walked every `.md` under `wiki/` and stripped leading whitespace before the opening `---`. After cleanup, Dataview re-indexed and immediately began surfacing the full ~16 event-tagged pages in the gap query (up from 4) and recognizing the full vault metadata.

Going forward, the Templater templates produce clean line-1 frontmatter automatically, so this regression cannot recur for new pages. Legacy pages are now consistent with new pages.

### Outstanding work

- Backfill `ap_date: [unknown]` on every event/history-tagged page. The gap-tracking query at [[calendar]] is the running worklist. Use Claude Code with the eadras-wiki skill for systematic backfill.
- Backfill era-appropriate mortal-calendar fields (`firethorn_regnal`, `first_rebrightening`, etc.) on event pages where the values are documented or derivable.
- Pin specific AP magnitudes for major events when the Tome's precision is to be published. Currently all AP values are `[unknown]` or `[Tome value]` placeholders.
- Backfill `historical_horizon` on pages currently missing the field. Dataview's era-aware logic in the gap-query depends on it.
- Regenerate `wiki/protocols/core-canon-and-thematic-principles.md` if any of today's canonical decisions drift the existing primer (probable — the AP system and Icon framework should be reflected).

### Session sources

User direction across the 2026-05-16 session. Built on prior canon from velveth-01/02/03/04 ingest (Velveth Apotheosis canon), imma-01/02/03/04 ingest (Imma canon), the `wiki/_sealed/README.md` sealed-folder rules, and the established 273-page wiki state at `wiki-export-2026-05-15.md`.

## 2026-05-16 (fourth) — Show-properties toggle retired wiki-wide; `hide-props` cssclass dropped

User direction: *"The `<label class="show-props-label">` code does not seem to work, so lets ditch it for obsidian's built in property folding."* Confirmed scope: full sweep across all 274 pages carrying the toggle; drop the paired `hide-props` cssclass entirely.

### What changed

Every wiki page used to carry, between the closing `---` of frontmatter and the H1:

```
<label class="show-props-label"><input type="checkbox" class="show-props-toggle"> Show properties</label>
```

The custom HTML toggle paired with `cssclasses: [hide-props]` to collapse Obsidian's in-document property panel until the reader clicked it. The toggle never worked correctly. Obsidian's native property folding (built-in disclosure-arrow on the property panel) does the same job natively, so the toggle and its paired class are both retired.

### The sweep

Python script `sweep_hide_props.py` at repo root (added today, dry-run-first per the no-sed rule in memory) applied two transformations:

1. **Toggle-line removal** — exact-string match on the single-line canonical toggle plus the following blank line; 274 files affected.
2. **`hide-props` cssclass removal** — three variants handled: `cssclasses: [hide-props]` (sole — 263 files, line removed entirely); `cssclasses: [hide-props, axes-unset]` and `[axes-unset, hide-props]` (paired — 11 files, `hide-props` stripped, line preserved with the remaining class).

Post-sweep verification: 0 pages contain the toggle line; 0 frontmatter blocks contain `hide-props`. The remaining `hide-props` mentions are in `wiki/log.md` historical prose (past log entries describing previous wiki operations) — correct to preserve as append-only history.

### CLAUDE.md updates

- **Page format example** — removed the `cssclasses: [hide-props, axes-unset]` → now `cssclasses: [axes-unset]`; removed the toggle line from the body example.
- **Frontmatter schema → `cssclasses:` row** — rewritten: no `hide-props` requirement; field is now fully optional (omit when no class applies); explicitly states that property folding is handled natively by Obsidian.
- **Body conventions → Show-properties toggle section** — renamed *Property panel*; rewritten to say the page body starts directly with the H1 (no toggle, no decoration); retirement note explains the 2026-05-16 change for future readers.
- **Plugin requirements paragraph** — removed the `hide-props` / `show-props-toggle` custom-CSS requirement; the schema no longer depends on a custom-CSS snippet for property folding.
- **Schema exceptions → `log.md` line** — removed the "no show-properties toggle" qualifier (vestigial after the sweep).

### Templates side question

User asked whether actual templates would be a better option than the CLAUDE.md de-facto pattern. Decision: keep CLAUDE.md as the de facto template. Templater plugin would only benefit the user's manual page-creation workflow; Claude writes pages by reading CLAUDE.md and using the Write tool, not by invoking Obsidian templates.

### Files

- **`sweep_hide_props.py`** (new) — repo-root sweep tooling. Documented well enough to be reusable if a similar wiki-wide cleanup is needed in the future. Joins `sweep_wikilinks.py`, `sweep_padded_links.py`, and `verify_no_stale_slugs.py` as the canonical Python str.replace-based cross-file edit tooling.
- **274 wiki pages** — toggle removed; `hide-props` removed from cssclasses.
- **`CLAUDE.md`** — five sections updated; net simplification.

## 2026-05-16 (third) — Core Canon primer regenerated to v2 against current canon

User request: *"Revise the core canon document to match current canon."* The v1 ingest (this morning) preserved the source verbatim but the source predated several major canon shifts; the drift-watch on the page itself listed the stale claims. This pass executes the regeneration.

### File updated

- **`wiki/protocols/core-canon-and-thematic-principles.md`** — full rewrite of the fenced prompt body. Title bumped to **(v2)**. Wiki shell preserved; `Sources` line records the v1 source and the 2026-05-16 revision; `Changes from v1` and `Drift-watch going forward` sections added below the fence so the v1→v2 deltas are auditable.

### Substantive changes inside the prompt

- **Magic & The Weave section rebuilt** — old framing ("Netharim biologically tied to the Weave", "Windtalkers stabilize it") replaced with the post-2026-05-09 four-order rework + 2026-05-14 defensive-Weave canon. The Weave is now described as a **purely defensive cosmological structure** that *carries Eldritch*, is *sustained by the lives of every magic user*, and is *anchored at conduit junctions by Windspeakers* (Netharim with greater innate capacity). "Windtalkers" → "Windspeakers" throughout. The **four orders** introduced explicitly: Wizards (most numerous), Priests (close second), Netharim (distant third, intuitive reality-shapers, Order Sharanel), Lexanari (almost mythic, innate-only Primordial speakers); Druids reframed as the sub-priesthood of Qoxli/Sylph/Nox. **Pillar Magic** (5×5=25) added as the shared grammar of Netharim and Lexanari.
- **Anti-Magic Crusade entry rebuilt** — pre-2026-05-15 brief entry replaced with current canon: **9,000–10,000 ya** preceding the previous Grand Conjunction; **Century of Sorrows** as Black Hand engineered ramp-up; **Cold Hearth** flat doctrine; **Icon-Habitation** as halting mechanism; **Silent Century** (priesthoods stripped of divine power for 100 years); **Knights of Lirra** as reparation; **three Windspeakers killed** → **Thousand-Year Dimming** at three conduit junctions; the broken power is named correctly as the **Amunorian Empire**, not "Sarathis".
- **Modern Powers list** — **Dragon Empire** added (2026-05-13 canon); Bold updated to **elected Conduit Republic** (not a kingdom); Orden updated to **Viking + Hanseatic Conduit Compact**; Amunorians given the Renaissance-Italy + Ancient-Egypt + Islamic-Golden-Age description and the Anti-Magic-Crusade-broken framing; Azure Basin given its non-Roman patchwork description with the six sub-zones.
- **Demon War entry** — twenty-year duration named; **Velveth** named explicitly (full mortal title **Vorandethi Kathira Spellsinger of House Valtharion**); Articles **Four** (Great Betrayal — emptying the Throne) and **Six** (Banishment) of the Divine Concordat named.
- **Modern era** — labelled **First Rebrightening** with the FR-dating-is-semi-formal qualifier.
- **Divine framing in Elder Gods section** — Icon-and-Simulacrum mediation made explicit (one Icon per god + one or more Simulacra in the spirit realms); **Avatars-impossible** principle stated as the cosmological floor; Icon-Habitation flagged as the strongest available Prime-Material divine response. The Three's universally-hands-off-on-engineered-races posture noted. Divine Bureaucracy / Infernal Bureaucracy briefly framed (terrifyingly-efficient mirror as the horror of Hell in Eadras).
- **Cosmology** — Tome of Baldaran named as the designated cosmic observer partially compensating for the missing ultimate external observer.

### Unchanged

- **Part I (36 in-world principles)** and **Part II (8 author-side principles)** — left structurally unchanged; verified line-by-line against the current state of [[principles-of-eadras]]. Principle 13 ("Divine presence requires mediation") received a clarifying inline parenthetical (*one Icon per god; Avatars impossible in Eadras*).
- **Major Themes** and **Tone Guidance** sections — unchanged.
- **Thematic Spine** — unchanged (seven words: *continuity · memory · catastrophe · identity · structure · survival · meaning*).

### Pattern

The v1→v2 regeneration is the **first applied case** of the versioning convention established this morning when the protocols subfolder was created. The drift-watch attached to v1 enumerated what was stale; the v2 regeneration resolves those items; the new drift-watch enumerates what would trigger v3. Versioning lives in the title (`(v2)`), not the filename — the canonical slug stays stable so anyone using the prompt loads the current authoritative version. Prior version content is recoverable from the raw source (`raw/eadras-core-canon & thematic principles.md`).

### Updated existing pages

- **`wiki/protocols/README.md`** — current-contents entry for the primer updated to **(v2)** with the regeneration note.
- **`index.md`** — Protocols entry updated to **(v2)** with the regeneration date and a [[dragon-empire|Dragon Empire]] cross-link to surface the most visible Modern-Powers shift.

## 2026-05-16 (second) — Core Canon & Thematic Principles primer added to `wiki/protocols/`

Same-day follow-on to the morning protocols-subfolder establishment. User dropped `raw/eadras-core-canon & thematic principles.md` (8.2KB, 10:29). Second protocol; first of a different sub-type.

### New page

- **`wiki/protocols/core-canon-and-thematic-principles.md`** — full source ingested verbatim into a fenced code block, wrapped in the standard protocol shell (frontmatter + Summary/Sources/Last-updated + Usage note + Protocol fence + Drift-watch section + Related pages). No version marker in title (source did not carry one); user can promote to `(v1)` if a `(v2)` ever lands. **Sub-type:** context-loading primer — designed to be prepended to almost every major prompt, condensed export of cosmology, Elder Gods, the Weave, timeline skeleton, modern powers, themes, tone, and the full Part I (36 items) + Part II (8 items) principles list.

### Drift-watch attached

The primer is **a derived condensed export of canon**, not the canonical source of record. The drift-watch block in the page itself enumerates the specific known stale claims: the Weave description still reflects pre-2026-05-09 magic-system canon (Netharim biologically tied to the Weave, Windtalkers stabilizing it; [[lexanari|Lexanari]] absent; [[netharim|Netharim]] reframed not represented); Anti-Magic Crusade entry predates the 2026-05-15 timeline-shift and Century-of-Sorrows basis ingest; *Sarathis* in the Crusade bullet is the pre-2026-05-12 name for the [[amunorians|Amunorian Empire]]; modern-powers list omits the [[dragon-empire|Dragon Empire]] (2026-05-13). When materially out of date, regenerate from current canon and version-promote to `(v2)`.

### Sub-type distinction documented

`wiki/protocols/README.md` now distinguishes the two protocol sub-types: **work-driving prompts** (race-deepening framework: copy-paste into a session to drive structured work) vs. **context-loading primers** (core-canon primer: prepend to other prompts to seed the LLM with Eadras canon). Both share the same fenced-prompt-body discipline (no markdown formatting inside the fence; copy-paste-clean as a single selection); the difference is in how they're used downstream.

### Updated existing pages

- **`wiki/protocols/README.md`** — added a 2026-05-16-same-day update note flagging the new sub-type distinction; current-contents list expanded with type labels and the new primer entry.
- **`index.md`** — Protocols section entry added under Wiki Meta.

## 2026-05-16 — `wiki/protocols/` subfolder established + Race Deepening Protocol (v1) ingested

User dropped `raw/Eadras Race Deepening Protocol (v1).txt` (3.3KB, 10:23) — a standardized, reusable 10-section framework for systematically expanding any race page. Decision before ingest: protocols are **out-of-universe authoring tools**, not in-universe canon; they need a structurally distinct home parallel to `wiki/rpg/` rather than living among canon pages. User explicitly requested the prompt body itself remain **clean and copy-pastable with no formatting inside the prompt** so it can be lifted in one selection into other working sessions.

### New subfolder

- **`wiki/protocols/`** — new top-level subfolder, parallel to `wiki/rpg/` and `wiki/_sealed/`. Holds reusable prompt-instruction documents (frameworks for systematically expanding, revising, or auditing parts of the setting). Frontmatter convention mirrors `wiki/rpg/`: `perspective: [ooc]`, `knowledge_access: [meta]`, `canon_status: [pending]`. Versioning convention: protocols carry `(v1)` / `(v2)` in their title so superseding revisions don't silently overwrite prior behavior.

### Pages created (2)

- **`wiki/protocols/README.md`** — subfolder overview. What lives here (copy-pastable prompt-instruction docs), what does not belong here (in-universe canon → main wiki; OOC tonal references → page `ooc-block`; RPG splat → `wiki/rpg/`; real-world inspirations → `inspirations.md`). The placement test: *is this a tool for producing wiki content, or is it wiki content?* If tool, here; if content, main wiki.
- **`wiki/protocols/race-deepening-protocol.md`** — Eadras Race Deepening Protocol (v1). Thin Obsidian-friendly wiki shell (frontmatter + Summary/Sources/Last-updated + Usage note) wrapped around a single fenced code block containing the protocol prompt **verbatim** from the raw source. The orc-specific examples (mare's-milk and yak-and-sheep cheeses; *Graybacks/Tuskers/Ash-Eaters/Dirt-Bloods/Brute-Kin* derogatory terms) are retained inside the prompt as illustrative concrete detail, not as canon claims.

### Updated existing pages (1)

- **`index.md`** — new *Protocols (separate subfolder)* sub-section added under Wiki Meta, parallel to the existing *RPG / Splatbook Material (separate subfolder)* sub-section. Two entries (README + race-deepening-protocol).

### Pattern established

The pattern for any future reusable prompt instruction document: ingest into `wiki/protocols/<slug>.md`; lead with usage context, wrap the prompt itself in a fenced code block (no inner markdown formatting, no wikilinks inside the fence) so the prompt body is selection-clean; version in the title (`(v1)` etc.); register in `index.md` under the Protocols sub-section; never link from in-universe canon pages.

## 2026-05-15 — Goldenwood ingest

Late-afternoon single-pass ingest of `raw/GOLDENWOOD ingestion document.txt` (dropped 14:15). Single-source in-world-facts document; no meta-commentary or principles companion. New atomic page created; no canon conflicts; no downstream sweeps required beyond the alien-objects entry.

### Page created (1)

- **`goldenwood.md`** — alien-origin tree species, the first documented alien-origin **living organism** in Eadras canon (all prior alien objects on `alien-objects.md` are inanimate: Worldender, Worldender Crystal, Cauldron of the Unnamed Voice). Greyish bark with faint golden sheen, green-gold trefoil leaves, dense golden heartwood, extreme cut-resistance, **biological viability persisting for years after cutting**, **propagation by planted cuttings behaving more like *continuation than reproduction***. Specialized harvest and craft techniques (rotational cutting, alternating blades, slow shaving, heat-softened scoring, long curing; leaving staves partially rooted during shaping so the wood "understands continuity"). Druidic interpretations from *tolerated immigrant* to *proof of coexistence* to *uneasy guests* to *dangerous groves at sufficient density* — four readings coexist without consensus. Scholarly theories (different entropy conditions, distributed biological continuity, different injury cognition, partial decay resistance, preserved foreign cosmological rules at microscopic scales) — none confirmed. Folk proverbs (*"Goldenwood never fully believes it has been cut."* / *"A dead oak rots. A dead Goldenwood waits."*).

### Updated existing pages (2)

- **`alien-objects.md`** — Goldenwood added to the Known Alien Objects list as the canonical example of alien-origin life (categorically distinct from the inanimate alien material previously listed). The framing that *alien-origin matter is not automatically hostile* now has Goldenwood as the load-bearing reference case.
- **`index.md`** — Goldenwood entry added in the Cosmology / Alien Objects section.

### Nature of the canon

Goldenwood is a clean greenfield ingest — no conflicts with established canon, no timeline shifts, no doctrinal reconciliation needed. The page's *Live Wires* are preserved as Open Canon items at the bottom of the new page; none required immediate decision.

## 2026-05-15 — Anti-Magic Crusade replacement (timeline shift + Century of Sorrows)

**Late-afternoon pure-replacement** of `wiki/anti-magic-crusade.md` per user direction (`raw/replacement anti-magic crusade.md` dropped 17:40). The replacement file is shorter, structurally cleaner, and introduces three substantive canon changes: a **timeline shift**, a **basis-of-Crusade shift**, and a **divine-intervention-mechanism alignment** with the Tier-1 framework established in the Velveth v2 re-ingest the same afternoon.

### Substantive changes

- **Timeline**: Crusade moved from ~5,000 ya → **~9,000–10,000 ya**, in the decades immediately preceding the previous [[grand-conjunction|Grand Conjunction]]. This aligns the Crusade with the 10,000-year cycle the user locked this morning (decision B1).
- **Basis**: Crusader doctrine reframed from *"the demons used magic, all magic is the same kind of power"* → *"the [[century-of-sorrows|Century of Sorrows]] proves all magic is wicked"*. The Black Hand engineered hundreds of major magical disasters and thousands of smaller ones across a hundred-year ramp-up; the populace's eventual anti-magic turn was, in their own terms, sound, since every grandparent could name a town the Sorrows had eaten.
- **Halt mechanism**: from "gods manifested avatars" → "gods inhabited their [[icons|Icons]] in direct confrontation". This is **consistent with the Tier-1 framework** from the Velveth v2 ingest (no Avatars in Eadras for any god). Full Icon-Habitation is the strongest possible form of direct Prime-Material divine presence the Mythos can bear.
- **Silent Century** added: 100 years stripped of divine power for participating priesthoods and martial orders.
- **[[knights-of-lirra|Knights of Lirra]]** added: each participating order donated one-third of its membership to a new order dedicated to magic-user protection. **Dual-source covenant** — power from original god *plus* Lirra; only Eadran order drawing from two sources. *"We are what they should have been. We do what they failed to do."*

### Pages created (2)

- **`century-of-sorrows.md`** — full atomic page documenting the Black Hand's hundred-year operational ramp-up. Three canonical major-incident examples (Vaelis poison cloud / 18,000 dead, Dun Lira hungry undead, Threeforks chaos pocket / reality dissolution). Self-sustaining-phase shift (Hand stopped manufacturing once the Crusade became self-sustaining). Plausible deniability framing.
- **`knights-of-lirra.md`** — full atomic page documenting the order. Dual-source covenant detail, function (bodyguards / companions / mob-deterrence / cross-pantheon liaison with Order Sharanel), doctrinal significance (institutional reminder that bureaucratic-oversight gaps have real consequences).

### Pages substantially rewritten (1)

- **`anti-magic-crusade.md`** — full replacement per user direction. Schema-compliant (show-properties toggle, full frontmatter), expanded Related Pages, retained Tier-of-Knowledge table, retained Three Cut Anchors / Bell Martyr / Burned Anchor / Silent Drowned naming, retained High Weave Age / Spire-Step / Fall-of-Spirelords political-revolution context. Fixed "Tome of Balderon" typo → "[[tome-of-baldaran|Tome of Baldaran]]".

### Downstream timeline sweep (10 existing pages updated)

The 5,000 ya → 9,000-10,000 ya shift propagated through the wiki via the following surgical updates:

- **`thousand-year-dimming.md`** — Crusade timing
- **`eadras-timeline.md`** — Crusade row moved from 5,000 ya to 10,000–9,000 ya; Silent Century, Knights-of-Lirra, and Dimming-end (~8,000 ya) added; per-row dates rebuilt
- **`grand-conjunction.md`** — cycle period **5,000 → 10,000 years** (aligning with morning B1 decision); previous-GC table row moved from ~5,000 ya to ~9,000–10,000 ya; Xar'vion's Spear-use and Lost Zenith both within the same conjunction window noted
- **`lost-zenith.md`** — previous-GC dating updated
- **`xarvion.md`** — Lost Zenith reference updated
- **`amunorians.md`** — Amunorian-fall timing updated
- **`order-sharanel.md`** — two surgical edits (Six Towers destruction timing; Black Hand engagement timing)
- **`black-hand.md`** — Phase 2 / Phase 3 historical-phase table dates rebuilt
- **`windspeakers.md`** — Crusade-targeting timing
- **`dragon-empire.md`** — softened the specific 5,000 ya anchor since dragon-empire founding date is open canon
- **`doctrine-of-unheld-hand.md`** — Anti-Magic Crusade exception section: *"manifested avatars publicly"* → *"fully inhabited their [[icons|Icons]] in direct confrontation"*; note added on Avatar-impossibility; Silent Century and Knights-of-Lirra linked. (This resolves the deferred reconciliation flagged in the morning Velveth-v2 log entry.)
- **`index.md`** — Anti-Magic Crusade entry rewritten; Century-of-Sorrows and Knights-of-Lirra entries added

### Things deliberately preserved from the old page

The old `anti-magic-crusade.md` had richer poetic detail (the "magical-orders lament", the *"Then they brought chains... Then they brought knives..."* couplet, the Sarathim divine-imperial framing). The replacement file is tighter and the **user's instruction was "pure replacement,"** so the rich detail was not preserved. The lament-tone is partially preserved on the new page via the Lirran "western stars vanished one by one" quote and the modern *"Once the Spirelords crossed the world between heartbeats"* lament.

### Items not swept

## 2026-05-15 — Velveth v2 re-ingest + Tier-1 cosmological framework

**Afternoon re-ingest** of the v2 Velveth quad (velveth-01/02/03/04 v2), superseding the v1 quad ingested in the Elder Gods Council pass earlier the same day. The v2 documents introduce **setting-wide cosmological canon** (Icon-and-Simulacrum framework, Avatar-impossibility in Eadras, Apotheosis universals) in addition to substantial Velveth-specific named canon. **User accepted Tier 1 + Tier 2 + Tier 3 in full** after the diff was surfaced; one user-supplied correction to the source's working title: the multi-article treaty is the **Divine Concordat of Joint Agreement between the Peoples and Gods of Eadras** (short form: *Divine Concordat*); the source's *Treaty of Article Four / Article Six* are individual articles of that single instrument.

### Pages created (4)

- **`apotheosis.md`** — Universal pattern of mortal-to-god transition: only living mortals can ascend; each mechanism is unique; gods reluctant to discuss; outcome is body→Icon, mind→divine, outer-plane realm appears, Simulacra appear in spirit realms. Apotheosis-as-Designation principle (Principle 17) is keyed to specific soul with specific architecture of bearing.
- **`divine-concordat.md`** — The multi-article treaty drafted by the **Coalition of Disillusioned High Command** and sealed with the Elder Gods. **Article Four** obliged the Throne to be emptied (signed 3 days before the poisoning). **Article Six** pre-accepted the Banishment. The Weave was *not* a Concordat deliverable. The canonical case of a mortal-divine bargain honoured *in full* with no later revision. Names **Meleth Vaethari-of-the-Crimson-Spire** as the treaty-architect for the first time on the page level.
- **`the-long-quiet.md`** — The named six-hour interval between the poisoning and the dawn alarm. Kathira's hair-combing reframed from flourish to **deliberate Velrathi-discipline composure ritual**. Doctrinally load-bearing for Velveth's portfolio (the triplet *Betrayal, Love, Duty* in fixed order recapitulates the temporal structure of the night).
- **`hall-of-the-long-quiet.md`** — Velveth's outer-plane divine realm: Velrathi-Gothic chamber, single low oil-flame that never burns out, carved chair, bone-handled comb on the table, House Valtharion midnight-blue stone, archive-shelf holding every bargain currently under her domain. The eternalised Long Quiet.

### Substantial rewrites (3)

- **`icons.md`** retitled to **Icons and Simulacra** — load-bearing Tier 1 rewrite. **Avatars dropped** entirely: no god of any tier (Elder, Elderborn, Ascended Mortal, Dao) can manifest an Avatar in Eadras; the Mythos is too wounded. The prior "Divine Avatar manifestation" second-manifestation-option is **retired**. **Simulacra section added** as the spirit-realm institutional working-presence framework (Solarion, Nyxar, Feywild, Shadowdark, Elemental Planes). Icon reframed as the god's permanent Prime-Material body (Stillness/Habitation states preserved). **Planar-location rule added** (Prime Material only, never Mirror/Upper/Lower/Elemental). **Visibility rule added** (most mortals don't know Icons exist; most hidden, some hidden in plain sight). **100-year unruled-domain consequence** language sharpened with Lirra's canonical-extreme case (magic would cease entirely). Total Icon Binding, Materials, Icon Warfare, Xar'vion, Ixthal sections all preserved. The old "Elder-Gods-can't-Avatar" rule is superseded by the broader "no-Avatars-period" rule.
- **`velveth.md`** — full rewrite with v2 canon. Full mortal title **Vorandethi Kathira Spellsinger of House Valtharion** (Vorandethi = heir-by-lineage title in the new Velrathi morphology). Father **Vorandar Narand of House Valtharion** named. **Northern Velrathi Titular Monarchy** (senior of two; House Valtharion ruling). Second-eldest daughter; succession passed sideways. Age 612 at Betrayal; 80-year engagement; Spellsinger ~4 centuries. Eastern Front Imperial command tent; 6 weeks after Broken Conclaves; 3 days after Article Four signed. Spellsinger work specifics (song-channelled spellwork; poison bypassed protections via calibrated vocal-arcane signature merged with Emperor's resonance over 80 years of formal engagement-rituals). Long Quiet linked. Hall of the Long Quiet linked. Office of Velrathi Affairs named. Iconography updated: **sealed treaty-vial + wine-cup + partly-veiled face + House Valtharion sigils** (canonical; tea-cup preserved as working detail). Icon appearance (3m, ashen-gray, red-eyed, long gray hair, midnight-blue robes). **Tea: Clarity Thorn**. Veyr'Keth life: survived, no remarriage, no lover. **"Still lives in blood-red crystal halls" reframed to v2-definite mortal misremembering of Apotheosis transition**. Prayer-traffic sources detailed (Velrathi exiles, Gray Matriarchy, cross-cultural impossible-choice, Katharim death-priests, modern Tarran-descended/Bold/Orden/Sarathim). Principle 17 (*Designation over acquisition*) **extended** with the Apotheosis personal-architecture dimension — Velveth as the cleanest cosmological reference case.
