## 2026-05-13 (fourth) — Mythic recitations ingest (Cataclysm + Chaos Incursions + Demon War)

Ingest of `raw/mythic-retellings-of-the-cataclysm-and-demon-war.md` (third of the four 5-11/5-12 pre-formatted Format-Guide-style ingest docs). New canon: a compendium of **recitation texts** for the three foundational catastrophes in characteristic cultural voices, plus the canonization of the **six institutional mythic voices** (dragon / unicorn / humanoid / orcish / Katharim / scholarly) as load-bearing canon for any future Eadran mythic-recitation material.

### Page created (1)

- **`wiki/mythic-recitations.md`** — central compendium page. Contains:
  - The meta-craft principle (**ancients remember through myth, not history**) — answering the puzzle of how anyone on modern Eadras can know about Kudur-eṭir 2 million years after the Cataclysm.
  - Six recitation forms of the [[arathi-cataclysm|Fall of Ssar'veth]] (core / standard bardic / dragon / unicorn / humanoid / [[tome-of-baldaran|Tome]] scholarly).
  - Four recitation forms of the [[chaos-crusades|Chaos Incursions]] (common mortal *First Wound* / dragon *Time the Sky Bled* / unicorn *Unraveling* / Order Sharanel scholarly).
  - Six recitation forms of the [[demon-war|Demon War]] (common *Demon War* / longer bardic *War of the Still King* / orcish *[[battle-of-the-broken-conclaves#Cultural Memory|Night of the Gray Wall]]* / [[katharim|Katharim]] *Breaking of the Three* / dragon contempt / unicorn ominous).
  - The institutional-voice section canonizing the six mythic voices as load-bearing for any future Eadran ancient-event recitation work.
  - A section on **how this material is meant to be used** — quotable in bardic performance scenes, priestly sermons, children's catechism, festival recitation, research scenes, cross-cultural friction encounters.
  - An OOC craft-notes block (why the texts are short, why they deliberately differ, the principle's generalization to future events, the category of *deliberate forgetting* (introduced by the beast-folk's relationship to the Demon War), mythic recitation as exposition).

### Pages updated (9)

- **[[arathi-cataclysm]]** — new section *"Mythic recitations — the Fall of Ssar'veth"* before *Religious Interpretations*. Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[chaos-crusades]]** — new section *"Mythic memory — The Wound / The Time the Sky Bled / The Unraveling"* before the *Names* section. *Names* section additionally annotated to cross-reference the popular mythic register names.
- **[[demon-war]]** — new section *"Mythic memory — The War of the Still King"* before *Long-Term Impact*. Includes the canonical Black-Hand-not-commonly-known constraint and the beast-folk forgetting note.
- **[[battle-of-the-broken-conclaves]]** — *Cultural Memory* extended with cross-reference to the orcish recitation form and the Katharim *Breaking of the Three*.
- **[[katharim]]** — new section *"The Katharim mythic voice — the keeping of true names"* before the *Lost Primer bitterness* section. Canonizes the Katharim voice as institutional precision / refusal-of-softening / *they do not forgive, and they do not forget*. Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[kudur-etir]]** — new section *"Mythic memory — the Fall of Ssar'veth"* at end of body (before Related pages). Notes that only the Tome scholarly version preserves the original Arathi name; only the unicorn version reads the event correctly as something alien intruding from outside reality.
- **[[xarvion]]** — new section *"Mythic memory — the Still King"* before *His Legacy on Magic*. Canonical constraint preserved: Black Hand not commonly known to be associated with Xar'vion.
- **[[unicorns]]** — new section *"The unicorn mythic voice — sorrowful, watchful, alarmed"* at end of body. Canonizes the unicorn register across all three catastrophes: *some wounds do not close — they only wait*.
- **[[orcs]]** — new section *"The Night of the Gray Wall — orcish mythic memory"* before *Trades and Skills*. Canonizes the orcish voice as fierce, mourning, refusal-of-forgetting.
- **[[beast-folk]]** — new section *"The forgetting of the Demon War"* before *Modern Role*. Canonizes the category of **deliberate forgetting as a mode of mythic-relationship**, of which beast-folk are the canonical Eadran example. Open canon on the precise mechanism (collective amnesia / institutional silence / Sylph Veil influence / combination).
- **[[tome-of-baldaran]]** — *Naming conventions in the Tome* section extended with a paragraph on the Tome's scholarly voice as one of the six canonical institutional mythic voices. Preserves the constraint that the Tome's open chapters know about the alien Falling Star but not the deeper Worldender Crystal mechanism, First Breach geometry, full Spear role, or post-event Spear-prison sequence.

### Index update

Added one new entry to `## History & Events` (`[[mythic-recitations]]` after `[[eras]]`), where event-level meta and timeline material is grouped.

### Canonical patterns established by this ingest

Two load-bearing patterns now exist for future work:

1. **Six institutional mythic voices** for Eadran ancient-event recitation: dragon (grim satisfaction over hubris) / unicorn (sorrowful watchful alarmed) / humanoid (didactic plain proverb-producing) / orcish (emotionally charged ritually reinforced grief-rooted) / Katharim (institutional precision the keeping of true names) / scholarly (measured admission of uncertainty). Any future event large enough to merit mythic memory should be developed in some subset of these voices.

2. **Deliberate forgetting** as a distinct mode of mythic-relationship — beyond *remembering accurately* and *remembering in mythic form*, a culture may make an active institutional choice to *not* keep certain memories alive. Beast-folk and the Demon War are the canonical example. Likely candidates for the same pattern: Velrathi exiles' relationship to the Firethorn Empire; Gray Matriarchy's relationship to the Great Betrayal. The mode of forgetting matters as much as the mode of remembering.

### Pending follow-ups (added)

- **Mythic recitations of other foundational events.** [[sorcerer-crusade|Sorcerer Crusade]], [[great-banishment|Great Banishment]], [[lost-zenith|Lost Zenith]], [[thousand-year-dimming|Thousand-Year Dimming]] — each is large enough to merit mythic-recitation forms in the established voices. None has been written.
- **Beast-folk forgetting mechanism.** Open canon — which of the four plausible mechanisms (or which combination)?
- **The Inner Hand's secret recitation of the Demon War.** The [[black-hand|Black Hand's]] Inner Hand know that the Motionless King is [[xarvion|Xar'vion]] and that their work is in his service. They presumably have their own secret cult-of-Xar'vion mythic form that inverts the public *War of the Still King*. None is written.
- **Lullaby version of the Ssar'veth myth.** Children encounter foundational myths first through *lullaby* — a sung short form that introduces the moral without the full bardic recitation. A *Ssar'veth lullaby* would be beautiful texture and is not written.
- **[[velrathi|Velrathi]] exiles' mythic relationship to Xar'vion.** Xar'vion was a Velrathi. The exiles in [[veyr-keth|Veyr'Keth]] presumably have their own painful relationship to his memory; none is written.
- **Regional variants of the humanoid recitations.** [[tariq-al-honor|Tariq al-Honor]], [[azure-basin|Azure Basin]] polities, [[orden|Orden]] member-states, [[kingdom-of-xanar|Kingdom of Xanar]], etc., each likely have slight inflections of the standard recitation worth elaborating.
- **The [[dragon-empire|Dragon Empire's]] official elaboration of the dragon voice.** Formally chanted in imperial temple, annotated by ranked priests with the hashmarks of their interpretive standing.
- **Failed myths** — the category of *what is no longer remembered*. The mythic version of the [[lost-zenith|Lost Zenith's]] hidden truths, of [[the-three|the Three Last Lights']] exact deaths, of the [[spear-of-crystallized-entropy|Spear's]] true history — many of these have failed as living recitation and survive only in scholarly form, if at all.

Previous follow-ups queued.

## 2026-05-13 (fifth) — Spear-containment ingest (alien-artifact principle + user-integrated four-prison sequence)

Ingest of `raw/spear-containment-diagnosis-and-the-alien-artifact-principle.md` (last of the four 5-11/5-12 pre-formatted Format-Guide-style ingest docs). This was the **single largest canon-supersession** in the session — substantial rewrite of the [[spear-of-crystallized-entropy|Spear]] page's prison sequence, retirement of the sealed Pacific-conclave canon, retroactive cosmological reframing of [[arathyn|Arathyn]] and the [[worldbreaker-scar|Worldbreaker Scar]], and integration of two new piece of cosmological framing (alien-artifact principle; gods'-failed-destruction-worsened-the-First-Crusade).

### Surface-diff process

Per user direction in the first triage round of this session, the Spear material was held back from automatic ingest. I read the new doc and the sealed `wiki/_sealed/fourth-hiding-place.md` and `wiki/spear-of-crystallized-entropy.md` in parallel and presented a side-by-side diff for user decision before any wiki writes.

### User-integrated resolution

The user's resolution **integrated** the new chat material with existing wiki canon rather than wholesale-adopting the chat sequence. Key user contributions:

1. **Four-prison sequence (new ordering):**
   1. **Hiding 1 (post-Kudur-eṭir)**: Gods tried to destroy the Spear (failed); covered the failure with **illusions of successful destruction**. Tarloth was the first to see through the illusion.
   2. **Hiding 2 (post-Tarloth)**: **Time-displacement** — Spear held **1 minute in the future** within Brightmirror. The plane's time-displaced exposure to the Spear over centuries corrupted Brightmirror into the **[[feywild|Feywild]]** we know today.
   3. **Hiding 3 (post-Darkhoof)**: **Reverse time bubble** (time runs *faster* inside — vs. *slower* for an ordinary time bubble, and vs. *1 minute future-displaced* for time displacement) over a [[dragons|volunteer Ascended Mortal Dragon God's]] Total Icon Binding prison, in the deepest depths of the **[[shadowdark|Shadowdark]]**. The volunteer subjectively endured **10^37 years** of unbroken solitude — vastly older, more powerful, more isolated, almost certainly suffering from **divine schizophrenia** by the end. The Spear's centuries-long presence corrupted Darkmirror into the Shadowdark we know today.
   4. **Hiding 4 (post-Xar'vion)**: **Shove it back down the hole** — gods rammed the Spear back into Kudur-eṭir's original First Breach Wound. Triggered global volcanism that forced [[arathyn|Arathyn]] into its modern shape. Arathyn is **scar tissue grown over the impalement**.

2. **Godkilling shifts to Xar'vion.** In the new doc's original sequence, Darkhoof killed the volunteer dragon god (placed in Prison 2). In the user-integrated sequence, the volunteer is in Prison 3, so **Xar'vion** kills the god — adding another atrocity to his arc.

3. **Plane-corruption canon preserved but reordered.** The existing canon's Spear-corrupts-plane mechanism is retained; the order is flipped: Feywild now post-Tarloth (was post-Tarloth in old canon too, oddly), Shadowdark now post-Darkhoof (was post-Kudur-eṭir in old canon). Both transformations took millions of years.

4. **Volunteer god is an Ascended Mortal Dragon God** (matches new doc); identity is open canon.

5. **Arathyn-as-scar-tissue adopted.** The continent's modern shape is directly caused by the post-Demon-War impalement. The pre-existing LIP geology is preserved (continent had been forming since the Cataclysm; surfaced ~1 mya); the impalement reactivated and accelerated the geological process into the modern continental form.

6. **Pacific Self-Crowned canon retired.** The sealed `fourth-hiding-place.md` was rejected as *"modern fantasy plotting copied from the Firestaff Chronicles, full of gameable plot devices rather than mythic resonance."* The file is preserved with a deprecation banner for historical reference; the new sealed canon is at `wiki/_sealed/fourth-attempt-impalement.md`.

### User clarification mid-session — the time mechanics

The user provided canonical time-mechanic definitions partway through writing:

- **Time displacement** = held 1 minute in the future. Any attempt to grasp it always reaches the empty space where it *had been* one minute ago.
- **Time bubble** = time moves slower inside.
- **Reverse time bubble** = time moves faster inside. For the volunteer dragon god: 10^37 subjective years for 10,000 objective years.

These definitions are now load-bearing canon for any future time-magic on Eadras and were integrated into the Spear page, the sealed file, the Feywild page, and the Shadowdark page mid-session.

### Pages updated (8)

- **[[spear-of-crystallized-entropy]]** — full Prisons section rewrite. New section *"The alien-artifact principle"* establishing the cosmological framing. Wielder paragraphs (Tarloth, Darkhoof, Xar'vion) updated for the new sequence. New section *"The four hidings"* with detailed treatment of each hiding (Hiding 1 destruction-illusions, Hiding 2 Feywild time-displacement, Hiding 3 Shadowdark reverse-time-bubble god-prison, Hiding 4 Wound impalement). New subsection *"The volunteer dragon god"* with the 10^37-year subjective-time elaboration and divine-schizophrenia working frame. New subsection *"Where the Spear is now, and who knows"* and *"Reaching the Spear"* with the *the obstacles are consequences of divine desperation, not clever defenses* framing. Significance section rewritten. New *Open canon* section.
- **[[arathyn]]** — Summary rewritten to identify Arathyn as scar tissue grown over the gods' fourth-attempt containment. Formation section extended with the post-Demon-War impalement phase and the cause/mechanism distinction. Implications list extended with the progressive-reality-fray rings around the conceptual center. Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[worldbreaker-scar]]** — Summary rewritten to identify the Scar as the active site of the Spear's impalement. New bullet in the Magical-and-metaphysical-significance section on the Spear's impalement. New subsection *"Reaching the Scar"* with the reality-fray rings. Practical implications updated. Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[feywild]]** — *History: Twisted by the Spear* section rewritten. The Spear is now post-Tarloth and held via time-displacement; the Feywild's temporal anomalies are downstream of that. Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[shadowdark]]** — *History: Twisted by the Spear* section rewritten. The Spear is now post-Darkhoof in the third hiding's god-prison; the Shadowdark's dark plane-character is downstream of the centuries the prison sat there. Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[kudur-etir]]** — *Final Death* section extended with a new subsection on what the gods did with the Spear after his death (the failed destruction attempts, the worsened First Crusade, the illusion cover-up). Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[chaos-crusades]]** — new section *"The First Chaos Crusade's amplification"* before the First Crusade detail section, attributing the Crusade's specific severity to the gods' deflected first-attempt attack on the Spear.
- **[[xarvion]]** — new section *"The Spear, the volunteer god, and the broken seal"* before the Mythic memory section, recording Xar'vion's killing of the volunteer dragon god and the open canon on what he absorbed in the act. Sources + Last updated refreshed.
- **[[dragons]]** — new subsection *"The volunteer of the Spear's third hiding"* under *Dragon Gods*, formalizing the dragon-god martyrdom canon and the dragons' grief beneath the public grim-satisfaction-over-Xar'vion register. Sources + Last updated refreshed.

### Pages created (2 sealed, 0 public)

- **`wiki/_sealed/fourth-attempt-impalement.md`** — new active sealed canon. Detailed treatment of the alien-artifact principle, the fourth-attempt impalement (why it worked when nothing else had; Arathyn as visible cost), the volunteer dragon god (identity, 10^37-year subjective endurance, divine schizophrenia), Xar'vion's killing (and the open canon on what he absorbed), the four plot vectors (Black Hand learns the principle / PCs approach Arathyn / the Wound stresses / a fragment of the volunteer's selves reaches the world), and the public-vs-sealed reconciliation.

File preserved for historical reference and for any campaign material developed against the old version. **The active sealed canon is the new `fourth-attempt-impalement.md`.**

### Sealed README updated

The `wiki/_sealed/README.md` *Current contents* section now lists `fourth-attempt-impalement.md` as **ACTIVE** and `fourth-hiding-place.md` as **DEPRECATED 2026-05-13** with the deprecation reason.

`spear-of-crystallized-entropy` entry rewritten in `## Artifacts & Objects` to capture the new four-hiding sequence in a single-line summary plus the alien-artifact-principle hook.

### Public canon vs. sealed canon — what the public page does and does not record

What the public Spear page now records (load-bearing):
- The alien-artifact principle (high-level): the Spear is alien to the Mythos.
- The four-hiding sequence (destruction-illusions / Feywild time-displacement / Shadowdark god-prison / Arathyn impalement).
- The volunteer dragon god's existence and Xar'vion's killing of them; identity open canon.
- Arathyn as scar tissue over the impalement.
- The reaching-the-Spear principle (obstacles are consequences of divine desperation, not clever defenses).

What the sealed `fourth-attempt-impalement.md` preserves but the public page does not:
- The full *cannot* (vs *have not*) destruction framing (the gods *cannot* destroy the Spear — load-bearing for the Black Hand's long-term strategy if they ever learn it).
- The 10^37 subjective-year duration and the full divine-schizophrenia elaboration of the volunteer's late-stage state.
- What Xar'vion may have absorbed in the killing (power / knowledge / fragments of the volunteer's fractured personas now inside his Icon / the Spear's attunement).
- The exact in-world coordinates of the impalement site within Arathyn.
- The four plot vectors for campaign use.
- Open author-questions on the volunteer's identity, the Black Hand's potential principle-aware extraction pathway, and the Grand Conjunction's effect on impalement stability.

### Pending follow-ups (added)

- **Tower of Stars** — drops out of the prison sequence entirely. Whether the Velrathi arch-wizard's stronghold survives in any non-prison role is open canon. No wiki page currently exists for it; if one is wanted, a stub flagged accordingly is straightforward.
- **The Pacific Self-Crowned material** — is it preserved in any form (a Black Hand decoy site, an unrelated sealed Rathari conclave, the Self-Crowned as a different villain in a different context), or is the entire structure retired? Decision deferred.
- **The volunteer dragon god's name, clan, and age.** Working candidates exist in `wiki/_sealed/fourth-attempt-impalement.md`; locking should happen when this becomes campaign-relevant.
- **Xar'vion's absorption** — what specifically did he take from the volunteer's killing? Power, knowledge, persona fragments? This is one of the richest unsettled threads from the new canon.
- **The Black Hand's knowledge of the alien-artifact principle.** As of canonical present, they probably do not know. If they did — or if Xar'vion knows from within his Icon and is feeding it to the Inner Hand — the entire Spear-recovery strategy shifts from *locate* to *principle-aware extraction*. Decision deferred.
- **The next Grand Conjunction's effect on impalement stability.** Open. The fourth hiding has held for 10,000 years, but the alien-artifact principle implies eventual emergence. Whether the next Grand Conjunction is a stress event for the impalement is one of the most campaign-active open questions.
- **The reality-fray ring structure of Arathyn.** Open canon. How wide are the rings? Where are habitability cutoffs? What does the deep-interior look like? A focused session on Arathyn's surface geography would benefit.
- **The Tarloth-saw-through-the-illusion mechanism.** Draconic Fire-perception? Specific Cindirith-related insight? Open.
- **The Darkhoof-seized-a-time-displaced-Spear mechanism.** Unicorn temporal sensitivity is the leading hypothesis but is not locked.

### Format Guide observation (final note for the four-doc batch)

This ingest closed out the four pre-formatted Format-Guide-style docs that arrived in `raw/` today. The pattern over the four ingests confirmed the [[project-pre-structured-triple-ingest|locked policy]]: pre-formatted docs with explicit `[CANONIZED]` / `[FLAG_FOR_REVIEW]` / `[META]` / `[IN-WORLD]` / `[CHAT_SUPERSEDES_WIKI]` flags are dramatically easier to ingest than chat logs, **but** when a doc uses `[CHAT_SUPERSEDES_WIKI]` (as the Spear doc did), the *diff-then-decide* loop becomes load-bearing — the user owns canon-supersession decisions, not the curator agent. The session worked because:

- The first triage round caught the supersession upfront and held back the Spear ingest pending decision.
- The diff was presented in chat (not as a derived file the user has to read separately).
- The user's resolution was *integrative* rather than wholesale-accept-or-reject — preserving load-bearing existing canon (Feywild and Shadowdark plane corruption) while adopting the new cosmology.
- Mid-ingest clarifications (the time-mechanic definitions) were absorbed and back-filled into the pages already written.

This pattern is worth preserving for future canon-supersession ingests. The user-integrated resolution mode is structurally different from either accept-wholesale or reject-wholesale, and the diff-then-decide loop is what makes it reliable.

Previous follow-ups queued.

## 2026-05-13 — Three-triple ingest: ForbiddenKindlingAndUnheldHand + DragonsAndUnicorns + VerdantScarAndArathCataclysm

Third triple-format ingest. Re-ingests Council Elements I–VIII of the original OpenAI Playground worldbuilding session via three topic triples (9 files, 3 docs each: InWorld_Facts / MetaCommentary / Principles_and_Diagnosis). Cleanup pass on already-canonized material per [[project-pre-structured-triple-ingest|the locked policy]] — the triples themselves flag retcons inline with `[SUPERSEDED_BY_WIKI]` / `[CANONIZED_AS X]` / `[WIKI_EXPANDS]` tags and most Doc 01 content is already present in wiki canon.

### User decisions taken before writing

The diff against existing canon surfaced one borderline (B1) and four placement questions (B2–B5), plus eight design-principle candidates. All decisions taken before any write hit the wiki.

- **B1: Divine seals on Sealed Hall, Shard of First Shell, and unicorn origin-memory.** User: *Ixthal seals are divine.* Reading: [[ixthal|Ixthal]] is himself a god; seals he places are genuinely divine work, not a *masquerade*. What is hidden is *which* god placed them. The dragons' tradition of "by order of the gods" is literally true; only the imprecise pluralization conceals that one god acted alone. Codified at [[ixthal#The seals Ixthal placed|Ixthal — The seals Ixthal placed]], [[ratharil#Why divine seals exist on dragon-side artifacts|Ratharil]], and [[unicorns#Ancestral Memory and the Forbidden Truth|Unicorns]].
- **B2: The Bathyric Mandate.** User: *open-questions.md only.* Note added to [[open-questions#Places and Settlements]]; not promoted to a wiki page. Status unchanged from the original 2026 deferral.
- **B3: Post-Cataclysm marine fauna.** User: *one consolidated [[post-cataclysm-fauna]] page.* New page created, covering **Abyssal Crownwhales**, **Vent Seraphs**, **Scaldwyrms**, **Crown-Eels**, **Lantern Dead**, and **Pressure Echoes**. [[arathalassic-sea#Inhabitants|Arathalassic Sea]] updated to redirect to the consolidated page rather than duplicate. The page also explicitly catalogs *what is conspicuously absent* (Arathi ghosts, surviving Altean wildlife, Drowned Continuities, Bathyric Mandate as confirmed canon).
- **B4: Cataclysm-born geographic features.** User: *open questions.* Features (Boiling Rifts, Crown Trenches, Steamfall Cliffs, Shattered Shelves, New Mountains) are already canonized at [[arathi-cataclysm#Geological Features Created]] as a flavor list; whether they get individual treatment or remain flavor is now noted at [[open-questions#Places and Settlements]].
- **B5: Religious interpretations of the Cataclysm.** User: *yes — add to arathi-cataclysm.md.* Existing section expanded with **Raja** (praise those who rebuilt) and **Sylph** (forbidden jokes about Arathi *"perfectly permanent"* seaside villas), in addition to the existing Ioa / Lirra / Qoxli / Nara / Nox entries.

### Additive flavor adopted (user-selected)

- **Sealed Hall oath** — *"By scale, by Source, by the nine first shells, I shall not call the Kindler by plea or command…"* — sworn by every dragon admitted to the deepest level of Sealed Hall access. Added to [[ratharil#The Sealed Hall oath]]; cross-referenced from [[doctrine-of-unheld-hand#The Sealed Hall oath]].
- **Per-clan secret draconic theology** — how each of the nine color clans would interpret the Forbidden Kindling truth if revealed (Gold = disciplined responsibility; Blue = preserve legal memory; Red = no inherited guilt; Purple = divine contraband; White = survival needs no permission; Silver = cosmic disquiet; Copper = born from devastation; Green = private interpretations; Black = what advantage does this provide?). Added to [[doctrine-of-unheld-hand#Per-clan draconic responses (esoteric, hypothetical)]].
- **Dragon scripture of the first hatching** — the verbatim hymn (*"After the long hunger of the world… nine eggs burned and did not break; nine shells sang and did not melt…"*) — added to [[nine-embers-of-renewal#Dragon scripture of the first hatching]], with the elder-draconic *Ithren*-as-Ixthal layered onto the elder/public-myth distinction.
- **Hospitality-by-color and clan-hall scent profiles** — Red mineral heat, Blue ozone, Green sap, Purple variable, Black peat-tannin, White snow + blood-warm food, Copper ash and metal, Silver salt and cold depth, Gold incense and scale-oil — plus the matching distinct hospitality protocol for each. Added to [[ratharil#The Nine Clan Halls]].
- **Two Kinds of Law** — explicit Omniversal-vs-Divine distinction added as a top-level section on [[doctrine-of-unheld-hand#Two kinds of law]]. Cross-link to [[omniversal-laws]]. The distinction was always implicit in canon; it is now explicit.

### Doc 03 → design principles (8 new, total now 23)

The Doc 03 *Principles and Diagnosis* files contained setting-wide design principles that passed the [[inspirations#Setting-wide design principles|two-domain test]] (the principle surfaces in two or more unrelated topic domains, making it a setting law rather than a one-off pattern). Eight new principles user-approved and added to [[inspirations#The principles]]:

- **#16 Catastrophes are bigger than their catalysts** (Kudur-eṭir/Worldbreaker; Xar'vion/Demon War; Tarloth/Shadowdark — disasters disproportionate to intent)
- **#17 Institutions are corrections to instinct** (Ratharil vs dragon-pride cycle; Chorus vs herd-reflex; Doctrine vs divine impulse)
- **#18 Justice is not comfort, balance is not mercy** (Omniversal Law of Justice grinds slow and impersonal; cosmic correction is not rescue; pairs with the anti-grimdark frame)
- **#19 Cultural exchange is the engine of magical development** (Great Exchange psionics; Weave divine transmission; Crystalmancy from Arathi material legacy; necromancy as archaeology)
- **#20 Design is hidden inside biology** (Ixthal-engineered age-deference; unicorn born-collective; species defaults as designer fingerprints)
- **#21 Theological positions produce political factions** (five Forbidden-Kindling movements as political alignments)
- **#22 Desire is dangerous geometry** (Spear strips motive; Want-Wolves hunt fixation; Root-Crucible motivational absence; Neverborn given contour by obsession; discipline of desire as load-bearing magical principle)
- **#23 The living world remembers what institutions forget** (Verdant Scar as ecology-of-memory; Marble Mourners; Glassharts; unicorn herd-field memory; Sealed Hall as partial institutional version)

[[inspirations#The principles|Inspirations]] header copy updated to reflect the new count (was "ten principles" → now "twenty-three principles"); the original ten + 2026-05-12 five + 2026-05-13 eight breakdown is documented in the surrounding prose.

## 2026-05-12 — Sarathim → Amunorian Empire wiki-wide rename

User direction late 2026-05-12: rename the Sarathim civilization (page and references throughout the wiki) to the Amunorian Empire. User-decided canonical forms:

- **Page slug:** `sarathim.md` → `amunorians.md` (matches the existing people-name slug pattern: `tarans.md`, `velrathi.md`, `rathari.md`)
- **People name:** Sarathim → **Amunorian** (used adjectivally: *"an Amunorian merchant"*) / **Amunorians** (plural collective: *"the Amunorians were"*)
- **Empire name:** Sarathim Empire → **Amunorian Empire**
- **Capital city:** *Sarathis* unchanged (user-decided — produces a slight historical tension where the capital's name predates the empire's rename, which is workable and historically common)
- **Tag / lineage modifier:** `sarathim` → `amunorian` (matches the existing race/lineage tag pattern: `tarran`, `velrathi`, `elfen`, etc.)
- **Aliases on the renamed page:** `[Sarathim, sarathim, "The Sarathim", "the Sarathim"]` — preserves Obsidian wikilink resolution for any historical `[[sarathim]]` references in `log.md` and other places the sweep deliberately skipped.

### Sweep tooling

Created `sweep_sarathim_to_amunorian.py` at the repo root, modeled on the existing `sweep_wikilinks.py` (pure `str.replace`, no regex; specific-phrase rules before the general fallthrough rule). Skips `log.md` by default to preserve historical entries; the aliases convention handles wikilink resolution for `[[sarathim]]` references in those historical entries.

Sweep statistics: **142 replacements across 13 files** (log.md skipped). Verification with `verify_no_stale_slugs.py`: **0 stale wikilinks** post-sweep.

### Manual cleanups after sweep

The general fallthrough rule `Sarathim X → Amunorian X` produced some grammatical artifacts the sweep couldn't disambiguate by string-replace alone. Cleaned up manually:

- **Article fixes**: `a Amunorian X` → `an Amunorian X` (Amunorian starts with a vowel sound, so the indefinite article changes). Affected `wiki/sarathim.md` (5 instances: building, city, ruler, house, OOC-block building) and `wiki/modernity.md` (1 instance: archive).
- **Plural-collective fixes**: `The Amunorian VERB → The Amunorians VERB` in cases the sweep's specific-phrase rules didn't enumerate. Affected `wiki/sarathim.md`: 11 instances (emerged, "from other", "a particular character", distinguished, preserved, viewed, lacked, treated, "added their own", "Tens of thousands of Amunorian died", "no longer had", consider).
- **Section heading**: `## Place within the Sarathim` → `## Place within the Amunorians` in `wiki/house-sitharis.md` and `## Modern Sarathim` → `## Modern Amunorians` in the renamed page (sweep didn't catch these — heading without surrounding-word context).

### Intentionally-not-touched residual `Sarathim` references

- **`wiki/amunorians.md` frontmatter `aliases:` field** — preserved as required by the renames-and-aliases convention.
- **`wiki/amunorians.md` Sources line: `sarathim-revision-2026-05-11.txt`** — this is a raw/ filename; never-modify-raw applies.
- **`wiki/open-questions.md` and `wiki/worldbuilding-needs.md` Sources lines**: historical references to the "2026-05-08 Sarathim/architectures/eras ingest" — these describe a historical event under its then-canonical name, comparable to how log.md entries are preserved.
- **`wiki/log.md` historical entries** — skipped by the sweep by default. Aliases on `amunorians.md` resolve any `[[sarathim]]` wikilinks in those entries.

### Page-level changes

- `wiki/sarathim.md` → `wiki/amunorians.md` — file renamed via `mv`. Frontmatter: title → "The Amunorian Empire"; aliases added. H1 → "The Amunorian Empire". 70 internal replacements (largest single-file count in the sweep) plus the manual grammar cleanups.
- All cross-references swept: `azure-basin.md`, `bold.md`, `clan-nightshade.md`, `eras.md`, `house-sitharis.md`, `index.md`, `inspirations.md`, `modernity.md`, `open-questions.md`, `orden.md`, `tariq-al-honor.md`, `worldbuilding-needs.md`.

### Bookkeeping note on the just-prior log entry

The same-day entry directly below this one (2026-05-12 seven-topic re-ingest) was written when the canonical name was still Sarathim. The entry describes work that integrated `BlendedKingdom_*` material into what was then `sarathim.md`. That entry's prose was deliberately not retroactively updated to "Amunorian Empire" — it accurately describes what was true at the moment of writing, and Obsidian aliases will resolve any wikilinks correctly. The rename happened later in the same day and is recorded here as a separate event.

## 2026-05-12 — Seven-topic Extra-Large-Grok-Chat re-ingest via expert-council triples

Second triple-format ingest of the day. Re-ingests `raw/Extra large grok chat 5-9-2026.txt` (the 380KB source for the original 2026-05-09 ingest) through the user's analysis pipeline as **seven topic triples**: Arathi, BlendedKingdom, Cosmology, DescendantCultures, FourOrders, HighArathiCampaign, OriginalHumanoids. **20 files** total (FourOrders is missing Doc 02 MetaCommentary — proceeded without it; can fold in later if it lands).

### Cleanup-pass framing

Per the policy locked in earlier 2026-05-12 (see [[inspirations]] design-principle catalog and project memory), this is a **cleanup pass on existing canon**, not a fresh ingest into empty space. The triple-format ingest is structurally cleaner than the chat-log ingest by design, so re-ingesting an already-ingested topic refines and corrects the existing canon. Per user direction: **canon-level differences surface for user decision; format/wording/structure cleanup is silent**. All differences surfaced; all decisions taken before any write hit the wiki.

### User decisions taken before writing

The diff against existing canon surfaced one borderline and seven load-bearing canon differences. User decisions:

- **Borderline: "interdivores"** (FourOrders §13 term for demon energy-consumers). User: *demons are energivores* — wiki canon stands ([[demons|demons]] = Alien-Mythos energivores). Triple typo silently corrected.
- **B1: Buried Chaos War as in-world canon vs splat.** User: *splat is correct, not meant to be referenced in wiki, only a possible future*. Closed-time-bubble stays in `wiki/rpg/` as non-canonical; Arathi §12-13's in-world promotion **rejected**. The Tome's sealing-capacity framework is preserved on [[tome-of-baldaran]] as canonical infrastructure; the campaign-as-splat status holds.
- **B2: Closed-time-bubble mechanism** — actualized-but-excised vs unactualized-branch. User: *the event was a branch that didn't happen, with the Tome recording it as a potential-future-that-wasn't*. May 9 canon stands; Cosmology §8's actualized-but-excised framing **rejected**.
- **B3: Language hierarchy tiers** — 4-tier vs 5-tier. User: *5 tier*. [[true-language]] updated to add **Mortal Language** (tier 4) as the explicit lowest tier at which ordinary mortal speech still anchors reality through naming, even though it cannot create. Pairs with the principle that ordinary mortals are not metaphysically inert.
- **B4: Era name** — Crystalline Age vs High Arathi Era. User: *Crystalline (names interchangeable)*. [[eras]] adds the High-Arathi-as-interchangeable-name note; Crystalline Age remains the primary canonical name; "High Arathi Era" is acceptable as alias.
- **B5: Neverborn — "no motive" vs "manic obsessive observation"**. User: *middle*. [[neverborn]] updated with a "Pre-rational drive, not structured-mind motive" section preserving the 2026-05-01 *no-structured-mind-motive* canon while explicitly incorporating the *compulsive observational drive* coloring as the shape of what the Neverborn *is*. Fascination is the shape, not a feeling-about-something.
- **B6: Princess-who-poisoned-emperor immunity question.** User: *velrathi*. Princess remains Velrathi per existing [[great-betrayal]] canon; OriginalHumanoids §6's lack-of-immunity reference dropped. Rare-Tarran-no-immunity remains canon as a Tarran sub-population trait (just not the princess).
- **B7: Tome scope.** User: *actualized + unactualized + curatorial judgment (most unactualized events are never revealed, thus making them irrelevant)*. [[tome-of-baldaran]] retains full scope (actualized + unactualized inflection-point potentials + curatorial-judgment sealings); new clarifying paragraph notes that **most unactualized potentials are never revealed** and stay sealed permanently — the canonical history is the unsealed surface; the sealed layer is the much larger archive.
- **D: BlendedKingdom topic.** User: *D-ii — this IS the Sarathim, re-described with a desert-empire emphasis you want adopted into sarathim.md*. Major [[sarathim]] restructure: Sarathim Empire framed as **desert empire** at the heartland with Sarathis as a desert capital (resolves Sarathis-location open canon); post-Crusade Mediterranean diaspora canon preserved; new **Imperial architecture** section adds the two-tier hierarchy (imperial vs ordinary), domes/minarets imperial-only, crystal-warded minarets (structurally parallel to [[taran-architecture|Tarran spell-crystal minarets]]), pharaonic guardian statues with hybrid Ottoman-Renaissance-Egyptian crown, hieroglyph-rune hybrid script as both decoration and active magical infrastructure, oasis gardens as imperial-control-of-water propaganda; OOC craft-notes block expanded.
- **C: Pure additions** — user batch-approved. Five content additions adopted: conduits-stayed-put-while-crust-slid clarification ([[arathi]]), proverb *"Proud as Arath before steam"* ([[arathi]]), cultural-anxiety/inherited-trauma framing across post-Arathi civilizations ([[arathi]]), specific Elfen blossom-wine clan vintages ([[elfen-blossom-wines]]), category-organized Velrathi tea variety names ([[velrathi-tea-culture]]).

### Wiki changes

**Cosmology cluster**
- [[true-language]] — 5-tier language hierarchy adopted (added Mortal Language as tier 4); naming-and-anchoring participation for ordinary mortal speech.
- [[neverborn]] — middle-ground framing added: pre-rational observational drive, not structured-mind motive. Preserves prior canon while incorporating the compulsive-fascination coloring.
- [[tome-of-baldaran]] — scope clarification: most unactualized potentials never revealed; canonical history is the unsealed surface over a much larger sealed depth.

**Arathi cluster**
- [[arathi]] — added the proverb *"Proud as Arath before steam"* alongside the existing tyrant proverb; added new section **The conduit-city dislocation** (crust slid relative to pinned conduits — Arathi cities ended up on dead ground, real conduits surface elsewhere); added new section **Inherited trauma** (no Arathi diary, no last words, trauma passes to second-generation survivors carrying someone else's pain; unconscious cultural drive to climb toward Arathi-tier power while trying to prove the climber is not Arathi); OOC craft-notes block added.
- [[arathi]] cross-link added to [[modernity]].

**Sarathim cluster (BlendedKingdom integration)**
- [[sarathim]] — major D-ii integration. Empire reframed as **desert civilization at the heartland** with post-Crusade Mediterranean diaspora. New **Imperial architecture** section adds the full architectural canon (two-tier hierarchy, imperial-only domes and minarets, crystal-warded minarets, pharaonic guardian statues with hybrid crown, hieroglyph-rune hybrid script, oasis gardens as propaganda, overall atmosphere). Sarathis-location open canon partially resolved (desert capital, exact continental placement still open). New open-canon items: imperial spellcasters, minaret crystal-mesh-housing materials, oasis water sources, conscious-vs-independent borrowing of minaret form from [[taran-architecture|Tarran]], hieroglyph-rune translation tradition. OOC block expanded with craft notes (synthesis over mashup, identity-loaded points, preserve form reassign function, architecture carries politics, water as political currency, magical architecture as genre-native).

**Cultural drinks**
- [[elfen-blossom-wines]] — new **Named clan vintages** subsection with five canonical-core named vintages (Starblossom Wine, Lunapetal Wine, Aetherbloom, Dawnpetal Reserve, Celestine Gold). Full ~25-name catalogue still open canon.
- [[velrathi-tea-culture]] — sample-names list restructured into **categorized variety table** (Floral/Fruity, Fermented/Sour, Smoked/Earthy, Gnomish/spiced, Memory-bright, Other/specialist) with the new names from the triple folded into the appropriate categories. Note added on shared roots between Elfen blossom-wine and Velrathi tea names (Starblossom, Dawn Ember) reflecting Elfen aesthetic naming convention applied across both projects.

**Era framework**
- [[eras]] — Crystalline Age section adds "High Arathi Era" as interchangeable name; Crystalline Age remains primary.

**Setting-wide design principles**
- [[inspirations]] — **5 new principles** added to the design-principle catalog (now 15 total). All five passed the two-domain test (the principle surfaces in two or more unrelated topic domains, making it a setting law rather than a one-off pattern):
  - **#11 Stable partnerships beat rivalries** (Velrathi/Tarran, Orden/Marrow, Velrathi/Elfen)
  - **#12 Cultural inheritance is partial** (Rathari from Velrathi bathing; language hierarchy corruption; Arathi conduit fragments)
  - **#13 Designation over acquisition** for powerful + rare elements (Lexanari, chosen observers)
  - **#14 Reality has an immune system** (closed time bubbles + Tome curation + sealed chapters as scaled versions of the same protective function; hiding-truth-as-protection folded in)
  - **#15 Preserve form, reassign function** (Sarathim minarets, Sarathim domes, Druid-as-sub-priesthood)
- Note on each principle: cross-links to the specific wiki pages that demonstrate it; preserved the existing 1-10 numbering, lost-ceiling corollary, and benchmark question intact.

**Open questions and bookkeeping**
- [[open-questions]] — Live-wires section expanded with **18 new prompts** drawn from the seven Doc 03 files (3 from Arathi, 3 from Cosmology, 4 from DescendantCultures, 4 from FourOrders, 2 from HighArathiCampaign, 7 from OriginalHumanoids — minus those already implicit in earlier batch). Resolved/partially-resolved open canon items removed from their source pages: Sarathis location (partially — desert capital; continental placement still open), Elfen blossom-wine named clan vintages (5 of ~25 documented), Velrathi tea variety category list (sample varieties documented; full 500-variety catalogue still deferred).
- [[index]] — Wiki Meta descriptions updated for inspirations and log.

### Source attribution

- Every modified page got the relevant Doc-01 (and Doc-02 where applicable) source files appended to its Sources line. Last-updated bumped to 2026-05-12 across the touched pages.
- No new tags required.
- The Doc 02 craft notes that were inlined as OOC blocks: [[arathi]] (Arathi Doc 02) and [[sarathim]] (BlendedKingdom Doc 02). For the multi-page topics (Cosmology, DescendantCultures, FourOrders, HighArathiCampaign, OriginalHumanoids), Doc 02 craft notes were not inlined this pass because they distribute across many pages without a clean single anchor; the principle-level material from Doc 02 was integrated into the [[inspirations]] design-principle catalog instead. The Doc 02 files remain in `raw/` for reference.
- Per the user's separately-stated plan, chat-log files in `raw/` will eventually be replaced by placeholders pointing to their triple files. **Claude does not perform that edit** (never-modify-raw rule); the user will do it after analysis generation completes.

### Held back / not ingested as canon

- The Doc 02 [META] and Doc 03 [DIAGNOSIS] *project-health* diagnostics from all 7 topics (cheerleading already stripped by the user; substantive material is the principles, which were ingested). The author-side process commentary remains in `raw/` only.

The closed-time-bubble [[rpg/closed-time-bubble|Crystalline Age splat campaign]] stays in `wiki/rpg/` as non-canonical splat material; the Tome's sealing infrastructure remains canonical without the Arathi-Chaos-War event being canonical.

## 2026-05-12 — Draconic + Modernity expert-council triple-set ingest

Ingested two pre-structured **expert-council triples** (six files total) produced by a ChatGPT council session on 2026-05-11:

- `raw/Draconic_01_InWorld_Facts.txt`, `raw/Draconic_02_MetaCommentary.txt`, `raw/Draconic_03_Principles_and_Diagnosis.txt`
- `raw/Modernity_01_InWorld_Facts.txt`, `raw/Modernity_02_MetaCommentary.txt`, `raw/Modernity_03_Principles_and_Diagnosis.txt`

**Source-shape note**: this is the first ingest of the **pre-separated triple format** (In-World Facts / Meta-Commentary / Principles-and-Diagnosis), and it is dramatically easier to ingest than a comparable chat log. Atomic, tagged ([IN-WORLD]/[META]/[DIAGNOSIS]), pre-separated by epistemic register (the meta layer never threatens to leak into in-universe canon by accident), and roughly 100% canon-shaped signal compared to ~15% in a typical chat log. **The shape is endorsed for future stabilized topics.** Chat logs still earn their keep for exploratory work; the triple is the right export shape once a topic has stabilized.

### Decisions taken before writing (user-confirmed)

1. **Doc 03 setting-wide principles** (cognitive-first design, multi-axial measurement, anti-linearity, the seven-word thematic spine, etc.) → folded into `wiki/inspirations.md` as a new top-level section.
2. **Doc 02 [META] craft notes** → inline at the bottom of the relevant in-world pages, in collapsed `<details class="ooc-block">` blocks. New pattern precedent: applied to `wiki/draconic-language.md` and `wiki/modernity.md`.
3. **New Modernity framework page** → `perspective: [reference]` (treated as measurement vocabulary, like `tags.md` or `naming-conventions.md`), not an in-universe Tome page.

### Wiki changes

- **`wiki/modernity.md` created** — new reference framework page (`perspective: [reference]`, `knowledge_access: [meta]`). Documents the six-axis modernity measurement (infrastructure / magical / bureaucratic / urban / trade / subsistence-distance), the five-stage civilizational spectrum (Stage 1 Subsistence → Stage 5 Conduit-Centered Hypercivilization, with explicit Arathi-as-Stage-5 / Sarathim-as-Stage-3 / Bold-as-Stage-3-approaching-4 / Orden-Compact-cities-as-Stage-3 placements), the **lost-ceiling principle** (peak civilization is behind, not ahead), **bureaucracy-as-technology** (administrative density is infrastructure on par with conduits and magitek), the **infrastructure-not-smokestack** Stage-4 aesthetic, the multi-axial vocabulary that replaces "tech level," and the **anti-linearity-as-setting-law** principle. Includes OOC craft-notes block.
- **`wiki/draconic-language.md` updated** — major new section **"Cognition and resonance"** added between Phonology and Morphology, covering: phonology-as-resonance-engineering (basalt chambers co-evolved with Council-formal speech, the room is part of the utterance); phonological scalability across hatchling/adult/elder; **conceptual clustering** (`RhTrKh` as one concept seen four ways, not four ideas — implies dragons grammatically resist some mortal thoughts); Council-formal as the named highest register, with the full register table (Council-formal / Ritual / Legal / Everyday / Hatchling-acquisition); **the mortal-limit reframed as simultaneous semantic compression** (cognitive bandwidth gap, not pronunciation — even Weavespinners only approximate); neurological foundation in dragons; Council-formal as desecrated form (cross-linked to `flesh-eaters.md`). OOC craft-notes block added at the bottom (cognitive-first-design, geological-rhythm, sensory-implication-beats-description, English-mouth-feel rejection, no-neutral-noun grammar, environment-is-part-of-utterance scene-writing note, linguistic-trauma as usable material, sacredness-as-emergent-structure).
- **`wiki/flesh-eaters.md` updated** — Council-Draconic mockery section extended with the **desecration-as-linguistic-trauma** framing: the practice is not mockery; some Council members cannot hear certain root cadences without flinching; trauma lodged at the neurological-foundation level Draconic occupies; choice of Council-formal is doctrinally preserved across cache cycles; cult is **grammatically obscene** (structural inversion, not opposite). Cross-links to the new `draconic-language.md` sections.
- **`wiki/arathi.md` updated** — new **"Civilizational stage"** subsection under World Scale explicitly placing the Arathi at peak as the canonical **Stage 5** of the modernity framework and naming them as the **lost ceiling** against which modern Eadras measures itself.
- **`wiki/sarathim.md` updated** — Sarathim Empire at peak placed as the **canonical Stage 3** of the framework — the illustration of *administrative depth and industrial volume scale independently* (advanced bureaucracy + dense urbanism + deep scholarship + **no** mass mechanization; runs on paper, ink, scribes, contracts, registries).
- **`wiki/bold.md` updated** — Bold placed as **Stage 3 approaching Stage 4** — closest modern Eadras comes to recovering the lost Stage 5 ceiling; the **arcane-urban-modernization aesthetic** (enchanted cranes, conduit freight, magical refrigeration; no smokestacks) named explicitly.
- **`wiki/orden.md` updated** — Conduit Compact cities placed as **Stage 3**, with the inland clans and smaller coastal Jarldoms preserving a **Stage 2** configuration. The Orden are flagged as the framework's clearest example of one people legitimately occupying two stages simultaneously, demonstrating the anti-linearity principle.
- **`wiki/inspirations.md` updated** — new top-level section **"Setting-wide design principles"** added. Catalogues the **seven-word thematic spine** (continuity · memory · catastrophe · identity · structure · survival · meaning) and the **ten cross-cutting principles** (cognitive-first design, multi-axial measurement, sacredness-as-emergent-structure, antagonists-as-grammatical-inversion, bodily-limitation-as-kindness, porous-category-boundaries, resonance-as-deep-logic, co-evolved geography, anti-linearity-as-setting-law, aesthetic-refusal-of-genre-defaults). Includes a **lost-ceiling corollary** and **the benchmark** (*"would this thing be plausibly produced by the being or culture said to produce it?"*).
- **`wiki/open-questions.md` updated** — new top-level **"Live wires"** section catalogues the 10 story-prompt-shaped open questions surfaced by the two council sessions (5 from each), with target wiki pages.
- **`wiki/index.md` updated** — `modernity` added to Wiki Meta with description; `inspirations` description updated to reflect the new design-principle catalog; `log` description updated to point at this entry.

### Bookkeeping notes

- **Source attribution** added to every modified page (`Draconic_01_InWorld_Facts.txt` / `Draconic_02_MetaCommentary.txt` / `Draconic_03_Principles_and_Diagnosis.txt` / `Modernity_*` as applicable). Last-updated bumped to 2026-05-12.
- **No new tags** required. `wiki/modernity.md` uses `[meta, conventions]` matching the existing pattern of reference pages (`open-questions.md`, `tags.md`).
- **The Doc 02 [META] and Doc 03 [DIAGNOSIS] project-health diagnostics** (the "every entry spawns 2-3 more is a success signal" / "inspiration is rising not collapsing" / "excavating not inventing" / "emotionally sustainable" / "curiosity not just discipline" / "final council observation" material) were **not** ingested into the wiki — those are author-process notes and live in `raw/` only. The setting-wide *principles* (which are different — they govern how Eadras itself is built) did make it in, via `wiki/inspirations.md`. This matches the user's prior `project-aramet-meta-framing` rule (NEVER add the author-meta layer to the wiki) while preserving the craft-principle material that is genuinely useful to future development.

### Held back / not ingested as canon

- The **five live-wire story prompts from each side** were filed as open-canon items in `wiki/open-questions.md` rather than worked into new pages. Working a single one of them into a full page would substantially exceed this ingest's scope.

## 2026-05-09 — Extra Large Grok Chat 5-9-2026 ingest: magic-system rework, cultural drinks, lifestyle deepening, RPG splat folder

Major dense ingest from `raw/Extra large grok chat 5-9-2026.txt` (~3,400 lines, multiple discussion threads spanning a single multi-hour evening-into-morning conversation). User direction during the ingest planning: **note-and-defer for the magic-system retcon's downstream effects**, **stub-now-rename-later for the D&D-coded Feywild/Shadowdark names**, and **a new `wiki/rpg/` subfolder for splat-book material**.

### Tier 1: canon-shifting (3 items)

- **Magic-system rework — Sorcerers and Druids retired in favor of new orders.** This **partially reverses the 2026-05-08 *"document the influences, no rework"* decision** documented at the end of [[inspirations]] and the previous log entry. The Sorcerer order was too distinctive in its [[inspirations#Tales of the Firestaff — novel series (James Galloway / "Fel")|Galloway-derived form]] to be kept as-is even with documentation. New orders: **[[lexanari]]** (Name-Bound — innate-only mortal speakers of the Primordial Language; mortal minds can't hold the deific complexity of the Primordial tier, so vague invocation is catastrophic; most candidates die in training; fills the niche the borrowed Druid concept used to occupy) and **[[netharim]]** (Little Gods — intuitive reality-shapers whose power scales with the accuracy of their personally-studied internal model of reality; worldwide order, numerous, politically and scholastically active; fills the niche the borrowed Sorcerer concept used to occupy). **[[druids]]** redefined as a specialized sub-priesthood of [[qoxli|Qoxli]], [[sylph|Sylph]], and [[nox|Nox]] (no longer a standalone order); self-sufficient wilderness-skilled mediators between mortals and the [[fae|fae]]. **[[true-language]]** extended with the explicit naming of the four-tier hierarchy as **True / Primordial / Divine / Arcane** plus a section on the Lexanari as the canonical mortal exception who reaches the Primordial tier. **Note-and-defer on existing pages**: [[magic-in-eadras]] (top-of-page banner saying Sorcerer/Druid/Weave material is partial-rework-pending), [[order-sharanel]], [[order-sworn-sorcerers]], [[weavespinners]], [[dashar]], [[sorcerer-crusade]], [[heart-of-the-goddess]] (each get a brief banner pointing to the new orders; existing narrative preserved unchanged for continuity until the user's later make-it-mine pass). The **Weave** is candidate-for-removal in that pass except possibly its defensive function as a Lirra ward against outsider magic theft.
- **Velrathi tea culture formalized.** The Velrathi **do not drink alcohol** — they treat it as cognitively detrimental — and instead developed an extensive tea culture around the load-bearing finding that **rationed tea consumption during study produces a measurable, perceptible improvement in mental acuity**. Tea was a Velrathi discovery (a single scholar dried particular leaves and steeped them just to see what would happen). The Velrathi commissioned the [[elfen|Elfen]] for ~10–15 new varieties; the Elfen fell deeply in love with the project and **vastly overshot**, returning every decade for centuries with 12–15 brand-new varieties at a time, until ~500 distinct varieties existed. Three formal roles: Tea Ceremony (formal ritual when superior visits inferior; selecting the right tea for the moment is a refined intellectual art), Personal Preference (decades-long search for the single favorite tea), Meditative Practice (focusing aid for memory-palace entry, not divination). Seven major Elfen clans grow the popular varieties in volume; seventeen minor clans grow rarer specialty varieties. Modern post-Banishment elves have added ~65 varieties in the last 10,000 years. New page [[velrathi-tea-culture]]; [[velrathi]] updated to link.
- **Beast-Folk Veil correction (semantic-only).** The 2026-05-09 conversation included a clarification that the [[beast-folk|Beast-Folk]] **gave up** their [[demon-war|Demon War]] memories to [[sylph|Sylph]] — they were not taken. The existing [[beast-folk]] page already had this framing correct (the user clarified the assistant's misstatement, not the wiki's record). The new material added is the **generational acculturation** distinction: the **first generation** chose lightness as a deliberate act of survival; **all subsequent generations** were acculturated into the deliberately-joyful civilization built afterward, never having the lost memories themselves. Both are real Beast-Folk; the civilization is the result of the founders' decision and the citizens are the result of the civilization. Substantial **lifestyle deepening** added: loud/expressive/physically affectionate; quick to forgive; jokey-and-attentive while working; two-mode life (work-mode dirty-and-focused vs. off-work-mode clean-fed-communal); communal-bath-and-shared-food anchors. New magical Beast-Folk wagon-pool with sealed [[eadras-cosmology|Plane of Water]] portal documented (3ft deep, fills/drains at 1ft/min, every Beast-Folk wagon carries one, open invitation to caravan companions of any race who haven't been recently insulting). Updated [[beast-folk]].

### Tier 2: cultural drinks tree (8 new pages)

The 2026-05-09 ingest produced a complete cultural-drinks layer of the wiki. Each major race got a signature drink documented; the universal alchemical-base substance got its own page; the Velrathi got tea (no alcohol).

- **[[aqua-vitae]] created** — Universal alchemical solvent and catalyst that underlies most potion-craft on Eadras. Distilled from each race's signature alcoholic drink (or a normal fermented beverage); each race's Aqua Vitae retains characteristics of its source. Elven Aqua Vitae (light, subtly bubbly, floral-herbal) detailed in full; other-race varieties sketched.
- **[[elfen-blossom-wines]] created** — Family of fermented Elfen wines (each clan keeps its own closely-guarded recipe; berries, edible flowers, herbs); aged in **sung living-wood barrels** that may either remain attached to the living tree or be separated once formed; magic de-alcoholization for children at celebrations. The high-magic variant (mana-rich ingredients from ley-line zones) is the source for the most prized [[aqua-vitae|Elven Aqua Vitae]]. Updated [[elfen]] to link.
- **[[goblin-ancestor-liquor]] created** — Harsh, high-proof spirit inherited from [[grug|Grug]] underground brewing; smells and tastes like brimstone, tar, pitch, and scorched earth (no Industrial-Revolution comparisons — the world has a magical industrial revolution, not a coal one). Goblins know exactly how nasty outsiders find it and embrace it; in their language the drink is called something equivalent to *Nasty Ancestor Liquor*. Updated [[goblins]] and [[grug]] to link.
- **[[orcish-drinks]] created** — Two-drink tradition matching the nomadic-and-settled split of orcish life. **Saddle Brew** is the low-alcohol communal-rotating fermented drink brewed in saddle-bags during long marches (every rider's bag pools into a common batch; clan rotates through batches; primary purpose is keeping plains water safe to drink). **Stonefire** is the high-proof distilled spirit produced only in clan holds and cities; doubles as a wound-and-instrument sterilizer; refines further into orcish [[aqua-vitae]]. Updated [[orcs]] to link.
- **[[taran-venom-aged-liquor]] created** — [[taran|Taran]] distilled spirit aged with carefully-selected animal venom that denatures over time but leaves a complex flavor signature behind. By the [[firethorn-empire|Imperial era]], aging time was a class marker (6mo = common swill; nobles drank 20+yr; finest 50+yr). Safe for Taran (genetic poison immunity); mildly to moderately dangerous for non-Taran races; serves as a subtle "the cup test" of true Taran identity. Updated [[taran]] to link.
- **[[orden-whale-honey-mead]] created** — Strong golden mead from "whale honey," a thick amber substance the great northern whales squirt into cold water to lure schools of small prey. Cooperative harvesting voyage with the [[merrow|Marrow]] who guide the whales to the surface; Orden harvesters use long ivory-and-teak syringes sealed with whale blubber to draw the substance while the whale feeds. 6-day voyages harvest from dozens of whales; participation is the **dangerous rite of passage** every young Ordon makes at least once. Finished mead is always shared with the Marrow, who carry bottles back to their underwater cities. Updated [[orden]] to link.
- **[[velrathi-cognitive-frogs]] created** — Upper-class Velrathi custom of carrying small **brilliantly multicolored** poison-dart-style frogs in elegant glass containers and **licking the frog's back directly** for a cognitive-acuity dose. Velrathi have generational immunity to the deadly fraction of the toxin; the practice is genuinely common among scholars, nobles, and mages. Deeply unsettling to outsiders; contributes substantially to the Velrathi's broader unsettling reputation. Updated [[velrathi]] to link.
- **[[bathing-customs]] created** — Cross-cultural compendium. Established that the **communal-bathhouse tradition is a Velrathi invention** (magical purification of all building water + auto-scrub cubicles before the soak); propagates downstream to the [[rathar|Rathari]] (full structure, hygiene-only disposition, scholars often need family interventions to bathe) and to the [[beast-folk|Beast-Folk]] (communal soak preserved, formal protocol dropped, magic-conjured tubs at every settlement, elder always present, magic wagon-pool with sealed Plane-of-Water portal). [[orden|Orden]] cast-iron communal pots (heaviest object in any village, **double as emergency kid-shelter during attacks**) developed independently. [[gnomes|Gnome]] pattern (eh, once or twice a week, fine) and [[goblins|Goblin]] pattern (filthy at work, hot bath after) likewise distinct.

Hub page [[food-and-drink]] updated to link the entire new tree.

### Tier 2: cultural deepening + clarifications (multiple existing pages)

- **[[philosophy-of-contribution]] created** — New cross-cultural page documenting the shared *every capable person contributes / freeloading not tolerated / sensible exceptions for inability* value running through the [[velrathi|Velrathi]] → [[grug|Grug]] → [[goblins|Goblin]] descent line, with each culture's distinct expression of the principle (Velrathi = intellectual/skilled/artistic contribution; Grug = deep cultural respect for physical labor with even high-rank keeping their hands on tools; Goblins = radically egalitarian work-gang rotation that includes kings, archmages, and high priests). Updated [[goblins]] (egalitarian work-gang section added) and [[grug]] (cultural-labor-respect framing added).
- **[[taran]] updated** — Full **Poison Immunity** section added: ~10,000-year inoculation ritual (gradually-increasing childhood doses of varied poisons; toughens AND immunizes); now genetic but ritual still performed as cultural rite of passage (most Taran don't realize the trait has become inherited). Full **Venomous Pets** section added: cultural appreciation for venomous animals as status symbols; engineered breeds commissioned from the [[velrathi|Velrathi]] (Venomfang Warhounds = neurotoxic-saliva war-dogs; Blood Parrots = crimson toxic-bite/claw intelligent aggressive; Ironscale Monitors = heavily-armored hemotoxic-claw monitor lizards); pragmatic-not-moral rejection of weaponized fleas (uncontrollable propagation = backfire risk).
- **[[elfen]] updated** — **Drink** subsection added (blossom wines, sung living-wood barrels, magic de-alc for kids, [[aqua-vitae|Elven Aqua Vitae]]). **Tea** subsection added (the centuries-long Elfen overshoot of the Velrathi commission; seven major + seventeen minor tea-growing clans; Elfen own much-more-casual tea culture as side effect). New **Relationship with animals and nature** section: no traditional pets, herbivores beg snacks, carnivores killed regretfully when entering villages; Elfen as guardians-of-natural-balance who hunt both herbivores and carnivores when ecosystem requires (with ritualistic respect, never for food/sport); non-clear-cut harrow-style agriculture between existing trees with nature-magic light/nutrient management.
- **[[velrathi]] updated** — **Drink** subsection added (no alcohol, primary beverage tea; full link to [[velrathi-tea-culture]]; resolves the food-as-fuel/tea-as-art apparent contradiction via the mental-acuity rationale). **Cognitive frogs** subsection added (link to [[velrathi-cognitive-frogs]]).
- **[[goblins]] updated** — Egalitarian work-gang rotation section added (every goblin including kings is on the labor roster); after-work bath-and-Ancestor-Liquor pattern noted; cross-link to [[philosophy-of-contribution]] and [[goblin-ancestor-liquor]].
- **[[grug]] updated** — Cultural-labor-respect framing added in Pre-War Society; cross-link to [[philosophy-of-contribution]] and [[goblin-ancestor-liquor]] (Grug origin of the brimstone-and-tar drink).
- **[[orcs]] updated** — Saddle Brew + Stonefire section added; cross-link to [[orcish-drinks]] and [[aqua-vitae]].
- **[[orden]] updated** — Whale-honey mead expanded into the summary; cast-iron communal-pot bathing tradition (which doubles as kid-shelter during attacks) noted; cross-links to [[orden-whale-honey-mead]] and [[bathing-customs]].
- **[[beast-folk]] updated** — Generational acculturation framing added under Origin (first generation chose lightness; subsequent generations inherited it). New **Daily life and personality** section added (loud/expressive/affectionate/forgiving/two-mode personality; jokey-while-working texture; communal bath and shared food as daily anchors; cross-link to [[bathing-customs]] for the magical wagon-pool and Plane-of-Water portal).

### Tier 3: held captures + clarifications

- **Internal Cosmology — [[feywild|Feywild]] and [[shadowdark|Shadowdark]] outer regions formalized as "Deep Feywild" and "Deep Shadowdark"** (provisional names). The "near-infinite extent beyond the reflection" was already documented on both pages from a 2026-04-30 ingest; the 2026-05-09 conversation captured the user's own restatement of it while explicitly **flagging the entire pair of plane names as D&D-coded placeholders** likely to be renamed before publication. Stubbed under placeholders per user direction.
- **Pre-Cataclysm Arathi geology clarification.** The pre-Cataclysm world was **tectonically still** — fixed continental layout, no plate motion — but **not geologically dead**. Earthquakes were a constant low-level background; an active subterranean hydrological cycle (massive underground oceanic reservoirs exchanging water with the surface) operated continuously. The Arathi lived with everyday geological churn but had no concept that the continents themselves could move at scale. Updated [[eadras-tectonic-history]], [[worldbreaker-mechanism]] (in two places), and [[eras]].
- **RPG splat-book material — `wiki/rpg/` subfolder created** per user direction to keep splat material from polluting in-universe canon. New folder pages: [[rpg/README]] (subfolder overview, segregation rationale) and [[rpg/closed-time-bubble]] (full standalone treatment of the **Closed-Time-Bubble Chaos Crusade** flagship campaign concept for the Crystalline Age splat — players as designated cosmic observers, the closed-time-bubble climax that does not break the *Time Is Absolute* [[omniversal-laws|law]], the Tome's complicit sealing of the chapter, the full design rationale for what makes the campaign work). Updated [[eras]] to link the standalone page; the original inline summary on [[eras]] preserved for context. Adventure content remains explicitly non-canonical (the Crystalline Age does not contain a remembered Chaos Crusade; the Tome holds the sealed chapter).

### Bookkeeping notes

- **Source attribution** added to every modified page: `Extra large grok chat 5-9-2026.txt` appended to Sources, Last updated bumped to 2026-05-09.
- **No new tags** required. All new pages used existing taxonomy.
- **Open-canon items** noted on each new page where appropriate; aggregation pass into [[open-questions]] performed in the same session.
- **One conversational ambiguity, since resolved**: the user said "Quetzal" when naming one of the three nature-and-fey deities the new Druid sub-priesthood serves. Treated during ingest as a clear slip for [[qoxli|Qoxli]] given the role description and Qoxli's existing canonical domain ("the wild, animals, the bow, forests, freedom, the chase"); **user confirmed Qoxli is correct** in the same session.

### Held back / not ingested as canon

- **User's Suno music links** (the conversation contained four published tracks — *Blood on the Halo*, *Crosswinds*, *The Mermaid Drank The Rum*, *Horse Run Home*, plus a Beast-Folk feast-day track and a goblin work-song with the *"Bottom of the pile / Still holding it up"* hook). Goblin lyrics user-confirmed as strong material; Beast-Folk and Orc-anthem lyrics user-acknowledged as still-too-generic and likely to be regenerated. None pulled into wiki pages without user direction.
- **Architecture mockup discussion** for a *new kingdom* (separate from Sarathim and the Firethorn Empire) blending New Kingdom Egyptian + Italian Renaissance + Ottoman aesthetics. Notable detail captured but not yet canonized: **Ottoman-style minarets and grand domes are reserved for imperial buildings; other Ottoman elements freely cascade to ordinary buildings**; the imperial-minaret-houses-spell-crystal-protection pattern matches [[taran-architecture]]'s spell-crystal minaret tradition but the originating culture for *this* particular new palace had not yet been named when the conversation moved on.
