## 2026-05-08 — Grok Chat 5-8-26 ingest (Tier 1 + 2): metaphysics, Lost Primer, eras, modern cultures, three architectures

Major dense ingest from `raw/Grok Chat 5-8-26.txt` (~14 pages, multiple discussion threads). Per user direction: full ingest of canon-shifting (Tier 1) + new modern cultures and architectures (Tier 2); Tier 3 (dragon-culture refinements, closed-time-bubble splatbook campaign) deferred. Cultures ingested as confident canon. Velrathi *genius loci* term resolved as "use both" — Eadras-native term *Stone-Bound* primary, *genius loci* as scholarly comparative gloss.

### Tier 1: canon-shifting (4 items)

- **Light/darkness welcome principle** added to `index.md`. User-mandated welcome blurb on the index/welcome page: *"In this world, light and darkness cannot exist without each other. The presence of one makes the other bigger, deeper, and brighter…"* Anti-grimdark tonal statement; epic dark fantasy with earned hope, not nihilism.
- **`observer-and-naming.md` created** — new metaphysics page formalizing observer-dependent reality and naming-stabilizes-reality as an extension of `true-language.md`. **Key Eadras-specific consequence**: because Evye and Fryr (the Primordial Duo) sacrificed themselves completely into the Mythos, **no ultimate observer remains in Eadras** — making reality here slightly less stable than in most Mythoi and load-bearing on naming, observation, memory, and tradition. Connects Neverborn (manic self-observation), Chaos (unnamed unreality), Tome of Baldaran (designated cosmic observer), and Aberrations (observer-stabilized residual-Chaos pockets).
- **`tome-of-baldaran.md` updated** with curator-of-acceptable-reality role. Tome records reality after-the-fact and via observer-witnessing; can choose what to reveal; sealed chapters exist for events scrubbed by reality (the Tome agrees with the universe's editorial choices and enforces them downstream). Dovetails with the existing `_sealed/` folder pattern at the wiki-meta level.
- **`lost-primer.md` created** — the canonical explanation for how post-Arathi civilizations got working crystalmancy/magitek. Joint Velrathi-Rathari expedition early in the High Firethorn Era opened an Arathi Deep Vault, recovered a foundational primer, used it to seed Velrathi/Rathari magitek/crystalmancy. Vault overrun and emptied by demons in Demon War; nothing of the Primer survived. **The Grug attendants kept meticulous notes that passed to gnomes and goblins** — canonical reason for gnomish racial obsession with vault-archaeology (ancestral trauma + restoration of lost greatness). Velrathi/Rathari never thought to ask the Grug if they took notes; Katharim still don't think to ask the gnomes. Updated `gnomes.md`, `katharim.md`, `deep-vaults.md` (vault inventory bumped from 5 opened/7 sealed/12 known to **6 opened/7 sealed/13 known**).
- **`eras.md` created** — the four officially-supported playable RPG eras (Star Wars Saga Edition-style splatbook structure):
  - **The Crystalline Age** (Arathi peak, centuries before Worldbreaker)
  - **The High Firethorn Era** (middle Firethorn, Three Races at peak, dragon/unicorn mercenaries)
  - **The Demon War**
  - **The Modern Era** (default canonical present, with two variants: **Spear Era** [default] and **Second Falling** [alternate dark future ~8000–12000 ya post-Demon-War with demons sending second asteroid carrying Demon Lords]). Modern Era is the spine of the core book; the other three are splat material.
  - Closed-Time-Bubble Chaos Incursion is filed as splatbook campaign material for Crystalline Age (NOT main canon — the Tome's curator role can absorb it as one of countless sealed-chapter possibilities).

### Tier 2: cultures + architecture (10 items)

- **`velrathi-architecture.md` created** — full Velrathi spell-lattice tradition. Gothic black-stone cathedrals/monasteries/castles; every architectural detail is a magical focus; whole building is one spell matrix; **willingly-bound wardspirit (Stone-Bound, akin to a *genius loci*)** inhabits each structure; **spell-plate + donation box at every entrance** for ongoing energetic and material upkeep. 20k+ years of iteration. Hybrid Velrathi-Elfen sites documented. Updated `velrathi.md` to link.
- **`taran-architecture.md` created** — three strict traditions: (1) **Military** = austere Roman, army-controlled, minimal decoration even on permanent fortresses; (2) **Sacred** = Roman + Bagan + Javanese, varies by religious order, every detail a magical focus, whole-temple spell matrix; (3) **Imperial** = Roman + Ottoman hybrid with **slender minaret-towers housing spell-crystals projecting protective wards**, reserved exclusively for buildings serving central Empire's bureaucracy/command/ceremony. **Imperial Palace = Angkor-Wat-scale layout** with grand open grounds, internal temples in many orders' styles, core admin buildings in imperial domed-and-minaret style. Updated `taran.md` to link.
- **`elfen-architecture.md` created** — song-shaping of living trees/fungi/roots into rigidified architecture; living-cathedral aesthetic; heart-groves, canopy walks, root-vaults, song-runes. **NO crystalmancy** — that was Arathi-only. Hybrid Velrathi-Elfen sites canonical. Updated `elfen.md` to clarify materials.
- **Tarran origin reframe in `taran.md`**: Tarran started as **peacekeepers** protecting non-warrior populations of all three races from external threats (wild beasts, rogue dragons, rogue unicorns); evolved into **police/law-enforcement** as crime emerged across the cooperative age; after Melania's retreat (~20–19,000 BP) asked themselves *"why aren't WE ruling?"* — birthing the Firethorn Empire (~18,000 BP). Peacekeeper → police → empire arc. Consistent with previously-canonical "first 21,000 years performed their duty honorably" framing — adds detail rather than overwriting.
- **`sarathim.md` created** — major new modern human culture. Renaissance-Italy + Ancient-Egypt + Islamic-Golden-Age fusion. Self-image: **true heirs of the Velrathi legacy** (vs. Katharim death-priesthood, Laughing Third chaos). Merchant-prince house league + ceremonial Emperor + Imperial Decree on charity. Capital **Sarathis** built atop a [[seven-conduits|conduit]] terminus with sorcerer tower; **broken in the Sorcerer Crusade** when Black-Hand-stirred mob + 3 military religious orders sacked the tower. Sarathis is one of the 6 destroyed Crusade conduit sites. Modern Sarathim are faded-glory diaspora across Azure Basin and beyond.
- **`house-sitharis.md` created** — wealthiest Sarathim noble house. Drug trade (mind-altering substances ONLY, not spices). Three internal castes: **Clear Minds** (sober political operators), **Socialites** (half-lucid public-face party-throwers and intelligence network), **The Blissed** (deeply-hedonistic majority). Head of house always takes the symbolic name **Arissa** (female) / **Arian** (male) on assuming position. Doesn't play the political game; if crossed, retaliates outside the rules with elegant poisons. Hospitality culture = drugging guests as courtesy. Patron of the world's most magnificent free-public zoo, strongest illusion magic in Sarathim world, leading bardic patron. Imperial-decreed charity targets orphans + ex-prisoners as long-term recruitment pipeline. Criminal-guild ties across multiple civilizations. Reputation: *"If your heart desires it, House Sitharis can procure it… for a price."*
- **`clan-nightshade.md` created** — elven clan allied to House Sitharis for centuries. Master horticulturalists running all major Sitharis drug crops + experimentation + quietly producing plant-based poisons (kept very quiet). **Major bridge between elven and human society** — bring industrialized goods/luxuries/exotic crafts back into elven lands in exchange for unparalleled botanical expertise. Other elves view with envy + dependence + suspicion. Research animals from the Sitharis zoo (venom extraction etc.).
- **`orden.md` updated** — Viking-clan Orden + Hanseatic Conduit Compact merged. Existing 4-century raiding-to-trading transition matured into the **Conduit Compact**: 6–8 conduit-anchored Orden trade-cities bound by **High Council of Guildmasters** in rotating neutral spires; tight Order Sharanel integration (every Compact city has a Tower of Lirra); controls overland/riverine ley-trade; concedes sea-trade to Bold; nicknamed "Gray Ledger" by Bold; pragmatic, contract-obsessed ("a contract is a spell — break it and the Weave breaks you"). Compact overlays older clan-and-Jarl governance — Jarls and High King handle non-trade governance; Compact handles trade and mutual defense. **Naming conflict resolution**: per user direction, the Hanseatic-style merchant league IS the Orden, not a separate civilization with the same name.
- **`bold.md` updated** — Bold reframed as the **Bold Conduit Republic** ("Spirehold"), elected merchant-prince city-state, NOT a kingdom. Elected **Spirewarden** (Doge-like, term-limited, succession constrained), guild council, permanent Weavespinner advisor. Aggressive sea-ley trade with **Spire-Step long-distance jumps**; relic auctions; magitek innovation; black-market pre-Cataclysm artifacts (open secret). Direct rival to Orden Conduit Compact ("the Compact owns the land. We own the rest."). Pre-republican royal era preserved as historical layer (ceremonial old castle compound now used for state occasions). Women hold significant merchant-prince seats. Masked carnivals, public spectacle culture. Quietly cordial with House Sitharis.
- **`azure-basin.md` created** — explicitly **non-Roman** Mediterranean-style coastal zone of fragmented polities. Greek maritime poleis backbone. Six broad zones: **Venethar** (Venice equivalent — lagoon republic, Council of Azure Magnates), **Serene Principalities** (Provence/Occitan), **Rif Clans & Oasis Cities** (N. African/Berber), **Iberian Marches** (Andalusian + duende), **Balkan Heights** (highland clans, gusle epic poetry), **Levantine Shore Enclaves** (multicultural ports, philosophical schools). Distributed Lirran shrines (no single dominant Tower). Tariq al-Honor strongest in southern/Levantine zones. Trade-triangle corner with Orden (continental) and Bold (independent maritime). Sarathim diaspora heavily concentrated here. Black Hand favored operating environment.
- **`tariq-al-honor.md` created** — syncretic post-Firethorn cultural-religious tradition. **La Fe de la Espina Ardiente** (Faith of the Burning Thorn): Catholic-Islamic syncretism; Maryam = La Reina de las Espinas, Queen of Thorns; Isa-Muhammad as blood-brothers in prophecy; Trinity of the Burning Rose. Veiled women as sacred Flores de la Espina (wielding huge soft power). Caballeros de la Espina (machismo + protection). Festivals (La Noche de las Espinas — 72hr Carnival/Eid/Día de los Muertos blend). Thorn Laws (variable across city-states). Thornscar bloodlines. Strongest in southern/Levantine Azure Basin; significant influence in Iberian Marches.

## 2026-05-08 — Inspirations catalog populated (three tiers: Direct fictional, Real-world references, Background)

User disclosed in conversation the structural inspirations behind several major Eadras concepts. The previously-empty `inspirations.md` is now populated with **three tiers**:

- **Direct fictional concept influences** — fiction works that contributed specific named concepts lifted from another author's invented world.
- **Real-world references** — scientific theories, mythological traditions, and other real-world inputs that informed Eadras concepts. *These are not fictional borrowings.* Concepts informed by real-world references remain the author's original work in the standard authorial sense — every fantasy author draws on real-world knowledge.
- **Background / atmospheric fictional influences** — the complete fiction reading-list that shaped Eadras's general register and feel.

This conversation began with the user reviewing the **Four Major Traditions** of magic (Priests, Druids, Wizards, Sorcerers) and asking how integrated they were because they "may be too distinctively borrowed from another author." After audit, the user disclosed the full inspirations map and explicitly chose to **document the influences** rather than restructure the magic system: *"That's why it's so clean and consistent."* The borrowing is conscious and structured, complemented by substantial original elaboration; no rework is planned.

### Direct fictional concept influences (7 entries)

- **Tales of the Firestaff** (James Galloway / "Fel"): Niami → [[lirra|Lirra]]; Sorcerers; the Orders / Four Major Traditions; the Weave; most of the rest of the magic mechanics; Firestaff → conceptual ancestor of the [[spear-of-crystallized-entropy|Spear of Crystallized Entropy]]
- **Weavespinner / Subjugation** (Galloway, *Firestaff* follow-up): [[bastion-of-light|Bastion of Light]]; [[nexus|Nexus]]
- **Nexus of Kelleran** (Wayne Edward Clarke): Source / Eldritch / Conduits triad; basic conception of [[dragons|Dragons]] and [[unicorns|Unicorns]]
- **Bard's Tales (Rose series)** (R22CoolGuy, storiesonline.com): [[the-three|The Three]]; [[dao|Dao]]; [[runeswords|Runeswords]]; [[mythos|Mythos]] cosmological unit; Progenitor Races structural pattern; Exile concept
- **Discworld** (Terry Pratchett): silicon trolls → seed of Eadras [[trolls|Trolls]]
- **Temeraire** (Naomi Novik): dragons-as-mercenaries strand of Eadras [[dragons|dragon]] culture
- **Valdemar** (Mercedes Lackey): Companions → seed of the spirit-component rule in [[necromancy-and-undeath|Necromancy]]

### Real-world references (2 entries)

- **K–T boundary impact theory** (scientific framework, Alvarez et al. 1980 onward): informed the **physical mechanism** of the [[arathi-cataclysm|Cataclysm]] — falling-star strike, global devastation, ecological reset. The Cataclysm itself remains the author's original work; no fictional precedent identified for the specific synthesis (astrophysical impact + 70%-land → 30%-land inversion + millions-of-years-ago framing).
- **Global flood mythology** (cross-cultural tradition: Mesopotamian / Hebrew / Greek / Hindu / Mesoamerican / Chinese / etc.): informed the **cultural and narrative frame** of the Cataclysm — diminished-present-after-lost-age archetype, surviving fragments and folk memory.

These are not fictional borrowings; concepts informed by real-world references remain the author's original work.

### Background / atmospheric fictional influences (15 entries — complete fiction reading-list)

The Background tier is the complete reading-list of works that shaped Eadras at any level; every Direct-influence work is also listed here, because every author who contributed a specific named concept also shaped the general register and feel through small background details that diffuse throughout the setting. (User correction during the session: *"all should be in background as well then because background details from all influence small background details throughout the setting."*)

Background-only (9): Belgariad/Malloreon (Eddings), Black Company (Cook), Elantris (Sanderson), Princess Bride (Goldman), Riftwar (Feist), Sword of Truth (Goodkind), Wheel of Time (Jordan), Witcher (Sapkowski), and Valdemar's general atmospheric register (Valdemar's specific Companions/necromancy-spirit-rule contribution is filed under Direct; the work itself appears in both lists).

Background-plus-Direct (6 — appearing in both lists): Tales of the Firestaff (Galloway), Weavespinner / Subjugation (Galloway), Nexus of Kelleran (Clarke), Bard's Tales / Rose series (R22CoolGuy), Discworld (Pratchett), Temeraire (Novik), Valdemar (Lackey).

The user explicitly noted that the boundary between Direct and Background is not airtight — some Background entries (the Valdemar Companions example surfaced during the conversation) actually contributed specific concepts that are documented under more specific tags. The Valdemar promotion is the precedent for future Background → Direct migrations.

### Original-content disclosure (alongside the borrowings)

User explicitly identified as their own original work, distinct from the borrowed seeds: **the Cataclysm** (informed by K–T impact theory and global flood myth — both real-world references, not fictional borrowings; the event itself, the 70%-land → 30%-land inversion synthesis, and the specific mechanism are original to Eadras), [[worldender|Worldbreaker]], [[kudur-etir|Kudur-eṭir]], the Spear's specific mechanics and lore beyond the Firestaff seed, [[rathar|Rathar]], [[orden|Orden]], [[sea-tua|Sea'tua]], [[tome-of-baldaran|Tome of Baldaran]] framing, the dragon Fire-of-the-World non-distinction, the Three-State Model (Quintessence/Eldritch/Mana), the plate-tectonic timeline, [[crystalmancy|Crystalmancy]], [[magitek|Magitek]], the modern races, the [[deep-vaults|Deep Vaults]], and the [[arathi|Arathi]] civilization as a whole. This list is illustrative, not exhaustive — the user explicitly noted that the catalog is "the solid core" of inspirations, not an exhaustive reading-list (museum visits, D&D books, life in the middle ages, YouTube worldbuilding videos, and so on were excluded by intent).

The user clarified the distinction explicitly: a concept counts as **original** if it has no *fictional* direct reference, even if real-world references (science, history, mythology) informed it. Drawing on real-world knowledge is normal authorial practice; "borrowing" in the derivative-work sense means lifting another author's invented concepts.

### Pages updated

- `inspirations.md`: catalog populated with seven Direct fictional entries, two Real-world reference entries, and fifteen Background entries. The previously-empty `## Catalog` section restructured into three sections — `## Direct fictional concept influences`, `## Real-world references`, `## Background / atmospheric fictional influences` — with a three-tier intro paragraph. **Summary** broadened from "external works" to "external works and frameworks" to accommodate non-fiction inputs. `**Last updated**` → 2026-05-08.

### Framing evolution during the session

The catalog structure went through two corrections during the session:

1. **First correction:** initial two-tier design (Direct concept influences + Background atmospheric) treated Direct and Background as mutually exclusive. User corrected: every Direct work also belongs in Background, because contributing a specific concept implies also shaping atmosphere. → Background expanded from 9 entries to 15 entries (all Direct works added).
2. **Second correction:** K–T impact theory and global flood mythology were initially added as "Direct concept influences." User corrected: real-world references (science, mythology, history) are categorically different from fictional borrowings, and concepts informed by real-world references remain original work in the standard authorial sense. → Three-tier structure adopted with Real-world references as its own section; Cataclysm restored to original-work registry with explicit note about the two informing real-world references.

Both corrections are now reflected in the catalog's intro paragraph and section structure.

### Provenance / scope note

Per `inspirations.md`'s rules, none of these works are cited as sources on canonical claims, and no per-source summary pages are created (unlike canon ingest). Catalog entries serve as lineage references for "where did concept X come from?" — answering questions about the *origin* of an idea separately from its *canonical Eadras form*. The original-vs-borrowed boundary is documented inline in each Direct entry; the original-with-real-world-informing boundary is documented inline in each Real-world reference entry.

## 2026-05-07 — Ingest: more notes on draconic language

**Source ingested**: `more notes on draconic language.txt` (3,092 bytes; written 2026-05-06 18:53, after that day's Mana / Commentary ingest finished at 18:34, so it landed unreviewed until today).

A **strictly additive expansion** to existing Draconic canon — no contradictions, no rewrites. The source formalises three previously hand-wavy aspects of the language:

1. **The suffix stack.** Six categories in fixed order from root outward: *Voice/Direction → Tense/Time → Mood/Attitude → Plurality/Scale → Honor/Social Register → Power/Magical Intensity.* Each category enumerated with several specific suffixes and their meanings.
2. **The three vowel slots given explicit roles.** V₁ = Aspect/Temporal, V₂ = Relational/Social Register, V₃ = Modality/Force/Voice. Existing canon merely said the slots "carry weight"; the source pins down what each slot carries.
3. **Full vowel inventory.** Twelve vowels in IPA (i, ɪ, e, ɛ, æ, a, ʌ, ə, o, ɔ, ʊ, ɯ) with semantic flavour for each. The same root in different vowel patterns reads as substantively different propositions.

### Curator decisions during ingest

- **`-esh` collision resolved by suffix replacement.** The source listed `-esh` under both Voice/Reflexive (Slot 1) and Mood/Desiderative (Slot 3). The Mood/Desiderative slot was reassigned to **`-uz`** to eliminate confusion entirely: vowel `ʊ` ("wild, chaotic, potential, irrealis") is thematically perfect for desire (which is by definition unrealised), and `z` is a canonical Draconic consonant. `-esh` retained for Voice/Reflexive only. This is a one-letter departure from the raw source; the source's stack-position-disambiguation reading is documented in the page so future readers can find it.
- **Honor suffix list reconciliation: union not replacement.** The existing page listed `-ara / -adru / -akhe / -rakh` plus First Flare. The new source listed `-ara / -adru / -rakh / -nakh`. Treated as partial enumerations of the same canonical set: kept `-akhe` (Shatterer/Stormbringer), added `-nakh` (Low/Disrespectful), all others unchanged.
- **Duplicate "Root Template & Vowel System" header in the raw** (lines 66 and 92, identical content) was a copy-paste artefact and merged into a single section.
- **End-to-end decoded examples added** to demonstrate the system. The canonical name **Rhtrakhadara** decodes cleanly under the new V₁=V₂=V₃=`a` reading ("manifest, balanced, undisputed in time" — fits "place where many gather in peace" exactly, the city's whole point). Two demonstration spell-words (a war-cry battle-invocation and a tomb-sealing line) and a controlled-flame-vs-firestorm comparison make the operative-speech mechanic concrete.
- **The Power/Magical Intensity slot** is the canonical mechanism behind the page's pre-existing line that *Draconic is not just descriptive; at sufficient register, it is operative.* Made this connection explicit on the page — the Power suffixes (`-ka` / `-kha` / `-khâr` / `-thûl` / `-zhar`) are the structural reason a spoken Draconic root *does* something rather than merely *describes* something.

### Pages updated

- `draconic-language.md`:
  - **Phonology → Vowels and the root template** rewritten and expanded. New "Three vowel slots" table giving V₁/V₂/V₃ explicit roles; new "Vowel inventory" table with all twelve IPA vowels and their semantic flavour; closing paragraph explaining how vowel choice changes what an utterance is heard to mean and why mortals frequently mean the opposite of what they say.
  - **New top-level section "Suffix system"** between Morphology and Naming Conventions. Stack order list; six sub-sections (one per slot) with full enumerated suffix tables; the `-uz` curator-departure note in the Mood section; the V₂-amplification / V₂-mockery interaction documented under Honor; the operative-speech mechanism documented under Power.
  - **Naming Conventions → Common honor suffixes** table extended with `-nakh` row and a one-line cross-reference to the broader Slot 5 register system.
  - **Naming Conventions → New "Decoded names — how the system reads end to end" sub-section** added after the existing Example names table. Decodes Rhtrakhadara / Kkharara / Lrrhadra under the new vowel + suffix machinery, then exhibits two demonstration utterances (Krzhænis as a young dragon's declared name; KKhRaenosakhatarakhâr as a Council battle-invocation; RhTrKhianisûlrakhthûl as a tomb-sealing line) and a paired-comparison table showing the same KKhR root producing a focused candle-flame versus a berserk firestorm depending only on V₁ and the Power suffix.
  - Sources field expanded with `more notes on draconic language.txt`. Last updated bumped to 2026-05-07.

### Pages not updated

- No other pages currently use specific suffix or vowel canon at a level that needs revision. The existing canonical names (Kkharara, Lrrhadra, Rhtrakhadara, Drrhadru, Rhngadra Zkhar Trkhar) all decode cleanly under the new system, which is the relevant compatibility test. `naming-conventions.md` and pages that wikilink Draconic do not need touching.
- `index.md` already lists `draconic-language` and the entry remains accurate.

### Memory implications

- `feedback-spelling.md` continues to apply unchanged — the transcription rule (multi-letter consonants only capitalize first letter) was already canonical and is reinforced, not modified, by this ingest.
- No new memory file warranted. The suffix system is large but lives entirely in the wiki page now; future cross-conversation recall is via that page, not a separate memory.

### Open canon (specific to this expansion)

- **Whether suffixes ever stack out of canonical order in poetic, archaic, or operatively-charged speech** — i.e., whether the fixed order is a hard syntactic rule or merely the standard register, with deliberate disordering used as emphasis or as a marker of antiquity. Canon silent.
- **Whether dragons can omit V₂ or V₃ and substitute the relevant slot's information into a suffix** (e.g., a Power suffix doing the work of V₃-modality), or whether all three vowel slots are obligatory in every well-formed root.
- **The behaviour of `-orim` ("countless / legion") when applied to scaled-down concepts** — does the same suffix that means "host of dragons" become rhetorically absurd or rhetorically powerful when applied to, say, "many dust motes"? Probably the latter, but undocumented.
- **Whether `-thûl` and `-zhar` ever combine in a single utterance** (precise *and* wild — e.g., a controlled storm), or whether they are mutually exclusive shapings of operative force.
- **Whether mortals who manage two or three suffixes correctly** (the rare extremely-talented Weavespinners, certain [[arathi|Arathi]] mages) have left documented examples in any surviving inscription, and what those inscriptions did when activated.

## 2026-05-07 — UX pass: collapsible Properties / Axes / Related pages

Mobile-friendly affordances added across the wiki. No content changes — purely structural.

- **New CSS snippet** `.obsidian/snippets/hide-properties.css` — defines three behaviors:
  - `cssclasses: [hide-props]` hides the in-document Properties block; an inline `<label><input class="show-props-toggle">…</label>` reveals it on demand.
  - `cssclasses: [axes-unset]` colors the `<details class="axes-block">` summary red until removed (calibration-pending indicator).
  - Generic `<details>` styling for Related pages and similar collapsibles.
  - **Activate**: Settings → Appearance → CSS snippets → toggle *hide-properties* ON.
- **`orden.md`** — pilot for the curator pattern: `axes-unset` flag in cssclasses, axes block wrapped in `<details class="axes-block">`, "Show properties" checkbox above the H1.
- **Sweep**: 181 wiki pages had `## Related pages` sections rewrapped in `<details><summary>Related pages</summary>…</details>` — folded by default, tap to expand. 1 page (orden) already done. 3 pages had no Related pages section.
- **`CLAUDE.md`** — page-format template updated so future pages follow the wrapped pattern.

## 2026-05-06 (evening) — Two-file ingest: Mana.txt + Commentary Ingest (Demon War / Chaos Crusades / Demons / Aberrations)

Two new raw sources ingested, plus several mid-ingest user clarifications that refined the canon as we went.

### File 1 — `Mana.txt` (load-bearing magical-substance canon)

The user notes this paragraph "has been bubbling for a decade" and was not yet in the wiki. The first paragraph is the canon; the rest is AI commentary kept out of canon for now ("discussion only — will examine again and possibly change in future").

**Three-state model** (Quintessence / Eldritch / Mana) added to `magic-in-eadras.md` as a new section *Quintessence, Eldritch, Mana* — replacing the deprecated "Names for Magic Over Time" section. User clarifications shaped the final framing:

- **Quintessence** = the **general/umbrella term** for magical energy as a substance (NOT a "deeper tier" — corrected mid-edit). Used by Velrathi scholars, Rathar archivists, high theology, metaphysical texts.
- **[[eldritch|Eldritch]]** = the **free-flowing state**. Used by practicing mages, Weavespinners, practical arcanists, adventurers.
- **Mana** = the **matrix-bound state** — magical energy held within the matrix of some matter, **organic or inorganic**. Used by miners, crystalmancers, alchemists, magitek engineers, Shada'din.
- All three are **technical terms** with practitioner-register associations (canonical, not flavor — user direction).
- **Every bit of matter has mana**, in varying concentrations. Everything in the Mythos is magical to some extent. *This is the canonical reason Eadras is one of the [[omniverse|seven Mythoi closest to the Bastion of Light]].* (Reaffirms canon already in `omniverse.md`.)

**The All — refined cosmology of the Source.** Two related user corrections:

- **The All** is *the leftover creation energy of [[primordial-duo|Evye and Fryr]]* — the deep reservoir throughout the [[mythos|Mythos]] (a defined reality, not a body) that remains after their total self-sacrifice into the world.
- **The Source (sun)** is the **surface representation** of The All. Sourceshine radiates The All from above; druids tap The All from below, through nature.
- **The Source is not an expression of Lirra or of the Weave.** The Source predates both: Lirra is an Elder God created by the Primordial Duo, and the Weave is a structure she wove during the Demon War atop the magical infrastructure that already existed. Lirra has *governance* over magic and sorcery as her divine portfolio; she is not its origin.
- Standardized canonical phrasing: **"leftover creation energy"** (used five times across `magic-in-eadras.md`, `eldritch.md`, `religion-in-eadras.md`).

**Pages updated for File 1**:
- `magic-in-eadras.md` — new "Quintessence, Eldritch, Mana" section (replaces deprecated "Names for Magic Over Time"); Source section enriched with deep-reservoir framing; Lirra/Weave-expression framing removed; "Why Eadras Has So Much Magic" expanded with seven-closest-Mythoi cross-link; Druids tradition entry rewritten to draw on The All from the deep, not raw Sourceshine
- `eldritch.md` — Overview rewritten to define Eldritch as the *free-flowing state* (one of three); Source-as-Lirra-expression line replaced with "The Source predates both" framing
- `religion-in-eadras.md` — "Source as ur-deity question" entry updated: Source is not Lirra-expression and not Weave-expression; primordial reservoir framing
- `mana-metals.md` — added overview paragraph explicitly tying mana-metals to the canonical principle (mana = magical energy in the matrix of matter; mana-metals are inorganic matter whose mineral matrix retains mana especially well)

### File 2 — `Commentary Ingest — Demon War, Chaos Crusades, Demons, and Aberrations.txt`

Mostly philosophical reaffirmation of canon ingested earlier today, with several additive hooks. User green-light to ingest the additive items:

- **Demon War as ontological warfare** (`demon-war.md`) — added "What kind of war it was" section pairing the Demon War (foundational *societal/existential* trauma) with the [[arathi-cataclysm|Cataclysm]] (foundational *geological/metaphysical* trauma). Demons threatened magical structure / coherent existence / identity stability / the Weave / metaphysical continuity — not merely lives and territory.
- **Demons as ecological end-state of a collapsed Mythos** (`demons.md`) — Origin section's "terminal state" subheading promoted; added explicit Tome philosophical synthesis: demons are *survival stripped of every balancing structure except predation*, not evil incarnate / not Chaos / not moral monsters
- **Energivory as ontological predation** (`demons.md`) — sharpened Energivores subsection
- **Mutability as accelerated ontological adaptation** (`demons.md`) — rewrote Mutable bodies section to emphasize survival-driven adaptation, not ordinary shapeshifting
- **Spell invention as deforming magical assumptions dynamically** (`demons.md`) — rewrote Spell invention section with the "rigid magical systems vs adaptive ontological improvisation" thematic point and the implication for Order Sharanel's relationship to Beast-Folk / Sylphic / Weavespinner adaptive technique

**Beast-Folk creation — narrowed to two deities** (per user direction "Sylph primary deity, Qoxli assist"):
- `beast-folk.md` Origin: added explicit Sylph-primary / Qoxli-assist framing. Qoxli's wild magic protects petitioners' biological coherence under demonic ecological pressure so Sylph's Veil of Forgetting can land cleanly.
- `demon-war.md` Beast-Folk subsection: rewrote to align with the same framing. Removed the older Lirra/druidic/Nara multi-deity multi-force framing per user's narrowed direction.

**Recurring Tragedy — Xar'vion ↔ Kudur-eṭir** (cross-references on each page, per user "cross references"):
- `xarvion.md` and `kudur-etir.md` each gain a "Recurring tragedy" subsection noting the structural parallel: both grief-driven, both refuse lawful limitation, both attempt to override existential structure, both catastrophic-despite-compassionate. Kudur-eṭir rejects entropy (Sixth Law), Xar'vion rejects death (Fifth). Both = compassion without sufficient humility before cosmological law. Canonical Eadran failure mode of the gifted and the merciful.

### Untouched on purpose

- AI commentary in `Mana.txt` beyond the canon paragraph — held back as discussion-only per user direction; will be examined again later
- File 2 reaffirmations of already-canonical material (Form-or-Dissolve Law, residual chaos pockets, aberrations-as-native-life-grown-wrong, Neverborn-doesn't-need-the-hole, Weave-as-defensive-infrastructure beyond what's already on the page) — no duplicate edits needed; the existing canon already aligns

Added "They are not arbitrary divine decrees" closing section: the Six Laws are **expressions of coherent existence itself**.

Explains why Banishment is a permanent solution.

## 2026-05-06 — Same-day corrections (Cindirith as Tarloth's mate; Red Wyrm not red worm; Voroik-woven key; Wyrm honorific)

Same-day corrections to the prior ingest. User clarifications:

- **Cindirith the Magnificent** (eldest of the Nine, First God of Dragons, Platinum) is Tarloth's mate. Sharpened: her grievance is specifically as the unascended consort of the Eldest.
- **The volcano-guardian is a Red dragon** — a **Red Wyrm**, where "Wyrm" is the universal draconic honorific for the oldest/most respected dragons of any clan, NOT a Red-specific term and NOT a separate worm species. Millions of years old, fully sapient, **partially Spear-corrupted (early-stage given only 10,000 years)**.
- **The shell key was woven by the Voroik into a thread of life** (User correction: "given" is wrong — they are weavers; the key is woven). The keybearer IS a person, woven before birth, not an object. Strong working hypothesis: the keybearer is a Weavespinner, since the Voroik also select Weavespinners by drawing fate-strands taut before birth — the same mechanism, possibly the same act.
- **Wyrm is a draconic honorific** for the eldest and most respected dragons across all nine clans, awarded by general recognition rather than ceremony.

**Pages corrected (4)**:

- `_sealed/fourth-hiding-place.md` — Wyrm not worm; Voroik-woven key replaces "specific key held by [open]"; Wyrm corruption section added; Wyrm identity section added; reconciliation note explains the misread; open questions list updated
- `spear-of-crystallized-entropy.md` — Tarloth's section now specifies Cindirith
- `nine-embers-of-renewal.md` — "Tarloth and the Nine" → "Tarloth and Cindirith"; Cindirith's stance noted as open
- `dragons.md` — added **Wyrm honorific** subsection under Social Customs; corrected the Red clan row to reflect heat-immune lava-dwelling generally rather than coining "Red Wyrms" as a separate framing

**Pages deleted (1)**:

- `red-worms.md` — misconceived species page; "red worm/wyrm" is dragon, not a worm species. Removed from `index.md`.

## 2026-05-06 — notes on various topics 1 (Spear sentience + Nine Embers all ascended + sealed plot-spine + Orcs/Dwarves/Gnomes culture)

**Source ingested**: `notes on various topics 1.txt`

**Structural change**: Created the `wiki/_sealed/` folder for **out-of-character / DM-only plot-spine secrets**. Files in `_sealed/` are *not* part of the in-universe Tome and are *not* wikilinked from public pages. See `wiki/_sealed/README.md` for the rules.

**Pages created (sealed, OOC — 2)**:

- `_sealed/README.md` — rules of the sealed folder; off-index; one-way linking only
- `_sealed/fourth-hiding-place.md` — full plot-spine canon for the Spear's current hiding place: Pacific-Ocean-equivalent oceanic location; permanent storm ring + magic-dead zone + outward wind + magical shell with key (blinds non-magicals permanently, magicals temporarily); sealed Rathari guardian conclave; volcano + great red worm; final ward requires Weavespinner + priest + druid + wizard. Sealed Rathari conclave details: post-Demon-War sealing (~10kya), Lirra-worshippers, decadent collapse, mad leader who believes himself an Elder God and "puts to sleep" troublesome members, missing-druid problem. Plot vectors and open author questions retained for campaign work.

**Pages created (public — 2)**:

- `red-worms.md` — bestiary page for the heat-and-fire-immune lava-swimming worm species; species fact, not unique to any specific individual; volcanic apex residents; Shada'din avoid red-worm-occupied volcanoes; sapience open canon
- `nine-embers-of-renewal.md` — the nine original dragon progenitors **all ascended** (User direction 2026-05-06); three publicly named (Cindirith/Davian/Koruss), six remain in draconic esoteric tradition only; Tarloth was the mate of one of the Nine and used the Spear to force ascension after her legitimate path was denied

**Pages updated (8)**:

- `spear-of-crystallized-entropy.md` — added **Form** section (crystalline shaft with dark stain; Spear is sentient with low awareness; **desires to be found**); added **per-use plane corruption** as generalized rule covering Darkmirror→Shadowdark and Brightmirror→Feywild; refined Tarloth's motive to "after her mate ascended" with link to Nine Embers; added a **What the world publicly knows** section listing sailor-tale fragments (none corroborated, none in open Tome chapters; Tome contains a sealed chapter that has not opened in this age). The new doc's "first time you touch it" curse-trigger framing was **deprecated** as a leftover from an earlier source — current canon retains *moment-of-ascension* as the trigger
- `dragons.md` — Origin section updated: Nine Embers all ascended (User direction 2026-05-06); reworked Dragon Gods section to lead with the all-nine-ascended canon; Tarloth-as-mate added
- `gods-of-eadras.md` — Dragon Gods section reworked to lead with all-nine ascension; six unnamed gods explicitly noted; Tarloth's outside-compact status flagged
- `ixthal.md` — Dragon Flare paragraph updated to note that all nine progenitors went on to ascend
- `orcs.md` — major expansion: **clan-holds** section (permanent mountain anchors, not cities; reconciles older "no permanent settlements" framing); **Honor, Mastery, Competition** section with Grandmaster pipeline; **Leadership and Succession** (years of testing, designated assistant, voluntary stepdown, elders+warriors removal procedure); **Great Gathering** every 3 years (trade, diplomacy, matchmaking, skill demos, championship competitions); **Disposition — not a conquering people**; cultural exchange duration updated from "one to two years" → "one to several years"
- `dwarves.md` — Relaxation Mode entry expanded: bright silks/satins/brocades; massive raucous parties; 24-hour shift cadence ensures parties at every hour; tied to Beast-folk textile trade
- `gnomes.md` — added **Sales and distribution** section: gnomes hire other races (halflings, gregarious humans, Beast-folk, city orcs, goblin network) as salespeople because gnomes don't travel for sales; sales teams carry **catalog crystals** (holographic product display) and **teleportation boxes built into carts** (paired magitek shipping with the dwarven factory); long-term salesperson partnerships with workshops
- `index.md` — added `nine-embers-of-renewal` under Ascended Mortals; added `red-worms` to extant races/creatures listing. Sealed folder deliberately not indexed.

**Major canon clarifications**:

1. **All nine original dragon progenitors (the Nine Embers of Renewal) ascended to godhood.** Three are publicly named in the modern pantheon (Cindirith, Davian, Koruss); the other six are present only in draconic esoteric tradition.
2. **Tarloth's motive refined**: she was the mate of one of the Nine Embers and sought to follow her ascended mate into divinity. Denied the legitimate path, she used the Spear and became Unrestricted, placing herself outside the divine compact.
3. **Spear is sentient at a low level of awareness and desires to be found.** It exerts a faint persistent pull on the world toward whatever locale conceals it.
4. **Each use of the Spear slowly corrupts the surrounding area or plane.** Generalizes the existing Darkmirror→Shadowdark and Brightmirror→Feywild canon as a rule, not exceptional events.
5. **The Spear curse fires at the moment of ascension, not first touch.** New doc's first-touch wording deprecated as leftover from earlier source. Existing canon retained.
6. **Orcs maintain permanent mountain clan-holds** as fixed anchors off the plains; not cities. Updates older "no permanent settlements" framing without replacing the no-cities rule.
7. **Orc culture is fundamentally non-conquering**; the cultural reflex sees territorial dominion as a kind of cheating that voids honor.
8. **The Great Gathering** is a triennial near-total assembly of all orc clans.
9. **Gnomes outsource sales entirely** — they invent and craft, hired members of other races sell. The catalog crystal + teleport-box system is the distribution backbone of the gnome-Shada'din factory partnership.
10. **Red worms are a heat-and-fire-immune species** native to active volcanoes throughout Eadras, not unique creatures.
11. **The wiki now distinguishes in-world Tome content (`wiki/`) from author/DM plot-spine secrets (`wiki/_sealed/`).** Hybrid secrecy pattern (User direction 2026-05-06).
12. **Pacific Rathari conclave is one of multiple sealed Rathar enclaves** (User direction 2026-05-06: "isolated guardians — b"). The mad leader's belief that they are the last is part of his delusion; Houses Valtharion, Archivault, and Voidscribe retain their separate sealed populations on Eadras as previously canon.
13. **Pacific Rathari conclave was sealed AFTER Xar'vion's use** (4th use, end of Demon War, ~10,000 ya), not after Tarloth's (User direction 2026-05-06: "Not after second use, after Xarvion's use").

## 2026-05-05 — Eadras Cannon Expansion (Varkhul + Servitors + Deep Vaults inventory + atmosphere + conduit origin)

**Source ingested**: `Eadras Cannon Expansion.txt`

**Pages created (7)**:

- `varkhul.md` — modern post-Eldravath southwestern continent; ~2× a major continent in size; ¼ Scorched Waste; world's prison continent. Inhabitants: dragonkin, Turkorcs, exiled clans. Hosts the Obsidian Sanctum.
- `continental-ward.md` — strongest magical barrier on Eadras; 25mi offshore around Varkhul; multi-layer hard/soft alternating; frequency-shifting; inward-reflective at amplified strength; fed continuously by hundreds of casters from nearly every nation in unbroken shifts. Cumulative cooperative magical effort of nearly all of Eadras.
- `turkorcs.md` — wholly individualistic, amoral warriors and casters of Varkhul; have no concept of honor and consider it stupid; strictly contained behind the Continental Ward.
- `dragonkin.md` — **Mendelian-bred humanoid descendants of dragons** on Varkhul. **Distinct from dragonfolk/dragonborn** — dragonkin are bred from dragons, not magically-created Lizard Peoples. Innate territorial hostility makes Varkhul's interior actively contested.
- `obsidian-sanctum.md` — sealed Arathi Deep Vault deep in Varkhul's Scorched Waste; the **only sealed Deep Vault on dry land**; no formal guardians; protected by the four-layered impossibility (Ward + Scorched Waste + Turkorcs + dragonkin).
- `deep-vaults.md` — full Arathi Deep Vault inventory page. **12 known on Eadras**: 5 opened (1 Darkhoof, 3 gnomes, 1 undersea), 7 sealed (6 underwater, 1 Obsidian Sanctum on land). **+1 vault on the red moon ([[daj|Daj]])**.
- `arathi-servitors.md` — dozens of Arathi engineered servant lineages; only Trolls survived. Named extinct lineage: **Household Servitors** (insectoid stock — mantis-like limbs, beetle carapaces, iridescent wings; domestic / lab / craftsmanship duties). All other lineages organic or semi-organic and died in the Cataclysm.

**Pages updated (10)**:

- `arathyn.md` — added **"Ignic Continent"** as a recurring descriptor (not alternate canonical name; refers to overwhelmingly igneous origin); **closed canon: Arathyn surfaced ~1 mya**, narrowing the prior 2–8 mya LIP-buildup window. Open-canon "surfacing date" entry removed.
- `Arathi.md` — added **glowing chest Focus Crystal** to species traits (biologically integrated, distinct from orbiting toolkit and worn orichalcum); added Arathi cultural patience characterization with Ssar'veth as hidden outlier; replaced old Engineered Races section with pointer to new `arathi-servitors`; **Deep Vaults section updated to new inventory** (5 opened / 7 sealed / +1 Daj — supersedes the old "three opened — Darkhoof, Velrathi archmage, gnome" canon; Velrathi-archmage attribution deprecated).
- `arathi-cataclysm.md` — added **pre-Cataclysm 35% O₂ atmosphere** baseline + fire-ecology context; added **continental drift deceleration curve** (km/y in first year → m/y → cm/y) consistent with the four tectonic snapshots.
- `pre-cataclysm-relics.md` — added new section **"Pre-Cataclysm Atmosphere & Fire Ecology"** with full pre-Cataclysm air canon: 35% O₂; Arathi fire-management infrastructure (crystal fire-suppression fields, humidity control, non-flammable construction, rapid-response Household Servitors, Lirra's stabilizing lattices); Cataclysm O₂ burn-off; modern 21–25% equilibrium; implications for revived pre-Cataclysm flora/fauna and recovered Arathi magitek.
- `trolls.md` — replaced vague hibernating-elder counts with **exact canonical numbers: 2,000 total (Arathi-programmed cap), 300–400 active, ~1,600 hibernating**. Added **"Hibernation Horror"** section: elders grow to hill or small-mountain size, accumulate landscape until unrecognizable, settlements unknowingly build beside them; awakening = mountain splits open, elder reshapes to humanoid form, walks the land for years, returns to dormancy elsewhere.
- `seven-conduits.md` — **major canon elevation**: conduit origin moved from Tome-speculation to closed canon — **Evye and Fryr created the Seven Conduits when they sacrificed themselves into the world**. Added: **fourteen termini are equidistant globally and NOT aligned to the rotational (north–south) axis** — distribution respects only antipodal pairing, not Earth-style cardinal frames. Added: **Lirra has governed and stabilized the conduits since their creation**, both before and after the Weave; conduit-governance predates the Weave by all of pre-Weave history. Tome's older origin question reframed (closed) but the deeper "why seven?" question retained as still-open.
- `katharim.md` — added explicit **"wandering caretakers"** section: small Katharim groups travel constantly to maintain memorial sites all over Eadras; this is the practical mechanism behind the rule that every grave eventually finds a Katharim.
- `order-sharanel.md` — added the **Sworn Eye amulet** as the formal regalia of sworn members; it is the binary external signal of full Order membership (vs. trainees, declined-Oath graduates, or non-Order sorcerers).
- `damedes.md` — clarified that **Damedes is a *pre-supercontinent* continent** (a post-Cataclysm Altean fragment that collided into Eldravath), and that **Varkhul is not Damedes** — Varkhul is a *post-Eldravath modern* continent occupying the southwestern position. The exact pre-Eldravath ancestor of modern Varkhul remains open canon.
- `spear-of-crystallized-entropy.md` — added "**hidden by the gods for the fourth time**" framing (one hiding after each of the four uses: Kudur-eṭir → Darkmirror; Tarloth → Brightmirror; Darkhoof → Tower of Stars; Xar'vion → present hiding place).

**Pages updated (index/log)**:

- `index.md` — added entries for `arathi-servitors`, `dragonkin`, `turkorcs`, `deep-vaults`, `obsidian-sanctum`, `continental-ward`, `varkhul`.
- `log.md` — this entry.

**Major canon clarifications**:

1. **Varkhul is a modern (post-Eldravath) continent** distinct from Damedes; the southwestern position is filled by different landmasses in different eras.
2. **Twelve known Deep Vaults on Eadras + one on the red moon Daj** — supersedes the older "three opened" framing. The Daj vault is the first canonical Arathi structure off-Eadras.
3. **Pre-Cataclysm atmosphere was ~35% O₂** — substantially oxygen-richer than modern; Arathi civilization ran integrated fire-management infrastructure to live in it; Cataclysm burned it down to today's range.
4. **Seven Conduits were created by Evye and Fryr** — closed canon; no longer Tome-speculation. Lirra has governed them since creation, pre- and post-Weave.
5. **Conduit termini are equidistant globally and NOT N–S-axis-aligned**.
6. **Trolls = exactly 2,000 total** (Arathi-programmed cap); 300–400 active, ~1,600 hibernating.
7. **The Hibernation Horror** is now named canon: elder troll awakening from a hidden body that has become indistinguishable from a hill or small mountain.
8. **Arathi Servitors were dozens of lineages**, of which only Trolls survived. Household Servitors (insectoid stock) named as extinct.
9. **Glowing chest Focus Crystal** added to Arathi species traits — biologically integrated, distinct from worn equipment.
10. **Arathyn surfaced ~1 mya** — closed canon; "Ignic Continent" is a descriptor, not an alternate canonical name.
11. **Spear has been hidden by the gods four times** — one after each known use; current hiding (post-Xar'vion) is the fourth.
12. **Order Sharanel sworn members wear the Sworn Eye amulet**.
13. **Damedes is pre-supercontinent**; modern descendant relationship to Varkhul is open canon.
14. **Velrathi-archmage Deep Vault opening is deprecated** from the canonical opened-vault list (was three openings; now five, with that attribution gone).

## 2026-05-04 — More Info 5-4-26 (Order Sharanel + Crusade truth)

**Source ingested**: `More info 5-4-26.txt`

**Page renamed (1)**:

- `order-of-ben-lirroth.md` → `order-sharanel.md`. The order's canonical name is **Order Sharanel** ("blended linguistic structure derived from the three progenitor humanoid races, without belonging to any single tradition; denotes those aligned with order, structure, and the maintenance of the Weave"). The "Order of Ben Lirroth" framing was a working placeholder and is **deprecated** — there is no Ben Lirroth. (User direction 2026-05-04.)

**Pages updated (8)**:

- `order-sharanel.md` (renamed) — added founding act detail (10,000 mortals transmuted simultaneously with Weave creation; mix of wizards/some priests/majority ordinary individuals with no prior magical training); added explicit canon that **NO members of the three progenitor humanoid races** were among the founding 10,000 — drawn entirely from engineered/descendant races and other non-progenitor populations; added "Sorcerers as Living Anchors of the Weave" section.
- `sorcerer-crusade.md` — major refinement of Black Hand intent and divine response. The Crusade was a Black Hand **diversion operation** for the Spear search during the previous Grand Conjunction, NOT a Weave-sabotage operation. **Outer Hand knew nothing of the sorcerer-Weave connection**; **Inner Hand suspected it** but the Spear search was the goal. Added the **avatar intervention** that halted the Crusade — Lirra detected Weave degradation, alerted the gods of the participating churches, who manifested avatars publicly before high priests and martial-order leaders. Added the **divine bureaucracy oversight gap** explanation. Crucial detail: avatars came too late to save the three Weavespinners; the Dimming had already begun.
- `black-hand.md` — Lost Zenith section refined: Crusade was the diversion operation; Weave damage was largely unintended, with explicit Outer-knew-nothing/Inner-suspected distinction.
- `doctrine-of-unheld-hand.md` — added "The Sorcerer Crusade exception" section + bureaucratic oversight gap as a structural feature of the doctrine.
- `lirra.md` — added "The Founding Act" section (Weave + 10,000 sorcerers + Order Sharanel as a single integrated working). Added "The Sorcerer Crusade — Detection and Avatar Call" section.
- `index.md` — updated Order entry, related entries, Bold entry to reference Order Sharanel.
- 24 other pages — bulk-updated via sed to replace `order-of-ben-lirroth` → `order-sharanel` and "Order of Ben Lirroth" / "Ben Lirroth" → "Order Sharanel" / "Sharanel".

**Page deleted (1)**:

- `order-of-ben-lirroth.md` — replaced by `order-sharanel.md`.

**Major canon clarifications**:

1. **The order is Order Sharanel.** "Ben Lirroth" was a placeholder and is deprecated.
2. **The Order Sharanel was founded during the Demon War** in a single integrated act with the Weave's creation and the transmutation of 10,000 mortals into the first sorcerers.
3. **No progenitors among the founding 10,000.** Weave's mortal foundation has never included Elfen, Velrathi, or Taran members.
4. **First sorcerers were mostly ordinary people** with no magical training. A minority were trained wizards or priests; the majority were commoners selected by inner resonance, not prior aptitude.
5. **The Sorcerer Crusade was a Spear-search diversion**, not a Weave-sabotage operation. Outer Hand knew nothing; Inner Hand suspected the sorcerer-Weave link but the Spear search was the goal. Weave damage was largely unintended.
6. **The Crusade was halted by avatar intervention** — but came too late to save the three Weavespinners or prevent the Dimming.
7. **Doctrine of the Unheld Hand has a recognized exception**: large-scale Weave disruption justifies direct divine intervention.
8. **Divine bureaucracy creates oversight gaps.** Gods aren't continuously aware of all actions in their name when those actions are framed within accepted doctrine. This is the structural gap the Black Hand exploited.

## 2026-05-04 — Combined Info Dump 2 (Chaos refinement + Aberrations)

**Source ingested**: `Combined info dump 2 5-4-2026.txt`

**Pages created (1)**:

- `aberrations.md` — new race/entity page. Aberrations as native Eadras life that developed in residual chaos pockets where reality's structure failed locally. Distinguished from demons, fae, undead, mutations, and Chaos-with-a-body. Canonical origin for D&D-style aberration creatures (mind flayers, beholders, aboleths analogues) — they're not foreign invaders, they're native life that grew up where the world's rules were broken.

**Pages updated (4)**:

- `chaos.md` — major rewrite. Chaos is now defined as the **absence of reality**, co-eternal with the Omniversal Creator. Each Mythos is a bounded region of imposed structure within the surrounding unreality. Intrusion = undermining of reality conditions, not replacement. Deprecated 600 Mya / 200 Mya Chaos Crusade dates (corrected to 6/2 mybp). Added link to aberrations and reference to residual chaos pockets.
- `chaos-crusades.md` — added "Residual Chaos Pockets — the lasting aftermath" section explaining the canonical origin of aberrations: each Crusade left scattered standing distortions where structure failed incompletely; First Crusade pockets across the modern continents and reflective planes, Second Crusade pockets continental-scale and younger.
- `creation-myth.md` — softened summary: Creator "imposed bounded structure within the surrounding Chaos" (not "forged from Chaos") to align with co-eternal canon.
- `neverborn.md` — softened "rational void cleaved from Chaos" → "rational structure imposed within the surrounding Chaos" + added clarification that Chaos is unreality, not a substance.
- `index.md` — added aberrations; refined chaos description.

**Major canon clarifications**:

1. **Chaos = absence of reality.** Not disorder, not contradiction, not weird-reality. The structures that constitute existence (time, space, identity, causality) do not exist in Chaos in any stable or meaningful form. The previous "shifting void" framing where one thing rapidly becomes another is replaced — the apparent shifting is an artifact of perceiving unreality with senses calibrated for reality. Nothing is actually shifting because nothing is.
2. **Chaos and the Creator are co-eternal.** Both have always existed; neither created the other. Each Mythos is a bounded region of imposed structure within the surrounding unreality, not a region carved out of Chaos by removal. Earlier framing of "Creator carved rational existence from Chaos" / "rational void cleaved from Chaos" is deprecated. The Omniversal Laws are unbreakable because they are constitutive — to break them would be to remove the imposition of structure, and what's there without the imposition is Chaos.
3. **Aberrations are native, not foreign.** They are matter and life that developed in residual chaos pockets where reality's structure failed locally. They are NOT Chaos with bodies (the form-or-dissolve law forbids that as anything but temporary). They ARE the durable consequence of biology growing up wrong in regions where the rules of biology held only partially. Heritable across generations once stabilized.
4. **The Crusades left residual pockets** that persist for millions of years after the breaches are sealed. First Crusade pockets are widespread across modern continents and reflective planes; Second Crusade pockets are younger, fewer, continental-scale. These pockets are the canonical aberration habitats and the reason aberrations rarely wander far from them.

---

## 2026-05-04 — Cosmological Mechanism Ingest (13 source files)

**Sources ingested**: All thirteen new files dated 2026-05-04 in `raw/`:

- Large page of notes 5-4-2026.txt
- Refinement — Sourceflare definition.txt
- Refinement — Sourceflare mechanism.txt
- Refinement — Weave function.txt
- Refinement — Ixthal Sourceflare influence.txt
- Refinement — Ixthal silence.txt
- Refinement — biological survival.txt
- Addition — Sourceflare manifestation (dragons).txt
- Addition — Sourceflare manifestation (unicorns).txt
- Addition — Ixthal communication method.txt
- Addition — Ixthal motivation.txt
- Addition — catastrophe sequence.txt
- Addition — supercontinent phase context.txt

**Pages created (4)**:

- `seven-conduits.md` — eternal magical (not physical) axes anchoring the Eldritch Cycle; 7 axes × 2 antipodal termini = 14 endpoints; survived the Cataclysm intact because they aren't matter
- `eldritch-cycle.md` — the planetary intake → transformation → distribution → reintegration loop; pre-Weave hydrology of rivulets/streams/rivers; rare unstable Eldritch pools as off-cycle anomalies
- `worldbreaker-mechanism.md` — companion to arathi-cataclysm.md treating the same event as deep geophysics: steam-flash cascade, crustal decoupling, polar stability, climate displacement, conduit-surface drift, knowledge provenance
- `oldest-continuous-settlements.md` — sites with continuous geographic (not cultural) significance across all eras; all anchored on conduit termini; layered habitation stratigraphy

**Pages updated (10)**:

- `ixthal.md` — added Two Million Years of Solitude section (petitions to Elder Gods refused, then independent action), no-regret stance, conceptual-transmission communication method, reframed silence as load-bearingly strategic concealment of the Forbidden Kindling, refined Forbidden Kindling to "amplified natural events, did not create directly"
- `source-surges.md` — added explicit Sourceflare = Source flare in Eldritch spectrum; rewrote "Weave as Buffer" → "Atmospheric and Magnetic Filtering" + "The Weave Does Not Buffer Sourceflares"; added threshold conditions section; corrected misunderstanding that the Weave protects against external Sourceflares
- `magic-in-eadras.md` — refined Weave function to "regulates internal Eldritch only, does not buffer external"; clarified that the seven conduits are eternal magical structures anchored to the planetary core; updated Eldritch flow description to use the rivulets→streams→rivers framing
- `eldritch.md` — clarified that the Seven Conduits are MAGICAL (not physical) and survived the Cataclysm intact; what was destroyed at the Cataclysm was the Arathi cities and crystalline control structures built around them; updated flow description to match the Eldritch Cycle page
- `arathi-cataclysm.md` — restructured Physical Consequences to fold in steam-flash cascade, crustal displacement, polar stability, climatic displacement, and the conduit-not-destroyed clarification; added link to dedicated worldbreaker-mechanism.md page
- `unicorns.md` — **REVERTED unicorn dating from ~4mybp BP back to ~6mybp BP on Eldravath** (2026-05-04 user direction); added herd-as-cohesive-unit manifestation pattern; added supercontinent-stability framing as the reason unicorns are inherently herd-oriented and system-attuned
- `eldravath.md` — reverted: unicorns back on Eldravath as the supercontinent's most consequential biological event; Silver Plains Flare back on Eldravath
- `eadras-timeline.md` — reverted unicorn emergence to ~6mybp BP on Eldravath; added explanatory note about the dating oscillation (orig ~6mybp → 2026-05-01 ~4mybp → 2026-05-04 reverted to ~6mybp); flagged that the source's "4 million years after dragons" detail is overridden by the supercontinent framing
- `eadras-tectonic-history.md` — reverted unicorn dating to 4mya post-Cataclysm = 6mybp BP on Eldravath; updated 4mya snapshot caption to include unicorn emergence and Ratharil founding alongside First Crusade
- `dragons.md` — added "nine distinct eggs as structured manifestation, each a unique archetype" detail to Origin section
- `index.md` — added the four new pages

**Major canon clarifications**:

1. **The Seven Conduits are magical, not physical.** They are eternal axes anchored to the planetary core at the cosmological level. They survived the Cataclysm intact because they are not made of matter. What was destroyed was the Arathi surface infrastructure built around them — cities, crystalline control structures, regulating arrays — not the conduits themselves. Earlier `eldritch.md` framing of "Arathi conduits destroyed and replaced by Weave conduits" is retconned. (User direction 2026-05-04.)
2. **The Weave does NOT buffer external Sourceflares.** It is the internal-Eldritch regulator only. Atmospheric and magnetic-field filtering perform the buffering against incoming external Eldritch radiation. A high-intensity Sourceflare bypasses the Weave whether the Weave is healthy or shattered. Earlier `source-surges.md` framing of the Weave as a Sourceflare buffer is retconned. (User direction 2026-05-04.)
3. **Unicorn emergence reverted to ~6mybp BP on Eldravath.** The 2026-05-01 afternoon move to ~4mybp BP on the post-Eldravath geography is undone. Map remains in flux; specific dating may be refined further. (User direction 2026-05-04.)
4. **Ixthal's silence is strategic concealment**, not divine condition or trauma alone. He is fully capable of speech and chose not to use it because verbal communication risks revealing the Forbidden Kindling. He communicates via direct conceptual transmission, which is structurally poor at conveying the kind of complex causal claim that would expose him.
5. **Ixthal does not regret the Forbidden Kindling.** He acted independently after two million years of refused petitions to the Elder Gods. Goal was the restoration of intelligent mortal life, not power.
6. **Worldbreaker mechanism = steam-flash crustal decoupling.** Subsurface high-pressure water reservoirs flash-vaporized on impact, decoupling the crust from the mantle and allowing the crust to slide as a semi-fluid layer over the deep interior. Rotational axis and magnetic poles remained stable; only the crust moved.

**Spelling normalization**: New source notes used "Ararhi" — silently normalized to "Arathi" per canon.

**Out of scope (ingested but not pageified)**: nothing — all thirteen files have been fully integrated. The "Sourceshine" terminology and "Source surge / Source flare / Sourceflare" interchangeability is now formalized on `source-surges.md`.

## 2026-04-29 — Grok WB Generation Full Ingest (Council Elements XL–LXXIX)

**Source ingested**: `Grok WB Generation 4-29.txt` (1,466 lines, ~77k tokens, 40 Council Elements)

A massive worldbuilding generation file establishing major canon corrections and entirely new lore around: the Three Thirds of the Rathar, the Banishment of all three progenitor races, the Hall of Kings, the Worldender alien crystal hoard, the Great Betrayal, and the Gray Matriarchy of Gaia ruled secretly by an ancient dragon.

### Spelling canon confirmations (per user)
- **Melania** (not Melvina)
- **Velrathi** (not Velrothi)
- **Orug** (not Orog)
- **Grug** (not Grog/Goog)
- **Aetherin** (replaces deprecated Extans/Spartans entirely)
- **Tarran** acceptable for the empire/people; **Taran** also accepted

### Major canon corrections established
- **The Three created only the three progenitors directly** (Elfen, Tarran, Velrathi). All "child races" were engineered by the progenitors themselves.
- **Mark, Rand, Melania were rescued by Dao from the Salem Witch Trials** on a distant world — their mother was burned for witchcraft. They are extramythic in origin.
- **Velrathi engineered the Rathar, Orug, and Grug** (not Rand directly).
- **All three progenitor races were collectively banished** to the three reflections of the moon Gaia after the Demon War.
- **Orug, El'mer, and Aetherin went totally extinct** at the Battle of the Broken Conclaves.
- **The Tarran Emperor was poisoned in bed by his Velrothi princess fiancée** at the Elder Gods' demand.
- **The Firethorn Throne vanished** after the Emperor's death and is in no known location — withdrew because no rightful claimant existed.
- **Hall of Kings was created by Dao** (not Melania), at the same time as the Runeswords; uses leftover alien crystal.
- **Worldender Crystal** is fully controlled by Dao; he possesses every fragment in existence; Runeswords' hearts and the vanished Throne are made from it.
- **The Runesword warrior souls** are extramythic in origin (from a collapsed Mythos).
- **"She Who Shall Not Be Named"** is not a goddess but a multi-million-year-old dragon, born after Ixthal's First Great Flare, who holds her crystal shard by Dao's sufferance.
- **Even the Elder Gods don't know Dao exists**; mortals know of the Omniversal Creator but not his avatars.

### New pages created (21 total)

**Rathar cluster:**
- `rathar.md` — Pre-war Rathar society; engineered by Velrathi; pure surviving enclaves
- `three-thirds-of-the-rathar.md` — The Demon War schism: Fallen, Laughing, Weighted
- `katharim.md` — The Weighted Third; undertakers and divine-only priests
- `kharathen.md` — The 12-mile-circumference City of Unforgotten Names
- `flyting.md` — Beast-folk poetic insult duels
- `orug.md` — Velrathi-engineered guardians; total extinction at Final Wall
- `grug.md` — Velrathi-engineered maintenance/inventors

**Broken Conclaves cluster:**
- `battle-of-the-broken-conclaves.md` — The Final Wall / Threefold Oath; three days; total extinction
- `three-who-stood.md` — Collective name for Orug, El'mer, Aetherin
- `el-mer.md` — Elfen-engineered proto-elves; extinct at Final Wall
- `aetherin.md` — Tarran-engineered superior humans; extinct at Final Wall (replaces Extans/Spartans)

- `gaia.md` — The moon and its three reflections (Prime-like, Feywild, Shadowdark)

**Throne / Hall / Crystal cluster:**
- `worldender-crystal.md` — Alien material; foreign to Mythos; all fragments held by Dao
- `firethorn-throne.md` — Melania's masterpiece; vanished after Emperor's death
- `hall-of-kings.md` — Dao's extradimensional sanctum; multi-tier dais; treasury/trap dual purpose

- `taran.md` — Aetherin replaces Extans/Spartans; added Banishment / Gray Matriarchy section

  - Where the Firethorn Throne actually went

## 2026-04-30 — Tag Taxonomy Established

**Source**: User directive in conversation.

**Changes**:
- Created `wiki/tags.md` — canonical Tag Registry page
- User mandated 27 category tags going forward: `characters`, `races`, `deities`, `places`, `events`, `myths`, `country`, `item`, `organization`, `religion`, `settlement`, `condition`, `document`, `culture`, `language`, `material`, `natural-law`, `plot`, `profession`, `title`, `spell`, `technology`, `tradition`, `conflict`, `vehicle`, `geographic-feature`, `building`
- Lowercase + hyphen convention applied per `CLAUDE.md` (e.g., user-supplied "Geographic Feature" → `geographic-feature`)
- Existing modifier tags (`eadras`, `omniverse`, `extinct`, `progenitor`, `elder-god`, `weave`, `magic`, etc.) are retained as supplemental tags alongside the new Required Taxonomy
- `wiki/index.md` — added "Wiki Meta" section linking to `[[tags]]`

**Open question for the user**: existing pages use older singular forms (`race`, `deity`, `event`, `myth`, `place`). The new Required Taxonomy uses plurals (`races`, `deities`, etc.) and adds many new category tags that don't currently appear on any page. Migration of existing pages has **not** been performed yet — awaiting user confirmation on whether to retroactively re-tag the ~110 existing pages or only apply the new taxonomy on new/edited pages going forward.

### Update — same day, user decision

User chose **forward-only with edit-as-you-go correction**:
- Apply new taxonomy on every new page.
- When editing an existing page for content reasons, also re-tag it via the Merge Map.
- If by **2026-05-30** the wiki has not been substantially re-tagged via that path, perform a full migration sweep.
- New natural category tags may be added to the Required Taxonomy as long as they don't conflict with existing tags. If a conflict arises, ask the user first.

Tag registry `wiki/tags.md` updated with full Tagging Policy, Merge Map (old → new), and the `2026-05-30` deadline.

---

## 2026-04-30 — Major Canon Revision: Altea, Arathalassic Sea, New Continent

**Source ingested**: `Major changes to Arathi Capitol.txt` (1.4 KB, written 2026-04-30).

**The change**: the Arathi capital was **Altea**, not "Arathalassa." Altea sat at the center of the continent-sized **Altean Highlands**. The [[worldender|Worldbreaker]] struck it directly, sundering the Highlands into three continents around a new ocean (the **Arathalassic Sea**). The impact wound became a Large Igneous Province that built a **new continent** at the sea's center over 2-8 million years. Altea left **no remnants whatsoever** — no ruins, no echoes, no spirits — though rare remnants of *other* Arathi cities exist. About **60% of all life** died in the cataclysm.

A separate clarification: the **Sea'tua** were created by the [[elfen|Elfen]] roughly **ten million years after the Cataclysm**. They are not Cataclysm survivors. Their descendants (Merfolk, Sahuagin, Kuo-toa) inhabit the Arathalassic Sea by stewardship, not inheritance.

### Pages created (5)

- `altea.md` — The actual Arathi capital. Three-ring lake city built of Crystal, Flame-veined Marble, Orichalcum, and [[magisterium|Magisterium]]; transit nexus connecting all Arathi cities.
- `altean-highlands.md` — The continent-sized upland that held Altea; sundered into three unnamed continents.
- `arathalassic-sea.md` — The post-Cataclysm ocean between the three sundered continents; houses Abyssal Crownwhales, Vent Seraphs, Scaldwyrms, Crown-Eels, the Bathyric Mandate.
- `new-continent.md` — Placeholder for the LIP-formed continent at the impact center. **Needs canonical name.**
- `magisterium.md` — Placeholder for the new Arathi material. **Properties undefined.**

### Pages renamed / removed

- `arathalassa.md` deleted; capital content moved to `altea.md`. Body-of-water content moved to `arathalassic-sea.md`. Pressure Echoes / Arathi spirits / Sea'tua-as-Cataclysm-survivors content **retconned out** per user direction (option A: full retcon, no Arathi echoes).

### Pages updated

- `arathi-cataclysm.md` — Replaced "Altean capital city" with "Altea"; replaced "Arathalassic Deep" with "Arathalassic Sea" and added the new continent and three-continent split; added planet-wide firestorms, oven-temp re-entry, year-plus rainstorm, months of rebounding earthquakes, ~60% extinction, multi-million-year LIP timeline. Removed Pressure Echo content. Tags merged: `[history, event, eadras, arathi]` → `[events, eadras, arathi, history]`.

## 2026-04-30 — Major Canon Revision: Spear Mechanic, Ssar'veth's Motive, Mana Metals, Arathyn

**Source ingested**: `New information about Arathi Cataclysm.txt` (3.5 KB, written 2026-04-30).

**The change**: Multiple major corrections to existing canon plus a complete new metallurgical system.

### Spear of Crystallized Entropy — mechanic retconned
- The Spear is **not a ritual instrument**. On **God's Day every 5,000 years, at noon in a particular time zone**, the Spear opens a path for unlimited power to flow from the [[eldritch|Source]] to whoever is holding it. This transforms physical form → [[icons|Icon]] and soul → divine soul, producing an **Unrestricted Elder God** (= "not bound by any rules agreed to by other gods"). Earlier wiki framing about ritual / celestial alignment / Wellspring access is deprecated.

### Ssar'veth — motive and curse outcome retconned
- Ssar'veth's true motive: **end entropy entirely** to "perfect Arathi civilization and make sure that it lasted forever, just as it was." (Earlier framing about reversing entropy is essentially the same; the perfectionist angle is new.)
- Dao's curse hit Ssar'veth differently because he was the Spear's *creator* AND had direct mental contact with the [[neverborn|Neverborn]] during forging. Instead of cleanly excising his motive, the curse **shredded his consciousness**, leaving him insane but still able to use his godly power and arcane knowledge intermittently.
- The Falling Star was called by the **insane god**, not as a planned ritual capstone. Earlier framing about cracking the planet to access the "Wellspring of Creation" is deprecated.

### Worldender — alien object lore added
- General principle: alien objects (objects not native to the Mythos) tend to be *other* — harder, stronger, more durable, or weirder than native objects. New page `alien-objects.md` captures this.
- The Worldender is one such alien object.
- **Style preference**: the user prefers archaic **"falling star"** over modern **"asteroid"**. All instances of "asteroid" in wiki prose replaced with "falling star." Saved as feedback memory.

### Verdant Scar — antipodal location
- The Verdant Scar / Arath-Veyr is at the **antipodal point from Altea**, on the opposite end of "the conduit." This implies a planet-spanning Arathi conduit ran from Altea to Arath-Veyr; only one end (Arath-Veyr / Verdant Scar) survives.

### Naming answers
- **The new continent is named Arathyn.** Renamed `new-continent.md` → `arathyn.md` and updated all 8 incoming links across the wiki.
- The three sundered continents — still **not yet** named.

### Mana Metals — full new metallurgical system
A 9-material system (4 base metals + 5 alloys) was canonized:

| Material | Composition | Notable property |
|---|---|---|
| Mithril | mana-transformed silver | lighter, stronger, stores mana |
| Orichalcum | mana-transformed gold | reddish-gold, heavier than gold, stores mana |
| Kylum | mana-infused copper | bright/glowing; conducts electricity AND magic |
| Valthyr | mana-infused iron | stronger durable iron; preferred enchantment metal |
| Valthrene | Valthyr + carbon | mana-steel; masterwork weapons/armor |
| Argentus | Mithril + Kylum | silver-blue; conducts/shapes magical energy |
| Aurelius | Orichalcum + Kylum | golden-red; long-term mana storage |
| Elyrium | Mithril + Orichalcum | platinum-like; complex long-lasting enchantments |
| Magisterium | Mithril + Orichalcum + Valthyr | apex tier; permanent self-sustaining magic |

### Pages created (3)
- `arathyn.md` — Renamed/replaced `new-continent.md`. Canonical name for the LIP-formed continent at the impact center.
- `mana-metals.md` — Single consolidated page covering all 9 materials. Replaces deleted `magisterium.md`.
- `alien-objects.md` — Captures the general principle that non-native objects have peculiar properties.

### Pages renamed / removed
- `new-continent.md` → `arathyn.md` (canonical name).
- `magisterium.md` deleted; content fully covered by the Magisterium section of `mana-metals.md`. Incoming links updated to `[[mana-metals#Magisterium|Magisterium]]`.

### Pages updated
- `spear-of-crystallized-entropy.md` — Major rewrite of the activation mechanic (God's Day, 5000-year cadence, noon in a particular time zone). Added Ssar'veth-exception clause for the curse. Fixed Ssar'veth's death narrative to align with new lore. Tag `artifact` → `item`.
- `ssarveth.md` — Rewrote motive (end entropy → perfect Arathi civilization eternally), curse outcome (insanity, not motive-stripping), Falling Star calling (act of insane god, not ritual). Removed Wellspring of Creation framing. Tag `character` → `characters`.
- `arathi-cataclysm.md` — Removed "Ssar'veth's Ritual" framing; replaced with God's Day mechanic. Removed Wellspring of Creation reference. Removed "ritual architecture" framing of Worldender impact.
- `worldender.md` — Added alien-object framing. Removed Wellspring / ritual capstone framing. Updated scholarly summary couplet.
- `verdant-scar.md` — Added antipodal-to-Altea / opposite-end-of-the-conduit location detail.
- `altea.md`, `Arathi.md` — Replaced `[[magisterium]]` links with `[[mana-metals#Magisterium|Magisterium]]` and added cross-link to `[[mana-metals]]`. Replaced "asteroid" with "falling star."
- `index.md` — Replaced `new-continent` entry with `arathyn`; replaced `magisterium` entry with `mana-metals` and `alien-objects` entries.

### Memories updated
- `feedback-falling-star-not-asteroid.md` — New feedback memory for the style preference.
- `project-canon-corrections.md` — TBD: append new section for these corrections.

### Open canon (still deferred to user)
- **Names of the three sundered continents** that fragmented from the Altean Highlands.
- Kylum + Valthyr alloys — the metals matrix has obvious gaps.
- Whether a four-base apex alloy exists beyond Magisterium.
